<sup>6:23</sup>&nbsp;On the first of the first month, the first of the fourth month, the first of the seventh month, and the first of the tenth month are memorial days and days of the seasons. They are written down and ordained at the four divisions of the year as an eternal testimony. <sup>6:24</sup>&nbsp;Noah ordained them as festivals for himself throughout the history of eternity with the result that through them he had a reminder. <sup>6:25</sup>&nbsp;On the first of the first month he was told to make the ark, and on it the earth became dry, he opened (it), and saw the earth. <sup>6:26</sup>&nbsp;On the first of the fourth month the openings of the depths of the abyss below were closed. On the first of the seventh month all the openings of the earth's depths were opened, and the water began to go down into them. <sup>6:27</sup>&nbsp;On the first of the tenth month the summits of the mountains became visible, and Noah was very happy.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>6:28</sup>&nbsp;በእንተዝ ሠርዖን ኪያሆን ሎቱ ለበዓላት ለተዝካር እስከ ለዓለም። ወከመዝ እማንቱ ሥሩዓት <sup>6:29</sup>&nbsp;ወያዐርግዎን ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ። ዓሥሩ ወሠላስ ሰንበታት አሐተ አሐተ እምኔሆን እምዛቲ ውስተ ዛቲ ተዝካሮን እምቀዳሚት እስከ ካልእት ወእምካልእት እስከ ሣልስት ወእምሣልስት እስከ ራብዕት። <sup>6:30</sup>&nbsp;ወይከውና ኵሎን መዋዕል ዘትእዛዛት ኀምሳ ወክልኤ ሰንበታተ መዋዕል። ወኵሎ ዓመተ ፍጹመ <sup>6:31</sup>&nbsp;ከመዝ ተቈርዐ ወተሠርዐ ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ። ወአልቦ ተዐድዎ አሐተ ዓመተ ዓመ ወዓመተ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>6:28</sup>&nbsp;For this reason he ordained them for himself forever as memorial festivals. So they are ordained, <sup>6:29</sup>&nbsp;and they enter them on the heavenly tablets. Each one of them (consists of) 13 weeks; their memorial (extends) from one to the other: from the first to the second, from the second to third, and from the third to the fourth. <sup>6:30</sup>&nbsp;All the days of the commandments will be 52 weeks of days; (they will make) the entire year complete. <sup>6:31</sup>&nbsp;So it has been engraved and ordained on the heavenly tablets. One is not allowed to transgress a single year, year by year. 
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>6:32</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተኒ አዝዞሙ ለደቂቀ እስራኤል ወይዕቀቡ ዓመታተ በዝ ኆልቍ ሠለስተ ምእተ ወስሳ ወረቡዐ መዋዕለ ወይከውን ፍጹመ ዓመት። ወኢያማስን ጊዜሁ እመዋዕሊሁ ወእምበዓላቲሁ እስመ ኵሉ ይበጽሕ በከመ ስምዖሙ ወኢያዐርፉ ዕለተ ወኢያማስኑ በዓለ። <sup>6:33</sup>&nbsp;ወለእመ ተዐደዉ ወኢገብርዎን በከመ ትእዛዙ ሎቱ አሜሃ ኵሎሙ ያማስኑ ጊዜያቲሆሙ ወዓመታትኒ ይትሐወሱ ዘእምውስተዝ ወጊዜያትሂ ያማስኑ ወዓመታትሂ ይትሐወሱ ወይትዐደዉ ሥርዓቶሙ። <sup>6:34</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሎሙ ውሉደ እስራኤል ይረስዑ ወኢይረክቡ ፍኖተ ዓመታት። ወይረስዑ ሠርቀ ወጊዜ ወሰንበተ ወኵሎ ሥርዓተ ዘዓመታት ይጌግዩ <sup>6:35</sup>&nbsp;አአምር አነ። ወእምይእዜ አነ አየድዐከ ወአኮ እምልብየ እስመ ከመዝ መጽሐፍ ጽሑፍ ቅድሜየ ወተሠርዐ ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ። ኩፋሌሁ ለመዋዕል። ከመ ኢይርሥዑ በዓላተ ኪዳን ወየሐውሩ በበዓላተ አሕዛብ ድኅረ ስሕተቶሙ ወድኅረ ኢያእምሮቶሙ <sup>6:36</sup>&nbsp;ወይከውኑ እለ ያስተሐይጹ ወርኀ በሑያጼ ወርኅ። እስመ ትማስን ይእቲ ጊዜያተ ወትቀድም እምዓመታት ለዓመት ዐሡረ ዕለተ። <sup>6:37</sup>&nbsp;በእንተዝ ይመጽእ ዓመታት ሎሙ እንዘ ያማስኑ ወይገብሩ ዕለተ ስምዕ ምንንተ። ወዕለተ ርኵሰተ በዓለ ወኵሉ ይዴምር ወመዋዕለ ቅዱሳተ ርኩሰ ወዕለተ ርኵሰተ ለዕለት ቅድስት። እስመ ይስሕቱ አውራኀ ወሰንበታተ ወበዓላተ ወኢዮቤለ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>6:32</sup>&nbsp;Now you command the Israelites to keep the years in this number — 364 days. Then the year will be complete and it will not disturb its time from its days or from its festivals because everything will happen in harmony with their testimony. They will neither omit a day nor disturb a festival. <sup>6:33</sup>&nbsp;If they transgress and do not celebrate them in accord with his command, then all of them will disturb their times. The years will be moved from this; they will disturb the times and the years will be moved. They will transgress their prescribed pattern. <sup>6:34</sup>&nbsp;All the Israelites will forget and will not find the way of the years. They will forget the first of the month, the season, and the sabbath; they will err with respect to the entire prescribed pattern of the years. <sup>6:35</sup>&nbsp;For I know and from now on will inform you — not from my own mind because this is the way the book is written in front of me, and the divisions of times are ordained on the heavenly tablets, lest they forget the covenantal festivals and walk in the festivals of the nations, after their error and after their ignorance. <sup>6:36</sup>&nbsp;There will be people who carefully observe the moon with lunar observations because it is corrupt (with respect to) the seasons and is early from year to year by ten days. <sup>6:37</sup>&nbsp;Therefore years will come about for them when they will disturb (the year) and make a day of testimony something worthless and a profane day a festival. Everyone will join together both holy days with the profane and the profane day with the holy day, for they will err regarding the months, the sabbaths, the festivals, and the jubilee.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>6:38</sup>&nbsp;በእንተዝ አነ እኤዝዘከ ወአሰምዕ ለከ ከመ ታስምዕ ሎሙ እስመ እምድኅረ ሞትከ ያማስኑ ውሉድከ ከመ ኢይግበሩ ዓመተ ሠለስተ ምእተ ወስሳ ወረቡዐ ባሕቲቶን። በእንተዝ ይስሕቱ ሠርቀ ወጊዜ ወሰንበተ ወበዓላተ ወይበልዑ ኵሎ ደመ ምስለ ኵሉ ዘሥጋ
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>6:38</sup>&nbsp;For this reason I am commanding you and testifying to you so that you may testify to them because after your death your children will disturb (it) so that they do not make the year (consist of) 364 days only. Therefore, they will err regarding the first of the month, the season, the sabbath, and the festivals. They will eat all the blood with all (kinds of) meat.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>7:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበሱባዔ ሳብዕ በቀዳሚ ዓመቱ ሎቱ በዝ ኢዮቤልዉ ተከለ ኖኅ ወይነ ኀበ ደብር እንተ ዲቤሁ አዕረፈት ታቦት ዘስሙ ሉባር እምአድባረ አራራት ወገብረ ፍሬ በራብዕ ዓመት ወዐቀበ ፍሬሁ ወቀሰሞ በውእቱ ዓመት በወርኅ ሳብዕ <sup>7:2</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረ እምውስቴቱ ወይነ ወወደዩ ውስተ ንዋይ ወዐቀቦ እስከ ዓመት ኃምስቱ እስከ ዕለት ቀዳሚት በሠርቀ ወርኅ ቀዳሚት <sup>7:3</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረ ዕለተ ዛቲ በዓል በፍሥሐ። ወገብረ ጽንሐሐ ለእግዚአብሔር ጣዕዋ እምአልህምት አሐደ ወበሐኰ አሐደ ወአባግዐ ዘዘ ዓመት ሰብዐተ ወመሐስአ ጠሊ አሐደ ከመ ያስተስሪ ቦቱ ለርእሱ ወበእንተ ውሉዱ <sup>7:4</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረ ማሕስአ ቅድመ ወአንበረ እምነ ደሙ ዲበ ሥጋ ዘምሥዋዕ ዘገብረ ወኵሎ ስብሐ አዕረገ ውስተ ምሥዋዕ ዘኀበ ገብረ ጽንሐሐ ወላህመ ወበሐኰ ወአባግዐ። ወአዕረገ ኵሎ ሥጋሆሙ ዲበ ምሥዋዕ <sup>7:5</sup>&nbsp;ወአንበረ ኵሎ መሥዋዕቶሙ ልዉሰ በቅብእ ላዕሌሁ ወእምዝ ነዝኀ ወይነ ውስተ እሳት ዘዲበ ምሥዋዕ አቅደመ ወአንበረ ስሒነ ዲበ ምሥዋዕ ወአዕረገ መዓዛ ሠናየ ዘይሠምር ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር አምላኩ። <sup>7:6</sup>&nbsp;ወተፈሥሐ ወሰትየ እምዝ ወይን ውእቱ ወውሉዱ በፍሥሓ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>7:1</sup>&nbsp;During the seventh week, in its first year, in this jubilee [1317] Noah planted a vine at the mountain (whose name was Lubar, one of the mountains of Ararat) on which the ark had come to rest. It produced fruit in the fourth year [1320]. He guarded its fruit and picked it that year during the seventh month. <sup>7:2</sup>&nbsp;He made wine from it, put it in a container, and kept it until the fifth year [1321] — until the first day at the beginning of the first month. <sup>7:3</sup>&nbsp;He joyfully celebrated the day of this festival. He made a burnt offering for the Lord — one young bull, one ram, seven sheep each a year old, and one kid — to make atonement through it for himself and for his sons. <sup>7:4</sup>&nbsp;First he prepared the kid. He put some of its blood on the meat (that was on) the altar which he had made. He offered all the fat on the altar where he made the burnt offering along with the bull, the ram, and the sheep. He offered all their meat on the altar. <sup>7:5</sup>&nbsp;On it he placed their entire sacrifice mixed with oil. Afterwards he sprinkled wine in the fire that had been on the altar beforehand. He put frankincense on the altar and offered a pleasant fragrance that was pleasing before the Lord his God. <sup>7:6</sup>&nbsp;He was very happy, and he and his sons happily drank some of this wine.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>7:7</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ ምሴተ ወቦአ ውስተ ሰቀላሁ ወሰከበ ስኩሩ ወኖመ ወተከሥተ በውስተ ሰቀላሁ እንዘ ይነውም። <sup>7:8</sup>&nbsp;ወርእዮ ካም ለኖኅ አቡሁ ዕራቆ። ወወፅአ ወነገረ ለክልኤ አኃዊሁ በአፍአ <sup>7:9</sup>&nbsp;ወነሥአ ሴም ልብሰ ወተንሥአ ውእቱ ወያፌት ወአንበሩ ልብሰ ዲበ መታክፍቲሆሙ ወገጾሙ ድኅሪተ ወከደኑ ኃፍረተ አቡሆሙ ወገጾሙ ድኅሪተ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>7:7</sup>&nbsp;When evening came, he went into his tent. He lay down drunk and fell asleep. He was uncovered in his tent as he slept. <sup>7:8</sup>&nbsp;Ham saw his father Noah naked and went out and told his two brothers outside. <sup>7:9</sup>&nbsp;Then Shem took some clothes, rose — he and Japheth — and they put the clothes on their shoulders as they were facing backwards. They covered their father's shame as they were facing backwards.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>7:10</sup>&nbsp;ወነቅሀ ኖኅ እምንዋሙ ወአእመረ ኵሎ ዘገብረ ላዕሌሁ ወልዱ ዘይንእስ ወረገሞ ለወልዱ ወይቤ ርጉም ከናአን ቅኑየ ገብረ ይኩን ለአኃዊሁ። <sup>7:11</sup>&nbsp;ወባረኮ ለሴም ወይቤ ይትባረክ እግዚአብሔር አምላኩ ለሴም። ወይኩን ከናአን ገብሮ <sup>7:12</sup>&nbsp;ያስፍሕ እግዚአብሔር ለያፌት ወይኅድር እግዚአብሔር  ውስተ ማኅደረ ሴም ወይኩን ከናአን ገብሮሙ። <sup>7:13</sup>&nbsp;ወአእመረ ካም ከመ ረገሞ አቡሁ ለወልዱ ዘይንእስ ወሕሡም ሎቱ እስመ ረገሞ ለወልዱ። ወተፈልጠ እምአቡሁ ውእቱ ወውሉዱ ምስሌሁ ኵስ ወምስጥሬም ወፉድ ወከናአን <sup>7:14</sup>&nbsp;ወሐነጸ ሎቱ ውእቱሂ ሀገረ ወጸውዐ ስማ በስመ ብእሲቱ ኔኤላተማኡክ። <sup>7:15</sup>&nbsp;ወርእየ ያፌት ወቀንአ ለእኁሁ። ወሐነጸ ሎቱ ውእቱሂ ሀገረ ወጸውዓ በስመ ብእሲቱ አደታኔሴስ። <sup>7:16</sup>&nbsp;ወሴምሰ ነበረ ምስለ አቡሁ ኖኅ ወሐነጸ ሀገረ በእደ አቡሁ ኀበ ደብር ወጸውዐ ስማ ውእቱሂ በስመ ብእሲቱ ሴዴቃቴልባብ <sup>7:17</sup>&nbsp;ናሁ አህጉር እላንቱ ሠላስ ቅሩበ ሉባር ደብር ሴዴቃቴልባብ ቅድመ ገጸ ደብር በጽባሒሁ ወናኤልታ ማኡክ ገጸ ሰሜኑ አዳተኔሴስ መንገለ ባሕር። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>7:10</sup>&nbsp;When Noah awakened from his sleep, he realized everything that his youngest son had done to him. He cursed his son and said: 'Cursed be Canaan. May he become an abject slave to his brothers'. <sup>7:11</sup>&nbsp;Then he blessed Shem and said: 'May the Lord, the God of Shem, be blessed. May Canaan become his slave. <sup>7:12</sup>&nbsp;May the Lord enlarge Japheth, and may the Lord live in the place where Shem resides. May Canaan become their slave'. <sup>7:13</sup>&nbsp;When Ham realized that his father had cursed his youngest son, it was displeasing to him that he had cursed his son. He separated from his father — he and with him his sons Cush, Mizraim, Put, and Canaan. <sup>7:14</sup>&nbsp;He built himself a city and named it after his wife Neelatamauk. <sup>7:15</sup>&nbsp;When Japheth saw (this), he was jealous of his brother. He, too, built himself a city and named it after his wife Adataneses. <sup>7:16</sup>&nbsp;But Shem remained with his father Noah. He built a city next to his father at the mountain. He, too, named it after his wife Sedeqatelebab. <sup>7:17</sup>&nbsp;Now these three cities were near Mt. Lubar: Sedeqatelebab in front of the mountain on its east side; Naeletamauk toward its south side; and Adataneses toward the west.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>7:18</sup>&nbsp;ወእሉ ውሉደ ሴም ኤላም ወአሱር ወአርፋክስድ። ዝንቱ ትውልድ እምድኅረ ክልኤ ዓም ዘአይኅ አራም ውሉድ <sup>7:19</sup>&nbsp;ውሉደ ያፌት ጎሜር ወማጉግ ወማዳይ ወኢዩአያቶቤል ምስክ ወቲራስ እሉ ውሉደ ኖኅ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>7:18</sup>&nbsp;These were Shem's sons: Elam, Asshur, Arpachshad (he was born two years after the flood), Aram, and Lud. <sup>7:19</sup>&nbsp;Japheth's sons were: Gomer, Magog, Madai, Javan, Tubal, Meshech, and Tiras. These were Noah's sons.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>7:20</sup>&nbsp;ወበዕሥራ ወሰማኒቱ ኢዮቤልዉሳት አኀዘ ኖኅ የአዝዝ ለውሉደ ውሉዱ ሥርዓተ ወትእዛዛተ ኵሎ ዘያአምር ፍትሐ ወአስምዐ ላዕለ ውሉዱ ከመ ይግበሩ ጽድቀ ወከመ ይክድኑ ኃፍረተ ሥጋሆሙ ወከመ ይባርክዎ ለዘ ፈጠሮሙ ወያክብሩ አበ ወእመ ወያፍቅሩ አሐዱ አሐዱ ቢጾ ወይዕቀቡ ነፍሶሙ እምዝሙት ወትኵስ ወእምኵሉ ዐመፃ። <sup>7:21</sup>&nbsp;እስመ በእንተ ዝንቱ ሠለስቱ ኮነ አይኅ ላዕለ ምድር እስመ በእንተ ዝሙት ዘዘመዉ ትጉሃን እምትእዛዘ ኵነኔሆሙ በድኅረ አዋልደ ሰብእ ወነሥኡ ሎሙ አንስተ እምኵሉ እለ ኀረዩ ገብሩ መቅድመ ርኵስ <sup>7:22</sup>&nbsp;ወወለዱ ውሉደ ናፊዲም ወኵሎሙ ኢይትማሰሉ። ወይበልዕ አሐዱ አሐዱ ካልኦ። ወቀተሎ ያርብሕ ለናፊል ወናፊል ቀተሎ ለኤልዮ ወኤልዮ እጓለ እመሕያው ወሰብእሂ ቢጾ <sup>7:23</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሉ ተሠይጠ ይግበር ዐመፃ ወከመ ይክዐው ደመ ንጹሐ ወመልአት ምድር ዐመፃ። <sup>7:24</sup>&nbsp;ወእምድኅረ እሉ ኵሎሙ አራዊት ወአዕዋፍ ወዘይትሐወስ ወዘያንሶሱ ዲበ ምድር። ወተክዕወ ደም ብዙኅ ላዕለ ምድር ወኵሉ ኅሊናሁ ወፈቃዱ ለሰብእ ይኄሊ ከንቶ ወእኩየ በኵሉ መዋዕል። <sup>7:25</sup>&nbsp;ወደምሰሰ እግዚአብሔር ኵሎ እምገጸ ምድር በእንተ ምግባሮሙ ወበእንተ ደም ማእከለ ምድር 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>7:20</sup>&nbsp;During the twenty-eighth jubilee [1324-72] Noah began to prescribe for his grandsons the ordinances and the commandments — every statute which he knew. He testified to his sons that they should do what is right, cover the shame of their bodies, bless the one who had created them, honor father and mother, love one another, and keep themselves from fornication, uncleanness, and from all injustice. <sup>7:21</sup>&nbsp;For it was on account of these three things that the flood was on the earth, since (it was) due to fornication that the Watchers had illicit intercourse — apart from the mandate of their authority — with women. When they married of them whomever they chose they committed the first (acts) of uncleanness. <sup>7:22</sup>&nbsp;They fathered (as their) sons the Nephilim. They were all dissimilar (from one another) and would devour one another: the giant killed the Naphil; the Naphil killed the Elyo; the Elyo mankind; and people their fellows. <sup>7:23</sup>&nbsp;When everyone sold himself to commit injustice and to shed innocent blood, the earth was filled with injustice. <sup>7:24</sup>&nbsp;After them all the animals, birds, and whatever moves about and whatever walks on the earth. Much blood was shed on the earth. All the thoughts and wishes of mankind were (devoted to) thinking up what was useless and wicked all the time. <sup>7:25</sup>&nbsp;Then the Lord obliterated all from the surface of the earth because of their actions and because of the blood which they had shed in the earth.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>7:26</sup>&nbsp;ወተረፍነ አነ ወአንትሙ ደቂቅየ ወኵሉ ዘቦአ ምስሌነ ውስተ ታቦት። ወናሁ አነ እሬኢ ቀዳሚ ምግባሪክሙ ከመዘ ኢኮንክሙ አንትሙ ዘተሐውሩ በጽድቅ እስመ በፍኖተ ሙስና ወጠንክሙ ትሖሩ ወትትፋለጡ አሐዱ አሐዱ እምነ ቢጹ ወትትቃንኡ ዝንቱ ምስለ ዝንቱ ወከመ ኢተሀልዉ ኅቡረ ውሉድየ አሐዱ ምስለ እኁሁ። <sup>7:27</sup>&nbsp;እስመ እሬኢ አነ ወናሁ አጋንንት አስሕቶ ወጠኑ ላዕሌክሙ ወላዕለ ውሉድክሙ። ወይእዜሂ እፈርህ አነ በእንቲአክሙ ከመ እምድኅረ ሞትኩ ትክዕዉ ደመ ሰብእ ውስተ ምድር ወትደመሰሱ አንትሙሂ እምገጸ ምድር <sup>7:28</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ኵሉ ዘይክዑ ደመ ሰብእ ወኵሉ ዘይበልዕ ደመ ዘኵሉ ዘሥጋ ይደመሰሱ ኵሎሙ እምድር። <sup>7:29</sup>&nbsp;ወኢይተርፍ ኵሉ ሰብእ ዘይበልዕ ደመ ወዘይክዑ ደመ ዲበ ምድር። ወኢይተርፍ ሎቱ ዘርአ ወደኃሪተ በታሕተ ሰማይ ሕያው እስመ ውስተ ሲኦል የሐውሩ ወውስተ መካን ዘደይን ይወርዱ ውስተ ጽልመት ማዕምቅ የአትቱ ኵሎሙ በሞት ዐዋግ <sup>7:30</sup>&nbsp;ኵሉ ደም ኢያስተርኢ እምኵሉ ደም ላዕሌክሙ ዘውእቱ በኵሉ መዋዕል ዘጠባሕክሙ ኵሎ አርዌ ወእንስሳ ወዘይሰርር ዲበ ምድር ወግበሩ ምጽዋተ ላዕለ ነፍስክሙ በደፊኖቱ ዘይትከዐው ዲበ ገጸ ምድር <sup>7:31</sup>&nbsp;ወኢትኩኑ ዘይበልዕ ምስለ ደም። ወአጽንዑ ከመ ኢይብልዑ ደመ በቅድሜክሙ ድፍኑ ደመ እስመ ከመዝ ተአዘዝኩ አስምዕ ለክሙ ወለውሉድክሙ ምስለ ኵሉ ዘሥጋ። <sup>7:32</sup>&nbsp;ወኢትብልዕዋ ለነፍስ ምስለ ሥጋ ከመ ኢይኩኑ ዘይትኀሠሡ ደምክሙ ዘነፍስክሙ እምእደ ኵሉ ዘሥጋ ዘይክዕው ዲበ ምድር <sup>7:33</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ምድር ኢትነጽሕ እምነ ደም እምዘ ተክዕወ ላዕሌሃ እስመ በደመ ዘከዐዎ ትነጽሕ ምድር በኵሉ ትዝምዳ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>7:26</sup>&nbsp;We — I and you, my children, and everything that entered the ark with us — were left. But now I am the first to see your actions — that you have not been conducting yourselves properly because you have begun to conduct yourselves in the way of destruction, to separate from one another, to be jealous of one another, and not to be together with one another, my sons. <sup>7:27</sup>&nbsp;For I myself see that the demons have begun to lead you and your children astray; and now I fear regarding you that after I have died you will shed human blood on the earth and (that) you yourselves will be obliterated from the surface of the earth. <sup>7:28</sup>&nbsp;For everyone who sheds human blood and everyone who consumes the blood of any animate being will all be obliterated from the earth. <sup>7:29</sup>&nbsp;No one who consumes blood or who sheds blood on the earth will be left. He will be left with neither descendants nor posterity living beneath heaven because they will go into sheol and will descend into the place of judgment. All of them will depart into deep drakness through a violent death. <sup>7:30</sup>&nbsp;No blood of all the blood which there may be at any time when you sacrifice any animal, cattle, or (creature) that flies above the earth is to be seen on you. Do a good deed for yourselves by covering what is poured out on the surface of the earth. <sup>7:31</sup>&nbsp;Do not be one who eats (meat) with the blood; exert yourselves so that blood is not consumed in your presence. Cover the blood because so was I ordered to testify to you and your children together with all humanity. <sup>7:32</sup>&nbsp;Do not eat the life with the meat so that your blood, your life, may not be required from every person who sheds (blood) on the earth. <sup>7:33</sup>&nbsp;For the earth will not be purified of the blood which has been shed on it; but by the blood of the one who shed it the earth will be purified in all its generations.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>7:34</sup>&nbsp;ወይእዜሂ ውሉድየ ስምዑ ግበሩ ፍትሐ ወጽድቀ ከመ ትተከሉ በጽድቅ ውስተ ገጸ ኵሉ ምድር ወይትሌዐል ክብርክሙ በቅድመ አምላኪየ ዘአድኀነኒ እምነ ማየ አይኅ <sup>7:35</sup>&nbsp;ወናሁ አንትሙ ተሐውሩ ወተሐንጹ ለክሙ አህጉረ ወትተክሉ ውስቴቶን ኵሎ ተክለ ዘዲበ ምድር። ወኵሎኬ ዕፀ ዘይፈሪ <sup>7:36</sup>&nbsp;ሠለስተ ዓመተ ይከውን ፍሬሁ ዘኢይትቀሠም እምኵሉ ለበሊዖቱ ወበዓመት ራብዕ ይትቄደስ ፍሬሁ ወያዐርጉ ቀዳሜ ፍሬ ዘይሠጠው ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር ልዑል ፈጣሬ ሰማይ ወምድር። ወኵሎ ከመ ያዕርጉ በጥሉል ቀዳሜ ወይን ወቅብእ ቀዳሜ ፍሬ ውስተ ምሥዋዐ እግዚአብሔር ዘይትወከፍ ወዘተረፈ ይብልዑ ላእካነ ቤተ እግዚአብሔር በቅድመ ምሥዋዕ ዘይትወከፍ። <sup>7:37</sup>&nbsp;ወበዓመት ኃምስ ግበሩ ኅድገቶ ከመ ትሕድግዎ አንትሙ በጽድቅ ወበርትዕ ወትጸድቁ ወይረትዕ ኵሉ ተክልክሙ <sup>7:38</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ከመዝ አዘዘ ሄኖክ አቡሁ ለአቡክሙ ለማቱሳላ ወልዱ ወማቱሳላ ለላሜክ ወልዱ ወላሜክ አዘዘኒ ኵሎ ዘአዘዝዎ አበዊሁ። <sup>7:39</sup>&nbsp;ወአነሂ እኤዝዘክሙ ውሉድየ በከመ አዘዞ ሄኖክ ለወልዱ በቀዳሚ ኢዮቤልዉሳት እንዘ ሕያው ውእቱ ውስተ ትዝምዱ ሳብዕ አዘዘ ወአስምዐ ለውሉዱ ወለውሉደ ውሉዱ እስከ አመ ዕለተ ሞቱ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>7:34</sup>&nbsp;Now hasten, my children. Do what is just and right so that you may be rightly planted on the surface of the entire earth. Then your honor will be raised before my God who saved me from the flood waters. <sup>7:35</sup>&nbsp;You will now go and build yourselves cities, and in them you will plant every (kind of) plant that is on the earth as well as every (kind of) fruit tree. <sup>7:36</sup>&nbsp;For three years its fruit will remain unpicked by anyone for the purpose of eating it; but in the fourth year its fruit will be sanctified. It will be offered as firstfruits that are acceptable before the most high Lord, the creator of heaven, the earth, and everything, so that they may offer in abundance the first of the wine and oil as firstfruits on the altar of the Lord who accepts (it). What is left over those who serve in the Lord's house are to eat before the altar which receives (it). <sup>7:37</sup>&nbsp;During the fifth year arrange relief for it so that you may leave it in the right and proper way. Then you will be doing the right thing, and all your planting will be successful. <sup>7:38</sup>&nbsp;For this is how Enoch, your father's father, commanded his son Methuselah; then Methuselah his son Lamech; and Lamech commanded me everything that his fathers had commanded him. <sup>7:39</sup>&nbsp;Now I am commanding you, my children, as Enoch commanded his son in the first jubilees. While he was living in its seventh generation, he commanded and testified to his children and grandchildren until the day of his death.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>8:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበዕሥራ ወተስዐቱ ኢዮቤልዉ በሱባዐዔ ቀዳሚ በቀዳሚሁ ነሥአ ሎቱ አርፋክስድ ብእሲተ ወስማ ራሱእያ ወለተ ሱሰን ወለተ ኤላም ሎቱ ብእሲተ ወወለደት ሎቱ ወልደ በዓመት ሣልስ ዘሱባዔ ዝንቱ ወጸውዐ ስሞ ቃይናም። <sup>8:2</sup>&nbsp;ወልህቀ ወልድ ወመሀሮ አቡሁ መጽሐፈ ወሖረ ይኅሥሥ ሎቱ መካነ ኀበ ይእኅዝ ሎቱ ሀገረ። <sup>8:3</sup>&nbsp;ወረከበ መጽሐፈ ዘቈረፁ ቀደምት ውስተ ኰኩሕ ወአንበበ ዘውስቴታ ወአዕለዋ ወረስዐ እምውስቴታ ከመ ሀሎ ውስቴታ ትምህርት ዘትጉሃን በዘ ይሬእዩ ሰገለ ፀሓይ ወወርኅ ወከዋክብት ወውስተ ኵሉ ተአምረ ሰማይ። <sup>8:4</sup>&nbsp;ወጸሐፈ ወኢነገረ በእንቲአሃ እስመ ይፈርሆ ለኖኅ ነጊረ በእንቲአሃ ከመ ኢይትመዓዕ ላዕሌሁ በእንቲአሃ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>8:1</sup>&nbsp;In the twenty-ninth jubilee, in the first week — at its beginning [1373] — Arpachshad married a woman named Rasueya, the daughter of Susan, the daughter of Elam. She gave birth to a son for him in the third year of this week [1375], and he named him Kainan. <sup>8:2</sup>&nbsp;When the boy grew up, his father taught him (the art of) writing. He went to look for a place of his own where he could possess his own city. <sup>8:3</sup>&nbsp;He found an inscription which the ancients had incised in a rock. He read what was in it, copied it, and sinned on the basis of what was in it, since in it was the Watchers' teaching by which they used to observe the omens of the sun, moon, and stars and every heavenly sign. <sup>8:4</sup>&nbsp;He wrote (it) down but told no one about it because he was afraid to tell Noah about it lest he become angry at him about it.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>8:5</sup>&nbsp;ወአመ ሠላሳ ኢዮቤልዉ በሱባዔ ካልእ በቀዳሚ ዓመቱ ነሥአ ሎቱ ብእሲተ ወስማ ሜልካ ወለተ አበዳይ ወልደ ያፌት። ወበዓመት ራብዑ ሎቱ ወለደ ወልደ ወጸውዐ ስሞ ሳላ እስመ ይቤ ተፈንዎ ተፈነውኩ። <sup>8:6</sup>&nbsp;ወበዓመት ራብዕ ተወልደ ወልህቀ ሳላ ወነሥአ ሎቱ ብእሲተ ወስማ ሙአክ ወለተ ኬሴድ እኅወ አቡሁ ሎቱ ብእሲተ። በዓመት ወበሠላሳ ኢዮቤልዉ በሱባዔ ኃምስ በቀዳሚ ዓመቱ <sup>8:7</sup>&nbsp;ወለደት ሎቱ ወልደ በኃምስ ዓመቱ ወጸውዐ ስሞ ኤቤር። ወነሥአ ሎቱ ብእሲተ ወስማ አዙራድ ወለተ ኔብሮድ። በሠላሳ ወክልኤቱ ኢዮቤልዉ በሱባዔ ሳብዕ በሣልስ ዓመቱ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>8:5</sup>&nbsp;In the thirtieth jubilee, in the second week — in its first year [1429] — he married a woman whose name was Melka, the daughter of Madai, Japheth's son. In its fourth year [1432] he became the father of a son whom he named Shelah, for he said: 'I have truly been sent'. <sup>8:6</sup>&nbsp;After he was born in the fourth year, Shelah grew up and married a woman whose name was Muak, the daughter of Kesed, his father's brother, in the thirty-first jubilee, in the fifth week, in its first year [1499]. <sup>8:7</sup>&nbsp;She gave birth to a son for him in its fifth year [1503], and he named him Eber. He married a woman whose name was Azurad, the daughter of Nebrod, during the thirty-second jubilee, in the seventh week, during its third year [1564].
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>8:8</sup>&nbsp;ወበሳድስ ዓመት ወለደት ሎቱ ወልደ ወጸውዐ ስሞ ፋሌክ። እስመ በመዋዕል ዘተወልደ አኀዙ ደቂቀ ኖኅ ይትካፈሉ ሎሙ ምድረ ወበእንተዝ ጸውዐ ስሞ ፋሌክ <sup>8:9</sup>&nbsp;ወተካፈሉ በእኩይ በበይናቲሆሙ ወነገርዎ ለኖኅ <sup>8:10</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ በቀዳሚሁ ለሠላሳ ወሠለስቱ ኢዮቤልዉ ወከፈልዋ ለምድር ሠለስተ መክፈልተ ለሴም ወለካም ወለያፌት በበ ርስቱ። በቀዳሚ ዓመት ዘአሐዱ ሱባዔ እንዘ ይነብር አሐዱ እምኔነ እለ ተፈኖነ ኀቤሆሙ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>8:8</sup>&nbsp;In the sixth year [1567] she gave birth to a son for him, and he named him Peleg because at the time when he was born Noah's children began to divide the earth for themselves. For this reason he named him Peleg. <sup>8:9</sup>&nbsp;They divided it in a bad way among themselves and told Noah. <sup>8:10</sup>&nbsp;At the beginning of the thirty-third jubilee [1569- 1617] they divided the earth into three parts — for Shem, Ham, and Japheth — each in his own inheritance. (This happened) in the first year of the first week [1569] while one of us who were sent was staying with them.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>8:11</sup>&nbsp;ወጸውዐ ደቂቆ ወቀርቡ ኀቤሁ እሙንቱ ወውሉዶሙ ወከፈለ ምድረ በዑፃዌ ዘይእኅዙ ሠለስቲሆሙ ውሉዱ። ወሰፍሑ እደዊሆሙ ወነሥኡ መጽሐፈ እምሕፅነ ኖኅ አቡሆሙ። <sup>8:12</sup>&nbsp;ወወፅአ በመጽሐፍ ዕፃሁ ለሴም ማእከለ ምድር ዘይእኅዝ ለርስቱ ወለውሉዱ ለትውልድ ዘለዓለም። እማእከለ ደብረ ራፋ እሙፃአ ማይ እምፈለገ ጢና ወየሐውር መክፈልቱ መንገለ ዐረብ እንተ ማእከሉ ለዝ ፈለግ። ወየሐውሩ እስከ ሶበ ይቀርቡ ኀበ ማየ ቀላያት እምኀበ ይወፅእ ዝንቱ ፈለግ እምኔሃ። ይወፅእ ዝንቱ ፈለግ ወይክዑ ማያቲሁ ውስተ ባሕረ ሜአት ወየሐውር ዝንቱ ፈለግ እስከ ባሐር ዐቢይ። ወኵሉ ዘመንገለ ደቡብ ለያፌት። ወኵሉ ዘመንገለ ገጸ ሰሜን ለሴም። <sup>8:13</sup>&nbsp;ወየሐውር እስከ ሶበ ይቀርብ ካራስ ዝውእቱ ውስተ ሕፅነ ልሳን እንተ ትኔጽር መንገለ ሰሜን <sup>8:14</sup>&nbsp;ወየሐውር መክፈልቱ እንተ መንገለ ባሕር ዐቢይ ወየሐውር ርቱዐ እስከ ይቀርብ መንገለ ዐረቢሃ ለልሳን እንተ ትኔጽር መንገለ ሰሜን። እስመ ዛቲ ባሕር ስማ ልሳነ ባሕረ ግብጽ <sup>8:15</sup>&nbsp;ወትገምጽ እምህየ መንገለ ሰሜን መንገለ አፉሃ ለባሕር ዐቢይ ውስተ ከናፍረ ማያት። ወተሐውር መንገለ ዐረብ ዐፍራ ወተሐውር እስከ ትቀርብ ኀበ ማየ ግዮን ፈለግ። ወመንገለ ሰሜኑ ለማየ ግዮን መንገለ ድንጋጉ ለዝ ፈለግ። <sup>8:16</sup>&nbsp;ወተሐውር መንገለ ጽባሕ እስከ ሶበ ይቀርብ ኀበ ገነተ ኤዶም መንገለ ሰሜኑ ለሰሜን። ወእምጽባሒሃ ለኵላ ምድረ ኤዶም ወለኵሉ ጽባሕ። ወይትመየጥ ውስተ ጽባሕ ወይመጽእ እስከ ይቀርብ መንገለ ጽባሒሁ ለደብር ዘስሙ ራፋ ወይወርድ መንገለ ጽንፉ ለሙፃአ ጢና ፈለግ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>8:11</sup>&nbsp;When he summoned his children, they came to him — they and their children. He divided the earth into the lots which his three sons would occupy. They reached out their hands and took the book from the bosom of their father Noah. <sup>8:12</sup>&nbsp;In the book there emerged as Shem's lot the center of the earth which he would occupy as an inheritance for him and for his children throughout the history of eternity: from the middle of the mountain range of Rafa, from the source of the water from the Tina River. His share goes toward the west through the middle of this river. One then goes until one reaches the water of the deeps from which this river emerges. This river emerges and pours its waters into the Me'at Sea. This river goes as far as the Great Sea. Everything to the north belongs to Japheth, while everything to the south belongs to Shem. <sup>8:13</sup>&nbsp;It goes until it reaches Karas. This is in the bosom of the branch which faces southward. <sup>8:14</sup>&nbsp;His share goes toward the Great Sea and goes straight until it reaches to the west of the branch that faces southward, for this is the sea whose name is the Branch of the Egyptian Sea. <sup>8:15</sup>&nbsp;It turns from there southward toward the mouth of the Great Sea on the shore of the waters. It goes toward the west of Afra and goes until it reaches the water of the Gihon River and to the south of the Gihon's waters along the banks of this river. <sup>8:16</sup>&nbsp;It goes eastward until it reaches the Garden of Eden, toward the south side of it — on the south and from the east of the entire land of Eden and of all the east. It turns to the east and comes until it reaches to the east of the mountain range named Rafa. Then it goes down toward the bank of the Tina River's mouth.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>8:17</sup>&nbsp;ዛቲ መክፈልት ወፅአት በዕፁ ለሴም ወለውሉዱ ለእኂዞታ ለዓለም ለትውልዱ እስከ ለዓለም። <sup>8:18</sup>&nbsp;ወተፈሥሐ ኖኅ እስመ ወፅአ ዝንቱ መክፈልት ለሴም ወለውሉዱ። ወተዘከረ ኵሎ ዘነበበ በአፉሁ በትንቢት እስመ ይቤ ይትባረክ እግዚአብሔር አምላከ ሴም ወይኅድር እግዚአብሔር ውስተ መኃድሪሁ ለሴም <sup>8:19</sup>&nbsp;ወአእመረ ከመ ገነተ ኤዶም ቅድስተ ቅዱሳን ወማኅደሩ ለእግዚአብሔር ውእቱ ወደብረ ሲና ማእከላ ለገዳም ወደብረ ጽዮን ማእከለ ሕንብርታ ለምድር። ሠለስቲሆሙ ዝንቱ መንጸረ ዝንቱ ለቅድስት ተፈጥሩ። <sup>8:20</sup>&nbsp;ወባረኮ ለአምላከ አማልክት ዘወደየ ውስተ አፉሁ ንባበ እግዚአብሔር ወእግዚአብሔር እስከ ለዓለም። <sup>8:21</sup>&nbsp;ወአእመረ ከመ መክፈልተ በረከት ወቡሩክ በጽሐ ለሴም ወለውሉዱ ለትውልድ ዘለዓለም ኵላ ምድረ ኤዶም ወኵላ ምድረ ባሕረ ኤርትራ ወኵላ ምድረ ጽባሕ ወእንደኬ ወበኤርትራ ወአድባሪሁ ወኵላ ምድረ ባሳ ወኵላ ምድረ ሊባኖስ ወደሰያተ ክብቱር። ወኵሎ ደብረ ሳኒር ወአማና ወደብረ አሱር ዘደቡብ ወኵላ ምድረ ኤላም አሱር ወባቤል ወሱሳን ወማዕዳይ ወኵላ አድባረ አራራት ወኵሎ ማዕዶተ ባሕር ዘማዕዶተ ደብረ አሱር ዘመንገለ ደቡብ ምድር ቡርክት ወስፍሕት ወኵሉ ውስቴታ ጥቀ ሠናይት። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>8:17</sup>&nbsp;This share emerged by lot for Shem and his children to occupy it forever, throughout his generation until eternity. <sup>8:18</sup>&nbsp;Noah was very happy that this share had emerged for Shem and his children. He recalled everything that he had said in prophecy with his mouth, for he had said: 'May the Lord, the God of Shem, be blessed, and may the Lord live in the places where Shem resides'. <sup>8:19</sup>&nbsp;He knew that the Garden of Eden is the holy of holies and is the residence of the Lord; (that) Mt. Sinai is in the middle of the desert; and (that) Mt. Zion is in the middle of the navel of the earth. The three of them — the one facing the other — were created as holy (places). <sup>8:20</sup>&nbsp;He blessed the God of gods, who had placed the word of the Lord in his mouth, and (he blessed) the Lord forever. <sup>8:21</sup>&nbsp;He knew that a blessed and excellent share had come about for Shem and his children throughout the history of eternity: all the land of Eden, all the land of the Erythrean Sea, all the land of the east, India, (that which is) in Erythrea and its mountains, all the land of Bashan, all the land of Lebanon, the islands of Caphtor, the entire mountain range of Sanir and Amana, the mountain range of Asshur which is in the north, all the land of Elam, Asshur, Babylon, Susan, and Madai; all the mountains of Ararat, all the area on the other side of the sea which is on the other side of the mountain range of Asshur toward the north — a blessed and spacious land. Everything in it is very beautiful.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>8:22</sup>&nbsp;ወለካም ወፅአ መክፈልት ዘዳግም መንገለ ማዕዶተ ግዮን መንገለ ሰሜን በየማነ ገነት ወየሐውር መንገለ ሰሜን ወየሐውር ኵሎ አድባረ እሳት። ወየሐውር መንገለ ዐረብ መንገለ ባሕረ አጤል ወየሐውር ዐረብ እስከ ይቀርብ ኀበ ባሕረ ማኡክ እንተ ይእቲ ዘኵሉ ይወርድ ውስቴታ ዘኢይትሐጐል። <sup>8:23</sup>&nbsp;ወይመጽእ ውስተ ደቡብ ውስተ ጽንፈ ጋዲር ወይመጽእ ውስተ ከንፈረ ማየ ባሕር ውስተ ማያተ ባሕር ዐቢይ እስከ ሶበ ይቀርብ ፈለገ ግዮን ወየሐውር ግዮን ፈለግ እስከ ሶበ ይቀርብ በየማነ ገነተ ኤዶም። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>8:22</sup>&nbsp;For Ham there emerged a second share toward the other side of the Gihon — toward the south — on the right side of the garden. It goes southward and goes to all the fiery mountains. It goes westward toward the Atel Sea; it goes westward until it reaches the Mauk Sea, everything that descends into which is destroyed. <sup>8:23</sup>&nbsp;It comes to the north to the boundary of Gadir and comes to the shore of the sea waters, to the waters of the Great Sea, until it reaches the Gihon River. The Gihon River goes until it reaches the right side of the Garden of Eden.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>8:24</sup>&nbsp;ወዛቲ ምድር እንተ ወፅአት ለካም በመክፈልት ዘይእኅዝ ለዓለም ሎቱ ወለውሉዱ ለትዝምዶሙ እስከ ለዓለም 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>8:24</sup>&nbsp;This is the land which emerged for Ham as a share which he should occupy for himself and his children forever throughout their generations until eternity.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>8:25</sup>&nbsp;ወለያፌት ወፅአ መክፈልት ሣልስ ማዕዶተ ጢና ፈለግ መንገለ ደቡባቲሁ ለሙፃአ ማያቲሁ ወየሐውር መንገለ ጽባሕ ደቡብ ኵሎ ደወለ ጎግ ወኵሎ ጽባሓቲሆሙ <sup>8:26</sup>&nbsp;ወየሐውር መንገለ ደቡብ ለደቡብ ወየሐውር መንገለ አድባረ ቄልጥ መንገለ ደቡብ ወመንገለ ባሕረ ማኡቅ ወይመጽእ መንገለ ጽባሑ ለጋዲር እስከ መንገለ እደ ማየ ባሕር <sup>8:27</sup>&nbsp;ወየሐውር እስከ ሶበ ይቀርብ መንገለ ዐረበ ፋራ። ወይገብእ መንገለ አፌራግ ወየሐውር መንገለ ጽባሕ መንገለ ማየ ባሕረ ሜአት <sup>8:28</sup>&nbsp;ወየሐውር መንገለ እደ ጢና ፈለግ መንገለ ጽባሐ ደቡብ እስከ ሶበ ይቀርብ እስከ ጽንፈ ማያቲሁ መንገለ ደብረ ራፋ ወየአውዳ ለደቡብ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>8:25</sup>&nbsp;For Japheth there emerged a third share on the other side of the Tina River toward the north of the mouth of its waters. It goes toward the northeast, (toward) the whole area of Gog and all that is east of them. <sup>8:26</sup>&nbsp;It goes due north and goes toward the mountains of Qelt, to the north and toward the Mauq Sea. It comes to the east of Gadir as far as the edge of the sea waters. <sup>8:27</sup>&nbsp;It goes until it reaches the west of Fara. Then it goes back toward Aferag and goes eastward toward the water of the Me'at Sea. <sup>8:28</sup>&nbsp;It goes to the edge of the Tina River toward the northeast until it reaches the bank of its waters toward the mountain range of Rafa. It goes around the north.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>8:29</sup>&nbsp;ዛቲ ምድር እንተ ወፅአት ለያፌት ወለውሉዱ በመክፈልተ ርስቱ ዘይእኅዝ ሎቱ ወለውሉዱ ለትዝምዶሙ እስከ ለዓለም። ደሰያት ዐበይት ኃምስቱ ወምድር ዐባይ በደቡብ <sup>8:30</sup>&nbsp;ወባሕቱ ቍሩር ይእቲ ወምድረ ካም መርቄ ይእቲ ወምድረ ሴምሰ ኢመርቄ ወኢደደክ እስመ ቱስሕት ይእቲ በቍር ወበሞቅ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>8:29</sup>&nbsp;This is the land that emerged for Japheth and his children as his hereditary share which he would occupy for himself and his children throughout their generations forever: five large islands and a large land in the north. <sup>8:30</sup>&nbsp;However, it is cold while the land of Ham is hot. Now Shem's land is neither hot nor cold but it is a mixture of cold and heat.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>9:1</sup>&nbsp;ወከፈለ ካም ማእከለ ውሉዱ ወወፅአ ቀዳሚ መክፈልት ለኵስ መንገለ ጽባሕ ወዐረቢሁ ለሜጽሬም ወዐረቢሁ ሎቱ ለፉድ። ወዐረቢሁ ሎቱ ለከናአን ወመንገለ ዐረቡ ባሕር። <sup>9:2</sup>&nbsp;ወሴምኒ ከፈለ ውእቱሂ ማእከለ ውሉዱ ወወፅአ መክፈልት ቀዳሚ ለኤላም ወለውሉዱ መንገለ ጽባሑ ለጢግሪስ ፈለግ እስከ ሶበ ይቀርብ መንገለ ጽባሐ ኵላ ምድረ እንደኬ ወበኤርትራ በእዴሁ ወማያተ ዴዳን ወኵሉ አድባር ዘምብሪ ወኤላ ወኵሉ ምድረ ሱሳን ወኵሉ ዘበእደ ፈርናክ እስከ ባሕረ ኤርትራ ወእስከ ጢና ፈለግ <sup>9:3</sup>&nbsp;ወለአሱርኒ ወፅአ መክፈልት ካልእ ኵላ ምድረ አሱር ወነነዌ ወሲናአር ወሰክ እስከ ቅሩበ እንደኬ ወየዐርግ ወደፋ ፈለግ <sup>9:4</sup>&nbsp;ወለአርፋክስድ ወፅአ መክፈልት ሣልስ ኵላ ምድረ ዘደወለ ከላዴዎን መንገለ ጽባሑ ለኤውፍራጢስ ዘቅሩብ ለባሕረ ኤርትራ ወኵሉ ማያተ ገዳም እስከ ቅሩብ ውስተ ልሳነ ባሕር እንተ ትኔጽር መንገለ ግብጽ ኵላ ምድረ ሊባኖስ ወሳኒር ወአማና እስከ ቅሩበ ኤውፍራጢስ። <sup>9:5</sup>&nbsp;ወለአራም ወፅአ መክፈልት ራብዕ ኵላ ምድረ ሜስጴጦምያ ማእከለ ጢግሮስ ወኤፍራጢስ መንገለ ደቡበ ከለዳውያን እስከ ቅሩበ ደብረ አሱር ወምድረ አራራ። <sup>9:6</sup>&nbsp;ወለሉድ ውፅአ መክፈልት ኃምስ ደብረ አሱር ወኵሉ ዘዚአሁ እስከ ይቀርብ ባሕረ ዐቢየ ወይቀርብ መንገለ ጽባሕ አሱር እኁሁ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>9:1</sup>&nbsp;Ham divided (his share) among his sons. There emerged a first share for Cush to the east; to the west of him (one) for Egypt; to the west of him (one) for Put; to the west of him (one) for Canaan; and to the west of him was the sea. <sup>9:2</sup>&nbsp;Shem, too, divided (his share) among his sons. There emerged a first share for Elam and his children to the east of the Tigris River until it reaches the east of the entire land of India, in Erythrea on its border, the waters of the Dedan, all the mountains of Mebri and Ela, all the land of Susan, and everything on the border of Farnak as far as the Erythrean Sea and the Tina River. <sup>9:3</sup>&nbsp;For Asshur there emerged as the second share the whole land of Asshur, Nineveh, Shinar, and Sak as far as the vicinity of India, (where) the Wadafa River rises. <sup>9:4</sup>&nbsp;For Arpachshad there emerged as a third share all the land of the Chaldean region to the east of the Euphrates which is close to the Erythrean Sea; all the waters of the desert as far as the vicinity of the branch of the sea which faces Egypt; the entire land of Lebanon, Sanir, and Amana as far as the vicinity of the Euphrates. <sup>9:5</sup>&nbsp;There emerged for Aram as the fourth share the entire land of Mesopotamia between the Tigris and Euphrates to the north of the Chaldeans as far as the vicinity of the mountain range of Asshur and the land of Arara. <sup>9:6</sup>&nbsp;For Lud there emerged as the fifth share the mountain range of Asshur and all that belongs to it until it reaches the Great Sea and reaches to the east of his brother Asshur.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>9:7</sup>&nbsp;ወያፌት ውእቱሂ ከፈለ ምድረ ለርስት ማእከለ ውሉዱ <sup>9:8</sup>&nbsp;ወወፅአ መክፈልት ቀዳሚ ለጎሜር መንገለ ጽባሕ እምገጸ ደቡብ እስከ ጢና ፈለግ። ወበደቡቡ ለመጎግ ወፅአ ኵሉ ውሣጥያቲሁ ለደቡብ እስከ ይቀርብ መንገለ ባሕረ ሚአት <sup>9:9</sup>&nbsp;ወለማዳይ ወፅአ መክፈልት ከመ የአኃዝ እምዐረብ ለክልኤሆሙ አኃዊሁ እስከ ደሰያት ወእስከ ጽነፊሆን ለደሰያት <sup>9:10</sup>&nbsp;ወለኢዮእዋን ወፅአ መክፈልት ራብዕ ኵሉ ደሴት ወደሰያት ዘመንገለ እደ ሉድ። <sup>9:11</sup>&nbsp;ወለቶቤልሂ ወፅአ መክፈልት ኃምስ ማእከለ ልሳን እንተ ትቀርብ መንገለ እደ መክፈልተ ሉድ እስከ ልሳን ካልእት ወማዕዶታ ለልሳን ካልእት ውስተ ልሳን ሣልስት። <sup>9:12</sup>&nbsp;ወለስምክ ወፅአ መክፈልት ሳድስ ወኵሉ ማዕዶተ ልሳን ዘሣልስት እስከ ይቀርብ ጽባሒሁ ለጋዲር። <sup>9:13</sup>&nbsp;ወለቲራስ ወፅአ መክፈልት ሳብዕ አርባዕቱ ደሰያት ዐበይት በማእከለ ባሕር እለ ይቀርባ ለመክፈልተ ካም። ወደሰያት ዘከማቱሪ ለውሉደ አርፋክስድ ወፅአ በዑፃዌ ርስት ሎቱ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>9:7</sup>&nbsp;Japheth, too, divided the land among his sons as an inheritance. <sup>9:8</sup>&nbsp;There emerged for Gomer a first share eastward from the north side as far as the Tina River. North of him there emerged (as a share) for Magog all the central parts of the north until it reaches the Me'at 15 Sea. <sup>9:9</sup>&nbsp;For Madai there emerged a share for him to occupy on the west of his two brothers as far as the islands and the shores of the islands. <sup>9:10</sup>&nbsp;For Javan there emerged as the fourth share every island and the islands that are in the direction of Lud's border. <sup>9:11</sup>&nbsp;For Tubal there emerged as the fifth share the middle of the branch which 20 reaches the border of Lud's share as far as the second branch, and the other side of the second branch into the third branch. <sup>9:12</sup>&nbsp;For Meshech there emerged a sixth share, namely all the (region on the) other side of the third branch until it reaches to the east of Gadir. <sup>9:13</sup>&nbsp;For Tiras there emerged as the seventh share the four large islands 25 within the sea which reach Ham's share. The islands of Kamaturi emerged by lot for Arpachshad's children as his inheritance.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>9:14</sup>&nbsp;ወከመዝ ከፈሉ ውሉደ ኖኅ ለደቂቆሙ በቅድመ ኖኅ አቡሆሙ። ወአምሐለ በመርገም ረጊሞ ለኵሉ በበ አሐዱ አሐዱ ዘፈቀደ የአኀዝ መክፈልተ ዘኢወፅአ በዑፃዌሁ። <sup>9:15</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሉ ኵሎሙ ለይኩን ወለይኩን ሎሙ ወለውሉዶሙ እስከ ለዓለም በትዝምዶሙ እስከ አመ ዕለተ ደይን በዘ ይኴንኖሙ እግዚአብሔር አምላክ በሰይፍ ወበእሳት በእንተ ኵሉ እከይ ዘርኵስ ዘጌጋዮሙ ዘመልእዋ ለምድር አበሳ ወርኵሰ ወዝሙተ ወኃጢአተ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>9:14</sup>&nbsp;In this way Noah's sons divided (the earth) for their sons in front of their father Noah. He made (them) swear by oath to curse each and every one who wanted to occupy the share which did not emerge by his lot. <sup>9:15</sup>&nbsp;All of them said: 'So be it'! So be it for them and their children until eternity during their generations until the day of judgment on which the Lord God will punish them with the sword and fire because of all the evil impurity of their errors by which they have filled the earth with wickedness, impurity, fornication, and sin.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>10:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበሱባዔ ሣልስ ዘኢዮቤልዉ ዝንቱ አኀዙ አጋንንት ርኩሳን ያስሕትዎሙ ለደቂቀ ውሉደ ኖኅ ወያዕብድዎሙ ወያሕጕልዎሙ። <sup>10:2</sup>&nbsp;ወመጽኡ ውሉደ ኖኅ ኀበ ኖኅ አቡሆሙ ወነገርዎ በእንተ አጋንንት እለ ያስሕቱ ወይጼልሉ ወይቀትሉ ውሉደ ውሉዱ። <sup>10:3</sup>&nbsp;ወጸለየ ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር አምላኩ ወይቤ አምላከ መናፍስት ዘውስተ ኵሉ ዘሥጋ ዘገበርከ ምስሌየ ምሕረተ ወአድኀንከኒ ወውሉድየሂ እምነ ማየ አይኅ ወኢገበርከኒ ከመ እኅለቅ ከመ ገበርከ ለውሉደ ሐጉል እስመ ዐቢይ ሣህልከ ላዕሌየ ወዐብየት ምሕረትከ ላዕለ ነፍስየ። ይትለዐል ሣህልከ ላዕለ ውሉደ ውሉድከ። ወኢይመብሉ መናፍስት እኩያን ላዕሌሆሙ ከመ ኢያማስንዎሙ እምነ ምድር። <sup>10:4</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተ ባርከኒ ኪያየ ወውሉድየ ንልሀቅ ወንብዛኅ ወንምልኣ ለምድር። <sup>10:5</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተ ታአምር ዘከመ ገብሩ ትጉሃኒከ አበዊሆሙ ለእሉ መንፈስ በመዋዕልየ። ወዝኒ መናፍስት እለ ሀለዉ በሕይወት ዕጽዎሙ ወአኀዞሙ ውስተ መካነ ደይን ወኢያማስኑ ውስተ ውሉደ ገብርከ አምላኪየ እስመ ፀዋጋን እሙንቱ ወለአማስኖ ተፈጥሩ <sup>10:6</sup>&nbsp;ወኢይመብሉ በመንፈሰ ሕያዋን እስመ አንተ ባሕቲትከ ታአምር ኵነኔሆሙ ወኢይትባውሑ ላዕለ ውሉደ ጻድቃን እምይእዜ ወእስከ ለዓለም። <sup>10:7</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤለነ አምላክነ ከመ ንእስር ኵሎ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>10:1</sup>&nbsp;During the third week of this jubilee [1583-89] impure demons began to mislead Noah's grandchildren, to make them act foolishly, and to destroy them. <sup>10:2</sup>&nbsp;Then Noah's sons came to their father Noah and told him about the demons who were misleading, blinding, and killing his grandchildren. <sup>10:3</sup>&nbsp;He prayed before the Lord his God and said: 'God of the spirits which are in all animate beings — you who have shown kindness to me, saved me and my sons from the flood waters, and did not make me perish as you did to the people (meant for) destruction — because your mercy for me has been large and your kindness to me has been great: may your mercy be lifted over the children of your children; and may the wicked spirits not rule them in order to destroy them from the earth. <sup>10:4</sup>&nbsp;Now you bless me and my children so that we may increase, become numerous, and fill the earth. <sup>10:5</sup>&nbsp;You know how your Watchers, the fathers of these spirits, have acted during my lifetime. As for these spirits who have remained alive, imprison them and hold them captive in the place of judgment. May they not cause destruction among your servant's sons, my God, for they are savage and were created for the purpose of destroying. <sup>10:6</sup>&nbsp;May they not rule the spirits of the living for you alone know their punishment; and may they not have power over the sons of the righteous from now and forevermore'. <sup>10:7</sup>&nbsp;Then our God told us to tie up each one.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>10:8</sup>&nbsp;ወመጽአ መልአከ መናፍስት መስቴማ ወይቤ እግዚአኦ ፈጣሪ አትርፍ እምኔሆሙ ቅድሜየ ወይስምዑ ቃልየ ወይግበሩ ኵሎ ዘእቤሎሙ እስመ እመ ኢተርፉ ሊተ እምውስቴቶሙ ኢይክል ገቢረ ስልጣነ ፈቃድየ ውስተ ውሉደ ሰብእ። እስመ እሙንቱ ውእቶሙ ለአማስኖ ወለአስሕቶ ቅድመ ኵነኔየ እስመ ዐቢይ እከዮሙ ለውሉደ ሰብእ። <sup>10:9</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ይትረፉ ቅድሜሁ ዐሥራቶሙ ወተስዓተ መክፈልተ ያውርድ ውስተ መካነ ደይን <sup>10:10</sup>&nbsp;ወለአሐዱ እምኔነ ይቤ ከመ ንምሀሮ ለኖኅ ኵሎ ፈውሶሙ እስመ ያአምር ከመ አኮ በርትዕ ዘየሐውሩ ወአኮ በጽድቅ ዘይትባአሱ። <sup>10:11</sup>&nbsp;ወገበርነ በከመ ኵሉ ቃሉ ወኵሎ እኩያነ እለ ይጸውጉ አሰርነ ውስተ መካነ ደይን ወዐሥራቶሙ አትረፍነ ከመ ይኰንኑ ቅድመ ሰይጣን ዲበ ምድር። <sup>10:12</sup>&nbsp;ወፈውሰ ደዌሆሙ ኵሎ ነገርናሁ ለኖኅ ምስለ አስሕቶቶሙ ከመ ይፈውስ በዕፀ ምድር። <sup>10:13</sup>&nbsp;ወጸሐፈ ኖኅ ኵሎ ዘከመ መሀርናሁ በመጽሐፍ በኵሉ ትዝምደ ፈውስ ወተዐፅዉ መናፍስት እኩያን እምድኅሬሆሙ ለውሉደ ኖኅ <sup>10:14</sup>&nbsp;ወወሀበ ኵሎ መጻሕፍተ ዘጸሐፈ ለሴም ወልዱ ዘይልህቅ እስመ ኪያሁ ያፈቅር ፈድፋደ እምኵሉ ውሉዱ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>10:8</sup>&nbsp;When Mastema, the leader of the spirits, came, he said: 'Lord creator, leave some of them before me; let them listen to me and do everything that I tell them, because if none of them is left for me I shall not be able to exercise the authority of my will among mankind. For they are meant for (the purposes of) destroying and misleading before my punishment because the evil of mankind is great'. <sup>10:9</sup>&nbsp;Then he said that a tenth of them should be left before him, while he would make nine parts descend to the place of judgment. <sup>10:10</sup>&nbsp;He told one of us that we should teach Noah all their medicines because he knew that they would neither conduct themselves properly nor fight fairly. <sup>10:11</sup>&nbsp;We acted in accord with his entire command. All of the evil ones who were savage we tied up in the place of judgment, while we left a tenth of them to exercise power on the earth before the satan. <sup>10:12</sup>&nbsp;We told Noah all the medicines for their diseases with their deceptions so that he could cure (them) by means of the earth's plants. <sup>10:13</sup>&nbsp;Noah wrote down in a book everything (just) as we had taught him regarding all the kinds of medicine, and the evil spirits were precluded from pursuing Noah's children. <sup>10:14</sup>&nbsp;He gave all the books that he had written to his oldest son Shem because he loved him much more than all his sons.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>10:15</sup>&nbsp;ወኖመ ኖኅ ምስለ አበዊሁ ወተቀብረ ውስተ ሉባር ደብር በምድረ አራራት <sup>10:16</sup>&nbsp;ተስዓተ ምእተ ወኀምሳ ዓመተ ፈጸመ በሕይወቱ ዐሠርተ ወተስዓተ ኢዮቤልዉ ወክልኤ ሱባዔ። ወኀምስተ ዓመተ <sup>10:17</sup>&nbsp;ዘአፈድፈደ ሐዪወ ዲበ ምድር እምውሉደ ሰብእ በእንተ ጽድቁ ዘባቲ ፍጹም በጽድቁ ዘእንበለ ኤኖክ። እስመ ግብሩ ለሄኖክ ፍጥረት ውእቱ ለስምዕ ለትዝምደ ዓለም ከመ ይንግር ኵሎ ግብረ ለትውልደ ትውልድ በዕለተ ደይን። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>10:15</sup>&nbsp;Noah slept with his fathers and was buried on Mt. Lubar in the land of Ararat. <sup>10:16</sup>&nbsp;He completed 950 years in his lifetime — 19 jubilees, two weeks, and five years — <sup>10:17</sup>&nbsp;(he) who lived longer on the earth than (other) people except Enoch because of his righteousness in which he was perfect ([i.e.] in his righteousness); because Enoch's work was something created as a testimony for the generations of eternity so that he should report all deeds throughout generation after generation on the day of judgment.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>10:18</sup>&nbsp;ወበሠላሳ ወሠለስቱ ኢዮቤልዉ በዓመት አሐዱ በዝ ካልእ ሱባዔ ነሥአ ሎቱ ፋሌክ ብእሲተ እንተ ስማ ሎምና ወለተ ሲናኦር ወወለደት ሎቱ ወልደ በዓመት ራብዕ ዘሱባዔ ዝንቱ ወጸውዐ ስሞ ራግው እስመ ይቤ ናሁ ውሉደ ሰብእ ኮኑ እኩያነ ለምክረ ፁግ ከመ ይሕንጹ ሎሙ ሀገረ ወማኅፈደ ውስተ ምድረ ሰኖኦር <sup>10:19</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ፈለሱ እምድረ አራራት መንገለ ጽባሕ ውስተ ሰናኦር እስመ በመዋዕሊሁ ሐነጽዎ ለሀገር ወለማኅፈድ እንዘ ይብሉ ንዕርግ ቦቱ ውስተ ሰማይ <sup>10:20</sup>&nbsp;ወአኀዙ ይሕንጹ ወበሱባዔ ራብዕ ወፈጡ በእሳት ወኮኖሙ ግንፋል ከመ እብን ወፅቡር በዘ ይመርዩ ቦቱ አስፋሊጦስ ዘይወፅእ እምነ ባሕር ወእምአንቅዕተ ማያት በምድረ ሰናኦር  <sup>10:21</sup>&nbsp;ወሐነጽዎ አርብዓ ዓመተ ወሠለስተ ዓመተ ሀለዉ የሐንጽዎ ግንፋለ ፍጹመ ሠለስተ ወዐሠርተ ውስቴቱ ወሣልስተ አሐቲ ለኑኁ ኀምሳ ምእት ወአርባዕቱ ምእት ወሠላሳ ወሠላስ በእመት ዐርገ ኑኁ። ወክልኤ ስዝር ወዐሠርቱ ምዕራፍ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>10:18</sup>&nbsp;During the thirty-third jubilee, in the first year in this second week [1576], Peleg married a woman whose name was Lomna, the daughter of Sinaor. She gave birth to a son for him in the fourth year of this week [1579], and he named him Ragew, for he said: 'Mankind has now become evil through the perverse plan to build themselves a city and tower in the land of Shinar'. <sup>10:19</sup>&nbsp;For they had emigrated from the land of Ararat toward the east, to Shinar, because in his lifetime they built the city and the tower, saying: 'Let us ascend through it to heaven'. <sup>10:20</sup>&nbsp;They began to build. In the fourth week [1590-96] they used fire for baking and bricks served them as stones. The mud with which they were plastering was asphalt which comes from the sea and from the water springs in the land of Shinar. <sup>10:21</sup>&nbsp;They built it; they spent 43 years building it (with) complete bricks whose width was 13 (units) and whose height was a third of one (unit). Its height rose to 5433 cubits, two spans, and thirteen stades.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>10:22</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤለነ እግዚአብሔር አምላክነ ለነ ናሁ ሕዝብ አሐዱ ወወጠነ ይግበር ወይእዜኒ ኢየሐልቅ እምኔሆሙ። ንዑ ንረድ ወንክዐው ልሳናቲሆሙ ወኢይስማዕ አሐዱ ካልኦ። ወይዘረዉ ውስተ አህጉር ወውስተ አሕዛብ ወኢትንበር እንከ አሐቲ ምክር ላዕሌሆሙ እስከ አመ ዕለተ ደይን <sup>10:23</sup>&nbsp;ወወረደ እግዚአብሔር ወወረድነ ምስሌሁ ንርአይ ሀገረ ወማኅፈደ ዘሐነጹ ውሉደ ሰብእ። <sup>10:24</sup>&nbsp;ወሦጠ ኵሎ ቃለ ልሳናቲሆሙ ወኢሰምዐ እንከ አሐዱ ቃለ ካልኡ ወአንተጉ እንከ ሐኒጸ ሀገር ወማኅፈድ። <sup>10:25</sup>&nbsp;በእንተዝ ተሰምየት ኵላ ምድረ ሰናኦር ባቤል እስመ በህየ ሦጠ አምላክ ኵሎ ልሳናቲሆሙ ለውሉደ ሰብእ። ወእምህየ ተዘርዉ ውስተ አህጉሪሆሙ በበ ልሳናቲሆሙ ወበበ ሕዘቢሆሙ <sup>10:26</sup>&nbsp;ወፈነወ እግዚአብሔር ነፋሰ ውስተ ማኅፈደ ወገፍትኦ ውስተ ምድር። ወናሁ ውእቱ ማእከለ አሱር ወባቢሎን ውስተ ምድረ ሰናኦር ወጸውዐ ሰሞ ድቀት 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>10:22</sup>&nbsp;Then the Lord our God said to us: 'The people here are one, and they have begun to work. Now nothing will elude them. Come, let us go down and confuse their tongues so that they do not understand one another and are dispersed into cities and nations and one plan no longer remains with them until the day of judgment'. <sup>10:23</sup>&nbsp;So the Lord went down and we went down with him to see the city and the tower which mankind had built. <sup>10:24</sup>&nbsp;He confused every sound of their tongues; no one any longer understood what the other was saying. Then they stopped building the city and the tower. <sup>10:25</sup>&nbsp;For this reason the whole land of Shinar was named Babel because there God confused all the tongues of mankind. From there they were dispersed into their cities, each according to their languages and their nations. <sup>10:26</sup>&nbsp;The Lord sent a wind at the tower and tipped it to the ground. It is now between Asshur and Babylon, in the land of Shinar. He named it the Collapse.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>10:27</sup>&nbsp;በሱባዔ ራብዕ በአሐዱ ዓመት በቅድመ ዚአሁ ዘሠላሳ ወአርባዕቱ ኢዮቤልዉ ተዘርዉ እምድረ ሰናኦር። <sup>10:28</sup>&nbsp;ወሖሩ ካም ወውሉዱ ውስተ ምድር እንተ እኅዝት ሎቱ ዘረከበ በመክፈልቱ ውስተ ምድረ ደቡብ <sup>10:29</sup>&nbsp;ወርእየ ከናአን ምድረ ሊባኖስ እስከ ሙሐዘ ግብጽ ከመ ሠናይት ይእቲ ጥቀ። ወኢሖረ ውስተ ምድረ ርስቱ መንገለ ዐረበ ባሕር ወኀደረ ውስተ ምድረ ሊባኖስ እምጽባሕ ወእምዐረብ እምእደ ሊባኖስ ወበእደ ባሕር። <sup>10:30</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ ካም አቡሁ ወኵስ ወመጽሬም አኃዊሁ እስመ ኀደርከ ውስተ ምድር እንተ ኢኮነት እንቲአከ ወኢወፅአ ለነ በዕፀው ኢትግበር ከመዝ። እስመ ለእመ ከመዝ ገበርከ አንተሂ ወደቂቅከሂ ትወድቁ ውስተ ምድር ወርጉማን በሀከክ  እስመ በሀከክ ኀደርክሙ ወበሀከክ ይወድቁ ደቂቅከ ወትሤሮ ለዓለም <sup>10:31</sup>&nbsp;ኢትኅድር ውስተ ማኅደረ ሴም። እስመ ለሴም ወለውሉዱ ወፅአ በዕፆሙ <sup>10:32</sup>&nbsp;ርጉም አንተ ወርጉመ ትከውን እምኵሎሙ ውሉደ ኖኅ በመርገም እንተ ተሠራዕነ በመሐላ በቅድሜሁ ለመኰንን ቅዱስ ወበቅድመ ኖኅ አቡነ። <sup>10:33</sup>&nbsp;ወኢሰምዖሙ ወኀደረ ምድረ ሊባኖስ እምኤማት እስከ ምብዋአ ግብጽ ውእቱ ወውሉዱ እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት <sup>10:34</sup>&nbsp;ወበእንተዝ ተሰምየት ይእቲ ምድር ምድረ ከናአን 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>10:27</sup>&nbsp;In the fourth week, during the first year — at its beginning — of the thirty-fourth jubilee [1639], they were dispersed from the land of Shinar. <sup>10:28</sup>&nbsp;Ham and his sons went into the land which he was to occupy, which he had acquired as his share, in the southern country. <sup>10:29</sup>&nbsp;When Canaan saw that the land of Lebanon as far as the stream of Egypt was very beautiful, he did not go to his hereditary land to the west of the sea. He settled in the land of Lebanon, on the east and west, from the border of Lebanon and on the seacoast. <sup>10:30</sup>&nbsp;His father Ham and his brothers Cush and Mizraim said to him: 'You have settled in a land which was not yours and did not emerge for us by lot. Do not act this way, for if you do act this way both you and your children will fall in the land and be cursed with rebellion, because you have settled in rebellion and in rebellion your children will fall and be uprooted forever. <sup>10:31</sup>&nbsp;Do not settle in Shem's residence because it emerged by their lot for Shem and his sons. <sup>10:32</sup>&nbsp;You are cursed and will be cursed more than all of Noah's children through the curse by which we obligated ourselves with an oath before the holy judge and before our father Noah'. <sup>10:33</sup>&nbsp;But he did not listen to them. He settled in the land of Lebanon — from Hamath to the entrance of Egypt — he and his sons until the present. <sup>10:34</sup>&nbsp;For this reason that land was named the land of Canaan.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>10:35</sup>&nbsp;ወያፌትሰ ወውሉዱ ሖሩ መንገለ ባሕር ወኀደሩ ውስተ ምድረ መክፈልቶሙ ወርእየ ማዳይ ምድረ ባሕር ወኢአደመቶ በቅድሜሁ ወአስተብቍዐ እምኀበ ኤላም ወአሱር ወአርፋክስድ እምኀበ እኀወ ብእሲቱ ወኀደረ ውስተ ምድረ ሜድቂን ቅሩበ ኀበ እኅወ ብእሲቱ እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት <sup>10:36</sup>&nbsp;ወሰመየ ምንባሪሁ ወምንባረ ውሉደ ሜዲቂን በስመ ማዳይ አቡሆሙ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>10:35</sup>&nbsp;Japheth and his sons went toward the sea and settled in the land of their share. Madai saw the land near the sea but it did not please him. So he pleaded (for land) from Elam, Asshur, and Arpachshad, his wife's brother. He has settled in the land of Medeqin near his wife's brother until the present. <sup>10:36</sup>&nbsp;He named the place where he lived and the place where his children lived Medeqin after their father Madai.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>11:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበሠላሳ ወኃምስቱ ኢዮቤልዉ በሱባዔ ሣልስ በአሐዱ ዓመቱ ሎቱ ነሥአ ሎቱ ራግው ብእሲተ ወስማ አራ ወለተ ኡር ወልደ ኬሴድ ወወለደት ሎቱ ወልደ ወጸውዐ ስሞ ሴሩግ በሳብዕ ሱባዔሁ ለዝ ሱባዔ። <sup>11:2</sup>&nbsp;ወበዝ ኢዮቤልዉ ወጠኑ ውሉደ ኖኅ ይትቃተሉ ለፄውዎ ወለቀቲል አሐዱ አሐዱ እኅዋሁ ወለክዒወ ደመ ሰብእ ዲበ ምድር ወለበሊዐ ደም ወለሐኒጸ አህጉር ጽኑዓት ወጥቅም ወማኅፈድ ወለተልዕሎ ብእሲ ላዕለ ሕዝብ ወለሰዪመ መቅድመ መንግሥት። ወለሐዊረ ፀብእ ሕዝብ ቅድመ ሕዝብ ወአሕዛብ ቅድመ አሕዛብ። ወሀገር ቅድመ ሀገር ወኵሉ ለአእክዮ ወለአጥርዮ ንዋየ ሐቅል ወለምህሮ ውሉዶሙ ጸብአ። ወአኀዙ ይፄውዉ ሀገር ለሀገር ወለሠዪጦ ለግብርና ወለአመትና። <sup>11:3</sup>&nbsp;ወሐነጸ ኡድ ወልደ ኬሴድ ሀገረ አራሃ እንተ ከልዴዎን ወሰመየ ስማ በስመ ዚአሁ ወበስመ አቡሁ <sup>11:4</sup>&nbsp;ወገብሩ ሎሙ ስብከዋተ ወይሰግድ አሐዱ ለጣዖት ዘገብረ ለርእሱ ስብኮ። ወወጠኑ ይግበሩ ግልፎ ወምስለ ወርኵሰ ወመናፍስተ ፀዋጋን ይረድኡ ወያስሕቱ ከመ ይግበሩ አበሳተ ወርኵሰ ወአበሳ።  <sup>11:5</sup>&nbsp;ወመኰንን ወስቴማ ይኄይል ለግብረ ዝንቱ ኵሉ ወይፌኑ በእደ መናፍስት ለእለ ተውህቡ ታሕተ እዴሁ ለገቢረ ኵሉ ጌጋይ ወኃጢአት ወኵሉ አበሳ ለአማስኖ ወለአሕጕሎ ወለክዒወ ደም ዲበ ምድር። <sup>11:6</sup>&nbsp;በእንተዝ ተጸውዐ ስሙ ለሴሩክ ሴሩክ እስመ ተመይጠ ኵሉ ለገቢረ ኵሉ ኃጢአት። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>11:1</sup>&nbsp;In the thirty-fifth jubilee, during the third week — in its first year [1681] — Ragew married a woman whose name was Ara, the daughter of Ur, Kesed's son. She gave birth to a son for him, and he named him Serug in the seventh year of this week [1687]. <sup>11:2</sup>&nbsp;During this jubilee Noah's children began to fight one another, to take captives, and to kill one another; to shed human blood on the earth, to consume blood; to build fortified cities, walls, and towers; men to elevate themselves over peoples, to set up the first kingdoms; to go to war — people against people, nations against nations, city against city; and everyone to do evil, to acquire weapons, and to teach warfare to their sons. City began to capture city and to sell male and female slaves. <sup>11:3</sup>&nbsp;Ur, Kesed's son, built the city of Ara of the Chaldeans. He named it after himself and his father. <sup>11:4</sup>&nbsp;They made molten images for themselves. Each one would worship the idol which he had made as his own molten image. They began to make statues, images, and unclean things; the spirits of the savage ones were helping and misleading (them) so that they would commit sins, impurities, and transgression. <sup>11:5</sup>&nbsp;Prince Mastema was exerting his power in effecting all these actions and, by means of the spirits, he was sending to those who were placed under his control (the ability) to commit every (kind of) error and sin and every (kind of) transgression; to corrupt, to destroy, and to shed blood on the earth. <sup>11:6</sup>&nbsp;For this reason Serug was named Serug: because everyone turned to commit every (kind of) sin.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>11:7</sup>&nbsp;ወልህቀ ወኀደረ ውስተ ኡር ዘከላዴዎን ቅሩበ አበ እመ ብእሲቱ ወኮነ ያመልክ ጣዖተ። ወነሥአ ሎቱ ብእሲተ አመ ሠላሳ ወስድስቱ ኢዮቤልዉ በሱባዔ ኃምስ በዓመት ቀዳሚሁ ሎቱ ወስማ ሜልካ ወለተ ካቤር ወለተ እኅወ አቡሁ <sup>11:8</sup>&nbsp;ወወለደት ሎቱ ናኮርሃ በዓመት ቀዳሚሁ ለዝ ሱባዔ ወልህቀ ወኀደረ ውስተ ኡር ውስተ ዘእለ ኡር ከለዳዊያን ወመሀሮ አቡሁ ኁሣሤሆሙ ለከለዳዊያን ለተማርዮ ወለተሰግሎ በተአምረ ሰማይ። <sup>11:9</sup>&nbsp;ወበሠላሳ ወሰብዓቱ ኢዮቤልዉ በሱባዔ ሳድስ በአሐዱ ዓመቱ ሎቱ ነሥአ ብእሲተ ወስማ ኢያስካ ወለተ ኔስታግ ዘከለዳዊያን <sup>11:10</sup>&nbsp;ወወለደት ሎቱ ታራሃ በዓመት ሳብዕ ለዝ ሱባዔ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>11:7</sup>&nbsp;He grew up and settled in Ur of the Chaldeans near the father of his wife's mother. He was a worshiper of idols. During the thirty-sixth jubilee, in the fifth week, in its first year [1744], he married a woman whose name was Melcha, the daughter of Kaber, the daughter of his father's brother. <sup>11:8</sup>&nbsp;She gave birth to Nahor for him during the first year of this week [1744]. He grew up and settled in Ur — in the one that is the Ur of the Chaldeans. His father taught him the studies of Chaldeans: to practice divination and to augur by the signs of the sky. <sup>11:9</sup>&nbsp;During the thirty-seventh jubilee, in the sixth week, in its first year [1800], he married a woman whose name was lyaseka, the daughter of Nestag of the Chaldeans. <sup>11:10</sup>&nbsp;She gave birth to Terah for him in the seventh year of this week [1806].
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>11:11</sup>&nbsp;ወፈነወ መኰንን መስቴማ ቋዓተ ወአዕዋፈ ከመ ይብልዑ ዘርአ ዘይዘራእ ውስተ ምድር ወለአማስኖ ምድር። ከመ ይሂድዎሙ ለውሉደ ሰብእ ትግብርቶሙ ዘእንበለ ይኅርሱ ዘርአ የአርዩ ቋአት እምገጸ ምድር <sup>11:12</sup>&nbsp;በእንተዝ ጽውዐ ስሞ ታራ።  እስመ ያስተጼንስዎሙ ቋዓት ወአዕዋፍ ወይበልዑ ሎሙ ዘርኦሙ። <sup>11:13</sup>&nbsp;ወአኀዙ ዓመታት ይዕበሩ እምቅድመ ገጾሙ ለአዕዋፍ ወኵሎ ፍሬ ዕፅ ይበልዑ እምአእዋም በኃይል ዐቢይ እመ ክህሉ አድኅኖ ኅዳጠ እምኵሉ ፍሬ ምድር በመዋዕሊሆሙ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>11:11</sup>&nbsp;Then Prince Mastema sent ravens and birds to eat the seed which would be planted in the ground and to destroy the land in order to rob mankind of their labors. Before they plowed in the seed, the ravens would pick (it) from the surface of the ground. <sup>11:12</sup>&nbsp;For this reason he named him Terah: because the ravens and birds reduced them to povery and ate their seed. <sup>11:13</sup>&nbsp;The years began to be unfruitful due to the birds. They would eat all the fruit of the trees from the orchards. During their time, if they were able to save a little of all the fruit of the earth, it was with great effort.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>11:14</sup>&nbsp;ወበዝ ሠላሳ ወተስዓቱ ኢዮቤልዉ በሱባዔ ካልእ በቀዳሚ ዓመት። ነሥአ ሎቱ ታራ ብእሲተ ወስማ ኤድና ወለተ አብራም ወለተ እኅተ አቡሁ ሎቱ ብእሲተ <sup>11:15</sup>&nbsp;ወበዓመት ሳብዕ ለዝ ሱባዔ ወለደት ሎቱ ወልደ። ወጸውዐ ስሞ አብራም በስመ አቡሃ ለእሙ እስመ ሞተ ዘእንበለ ይፀነስ ወልደ ወለቱ። <sup>11:16</sup>&nbsp;ወአኀዘ ሕፃን ያእምር ስሕተተ ምድር ከመ ኵሉ ይስሕት በድኅሬሆሙ ለግልፎ ወድኅረ ርኵስ። ወመሀሮ አቡሁ መጽሐፈ ወወልደ ክልኤ ሱባዔ ዓመት ውእቱ ወተፈልጠ እምድኅረ አቡሁ ከመ ኢይስግድ ምስሌሁ ለጣዖት። <sup>11:17</sup>&nbsp;ወአኀዝ ይጸሊ ኀበ ፈጣሬ ኵሉ ከመ ያድኅኖ እምስሕተተ ውሉደ ሰብእ። ወከመ ኢይረድ መክፈልቱ ውስተ ስሒት ድኅረ ርኵስ ወምናኔ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>11:14</sup>&nbsp;During the thirty-ninth jubilee, in the second week, in the first year [1870], Terah married a woman whose name was Edna, the daughter of Abram, the daughter of his father's sister. <sup>11:15</sup>&nbsp;In the seventh year of this week [1876] she gave birth to a son for him, and he named him Abram after his mother's father because he had died before his daughter's son was conceived. <sup>11:16</sup>&nbsp;The child began to realize the errors of the earth — that everyone was going astray after the statues and after impurity. His father taught him (the art of) writing. When he was two weeks of years [= 14 years], he separated from his father in order not to worship idols with him. <sup>11:17</sup>&nbsp;He began to pray to the creator of all that he would save him from the errors of mankind and that it might not fall to his share to go astray after impurity and wickedness.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>11:18</sup>&nbsp;ወበጽሐ ጊዜ ዘርእ ለዘሪእ  ውስተ ምድር። ወወፅኡ ኵሎሙ ኅቡረ ከመ ይዕቀቡ ዘርአ እምገጸ ቋዓት። ወወፅአ አብራም ምሰለ እለ ወፅኡ ሕፃን ወልደ ዐሠርቱ ወአርባዕቱ ዓመት። <sup>11:19</sup>&nbsp;ወደመና ቋዓት መጽኡ ከመ ይብልዑ ዘርአ ወአብራም ይረውጽ አንፃሪሆሙ ዘእንበለ ይንበሩ ውስተ ምድር ወይኬልሕ ላዕሌሆሙ ዘእንበለ ይንበሩ ዲበ ምድር ለበሊዐ ዘርእ ወይብል ኢትረዱ ግብኡ ውስተ መካን ኀበ ወፃእክሙ ወተመይጡ <sup>11:20</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረ በይእቲ ዕለት ለደመና ቋዓት ሰብዓ ወኢነበረ እምኵሉ ቋዓት ውስተ ኵሉ ገራውህ ኀበ ሀሎ አብራም ህየ ወኢአሐዱ። <sup>11:21</sup>&nbsp;ወይሬእይዎ ኵሎሙ እለ ምስሌሁ ውስተ ኵሉ ገራውህ እንዘ ይኬልሕ ወኵሉ ቋዓት ተመይጡ። ወዐብየ ስሙ በኵሉ ምደረ ከለዴዎን። <sup>11:22</sup>&nbsp;ወመጽኡ ኀቤሁ በዓመት ዝንቱ ኵሎሙ እለ ይዘርኡ ወሀሎ የሐውር ምስሌሆሙ እስከ አመ የሐልቅ ጊዜ ዘርእ ወዘርኡ ምድሮሙ። ወአብኡ በውእቱ ዓመት። እክለ እኩለ። ወበልዑ ወጸግቡ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>11:18</sup>&nbsp;When the time for planting seeds in the ground arrived, all of them went out together to guard the seed from the ravens. Abram — a child of 14 years — went out with those who were going out. <sup>11:19</sup>&nbsp;As a cloud of ravens came to eat the seed, Abram would run at them before they could settle on the ground. He would shout at them before they could settle on the ground to eat the seed and would say: 'Do not come down; return to the place from which you came'! And they returned. <sup>11:20</sup>&nbsp;That day he did (this) to the cloud of ravens 70 times. Not a single raven remained in any of the fields where Abram was. <sup>11:21</sup>&nbsp;All who were with him in any of the fields would see him shouting: then all of the ravens returned (to their place). His reputation grew large throughout the entire land of the Chaldeans. <sup>11:22</sup>&nbsp;All who were planting seed came to him in this year, and he kept going with them until the seedtime came to an end. They planted their land and that year brought in enough food. So they ate and were filled.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>11:23</sup>&nbsp;ወበዓመት አሐዱ ዘሱባዔ ኃምስ መሀረ አብራም ለእለ ይገብሩ ንዋየ አልህምት ለኬነተ ዕፅ ወገብሩ ንዋየ በመልዕልተ ምድር በአንጻረ ድጕር ዕርፍ ከመ ያንብር ላዕሌሁ ዘርአ ወይወርድ እምውስቴቱ ዘርእ ውስተ ከተማ ዕርፍ ወይትኀባእ ውስተ ምድር ወኢይፈርሁ እንከ እምገጸ ቋዓት <sup>11:24</sup>&nbsp;ወገብሩ ከመዝ ላዕለ ኵሉ ድጕረ ዕርፍ መልዕልተ ምድር ወዘርኡ ወገብሩ ኵሉ ምድር ዘከመ አዘዞሙ አብራም ወኢይፈርሁ እንከ እምአዕዋፍ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>11:23</sup>&nbsp;In the first year of the fifth week [1891] Abram taught the people who made equipment for bulls — the skillful woodworkers — and they made an implement above the ground, opposite the plow beam, so that one could place seed on it. The seed would then drop down from it onto the end of the plow and be hidden in the ground; and they would no longer be afraid of the ravens. <sup>11:24</sup>&nbsp;They made (something) like this above the ground on every plow beam. They planted seed, and all the land did as Abram told them. So they were no longer afraid of the birds.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>12:1</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ በኡባዔ ሳድስ ዓመቱ ሎቱ ይቤ አብራም ለታራ አቡሁ እንዘ ይብል አባ ወይቤ ነየ አነ ወልድየ። <sup>12:2</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ምንተ ረድኤተ ወተድላ ለነ እምእሉ ጣዖት ዘአንተ ታመልክ ወትሰግድ ቅድሜሆሙ <sup>12:3</sup>&nbsp;እስመ አልቦ ላዕሌሆሙ ምንተኒ መንፈሰ እስመ ስግመት እሙንቱ ወስሕተተ ልብ እሙንቱ ኢታምልክዎሙ። <sup>12:4</sup>&nbsp;አምልኩ አምላከ ሰማይ ዘያወርድ ዝናመ። ወጠለ ላዕለ ምድር ወይገብር ኵሎ ላዕለ ምድር ወኵሎ ፈጠረ በቃሉ። ወኵሉ ሕይወት እምቅድመ ገጹ። <sup>12:5</sup>&nbsp;ለምንት አንትሙ ታመልኩ እለ አልቦሙ መንፈሰ ላዕሌሆሙ እስመ ግብረ እደው እሙንቱ ወዲበ መታክፍቲክሙ አንትሙ ትጸውርዎሙ ወአልቦ እምኔሆሙ ለክሙ ረጽኤተ ዘእንበለ ኀሳር ዐቢይ ለእለ ይገብርዎሙ ወስሕተተ ልብ ለእለ ያመልክዎሙ ኢታምልክዎሙ <sup>12:6</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ አነሂ አአምር ወልድየ ምንተ እሬሲ ለሕዝብ እለ አዘዙኒ እትለአክ ቅድሜሆሙ <sup>12:7</sup>&nbsp;ወእመ ነገርክዎሙ ጽድቀ ይቀትሉኒ እስመ ተለወት  ነፍሶሙ ኀቤሆሙ ከመ ያምልክዎሙ ወይሰብሕዎሙ። አርምም ወልድየ ኢይቅትሉከ <sup>12:8</sup>&nbsp;ወነገረ ዘንተ ነገረ ለክልኤ አኃዊሁ ወተምዕዑ ላዕሌሁ ወአርመመ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>12:1</sup>&nbsp;During the sixth week, in its seventh year [1904], Abram said to his father Terah: 'My father'. He said: 'Yes, my son'? <sup>12:2</sup>&nbsp;He said: 'What help and advantage do we get from these idols before which you worship and prostrate yourself? <sup>12:3</sup>&nbsp;For there is no spirit in them because they are dumb. They are an error of the mind. Do not worship them. <sup>12:4</sup>&nbsp;Worship the God of heaven who makes the rain and dew fall on the earth and makes everything on the earth. He created everything by his word; and all life (comes) from his presence. <sup>12:5</sup>&nbsp;Why do you worship those things which have no spirit in them? For they are made by hands and you carry them on your shoulders. You receive no help from them, but instead they are a great shame for those who make them and an error of the mind for those who worship them. Do not worship them'. <sup>12:6</sup>&nbsp;Then he said to him: 'I, too, know (this), my son. What shall I do with the people who have ordered me to serve in their presence? <sup>12:7</sup>&nbsp;If I tell them what is right, they will kill me because they themselves are attached to them so that they worship and praise them. Be quiet, my son, so that they do not kill you'. <sup>12:8</sup>&nbsp;When he told these things to his two brothers and they became angry at him, he remained silent.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>12:9</sup>&nbsp;ወበአርብዓ ኢዮቤልዉ በሱባዔ ካልእ በሳብዕ ዓመቱ ሎቱ ነሥአ ሎቱ አብራም ብእሲተ ወስማ ሶራ ወለተ አቡሁ ወኮነቶ ሎቱ ብእሲተ። <sup>12:10</sup>&nbsp;ወአራን እኁሁ ነሥአ ሎቱ በዓመት ሣልስ ዘሱባዔ ሣልስ ወወለደት ሎቱ ወልደ በዓመት ሳብዕ ዘሱባዔ ዝንቱ ወጸውዐ ስሞ ሎጥ። <sup>12:11</sup>&nbsp;ወናኮርኒ እኁሁ ነሥአ ሎቱ ብእሲተ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>12:9</sup>&nbsp;During the fortieth jubilee, in the second week, in its seventh year [1925], Abram married a woman whose name was Sarai, the daughter of his father, and she became his wife. <sup>12:10</sup>&nbsp;His brother Haran married a woman in the third year of the third week [1928], and she gave birth to a son for him in the seventh year of this week [1932]. He named him Lot. <sup>12:11</sup>&nbsp;His brother Nahor also got married.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>12:12</sup>&nbsp;ወበዓመት ዘስሳ ዘሕይወተ አብራም ውእቱ ሱባዔ ራብዕ። በዓመት ራብዑ ሎቱ ተንሥአ አብራም በሌሊት ወአውዐየ ቤተ ጣዖታት ወአውዐየ ኵሎ በውስተ ቤት ወሰብእ አልቦ ዘአእመረ። <sup>12:13</sup>&nbsp;ወተንሥኡ ሌሊተ ወፈቀዱ ያድኅኑ አማልክቲሆሙ እማእከለ እሳት <sup>12:14</sup>&nbsp;ወሰረረ አራን ከመ ያድኅኖሙ ወነደደ እሳት ላዕሌሁ ወውዕየ በእሳት ወሞተ በኤኑር ዘከላዴዎን በቅድመ ታራ አቡሁ ወቀበርዎ በኤኑር ዘከላዴዎን። <sup>12:15</sup>&nbsp;ወወፅአ ታራ እምነ ኡር ዘከለዳዊያን ውእቱ ወውሉዱ ከመ ይምጽኡ ውስተ ምድረ ሊባኖስ ወውስተ ምድረ ከናአን ወኀደረ ውስተ ካራን። ወኀደረ አብራም ምስለ አቡሁ ውስተ ካራን ክልኤ ዓመታተ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>12:12</sup>&nbsp;In the sixtieth year of Abram's life (which was the fourth week, in its fourth year [1936], Abram got up at night and burned the temple of the idols. He burned everything in the temple but no one knew (about it). <sup>12:13</sup>&nbsp;They got up at night and wanted to save their gods from the fire. <sup>12:14</sup>&nbsp;Haran dashed in to save them, but the fire raged over him. He was burned in the fire and died in Ur of the Chaldeans before his father Terah. They buried him in Ur of the Chaldeans. <sup>12:15</sup>&nbsp;Then Terah left Ur of the Chaldeans — he and his sons — to go to the land of Lebanon and the land of Canaan. He settled in Haran, and Abram lived with his father in Haran for two weeks of years.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>12:16</sup>&nbsp;ወበሳድስ ሱባዔ በዓመት ኃምሱ ሎቱ ነበረ አብራም በሌሊት በሠርቀ ወርኅ ሳብዕ ከመ ያበይን ከዋክብተ እምሰርክ እስከ ነግህ ከመ ይርአይ ምንተ ግብረ ዓመት በዝናማት ወሀሎ ውእቱ ባሕቲቱ ይነብር ወያቤይን <sup>12:17</sup>&nbsp;ወመጽአ ውስተ ልቡ ቃል ወይቤ ኵሉ ተአምረ ከዋክብት ወተአምሪሃ ለወርኅ ወለፀሐይ ኵሉ በእደ እግዚአብሔር። ለምንት አነ እትኃሠሠ <sup>12:18</sup>&nbsp;ለእመ ፈቀደ ያዘንም ነግህ ወሰርክ ወእመ ፈቀደ ኢያወርድ ወኵሉ ውስተ እዴሁ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>12:16</sup>&nbsp;In the sixth week, during its fifth year [1951], Abram sat at night — at the beginning of the seventh month — to observe the stars from evening to dawn in order to see what would be the character of the year with respect to the rains. He was sitting and observing by himself. <sup>12:17</sup>&nbsp;A voice came to his mind and he said: 'All the signs of the stars and signs of the moon and the sun — all are under the Lord's control. Why should I be investigating (them)? <sup>12:18</sup>&nbsp;If he wishes he will make it rain in the morning and evening; and if he wishes, he will not make it fall. Everything is under his control'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>12:19</sup>&nbsp;ወጸለየ በዛቲ ሌሊት ወይቤ አምላኪየ አምላኪየ አምላክ ልዑል አንተ ባሕቲትከ ሊተ አምላክ ወአንተ ኵሎ ፈጠርከ ወግብረ እደዊከ ኵሉ ኮነ ወሀለወ ወኪያከ ወመለኮትከ ኀረይኩ። <sup>12:20</sup>&nbsp;አድኅነኒ እምእደ መናፍስት እኩያን እለ ይሴለጡ ውስተ ኅሊና ልበ ሰብእ ወኢያስሕቱኑ እምድኅሬከ አምላኪየ ወትረስየኒ ኪያየ ወዘርእየ አንተ ለዓለም። ወኢንስሐት እምይእዜ ወእስከ ለዓለም። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>12:19</sup>&nbsp;That night he prayed and said:
My God, my God, God most High,
You alone are my God.
You have created everything;
Everything that was and has been is the product of your hands. 
You and your lordship I have chosen.
<sup>12:20</sup>&nbsp;Save me from the power of the evil spirits who rule the thoughts of people's minds.
May they not mislead me from following you, my God.
Do establish me and my posterity forever. 
May we not go astray from now until eternity.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>12:21</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ እመ እገብእሁ ውስተ ኡር ዘከለዳዊያን እለ እሙንቱ የኀሥሡ ገጽየ ከመ እግባእ ኀቤሆሙ ወሚመ  እንበር ዝየ በዝ መካን ፍኖተ ርቱዐ ቅድሜከ ኪያሃ ሰርሕ በእደ ገብርከ ይግበር ወኢይሖር በስሕተተ ልብየ አምላኪየ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>12:21</sup>&nbsp;Then he said: 'Shall I return to Ur of the Chaldeans who are looking for me to return to them? Or am I to remain here in this place? Make the path that is straight before you prosper through your servant so that he may do (it). May I not proceed in the error of my mind, my God'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>12:22</sup>&nbsp;ወውእቱ ሶበ ፈጸመ ተናግሮ ወጸዕዮ። ወናሁ ቃለ እግዚአብሔር ተፈነወ ኀቤሁ በእዴየ እንዘ ይብል ነዓ አንተ እምድርከ ወእምነ ትዝምድከ ወእምነ ቤተ አቡከ ውስተ ምድር እንተ አርእየከ። ወእሬስየከ ሕዝበ ዐቢየ ወብዙኀ <sup>12:23</sup>&nbsp;ወእባርከከ ወአዐቢ ስመከ ወትከውን ቡሩከ ውስተ ምድር። ወይትባረኩ ብከ ኵሎሙ አሕዛበ ምድር ወለእለ ይባርኩከ እባርኮሙ። ወለእለ ይረግሙከ እረግሞሙ <sup>12:24</sup>&nbsp;ወእከውነከ ለከ ወለወልድከ ወለወልደ ወልድከ ወለኵሉ ዘርእከ አምላከ ኢትፍራህ እምይእዜ ወእስከ ኵሉ ትዝምደ ምድር አነ አምላክከ። <sup>12:25</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤለኒ እግዚአብሔር አምላክ ፍታሕ አፉሁ ወእዘኒሁ ይስማዕ ወይንብብ በልሳኑ በልሳን እንተ ታስተርኢ እስመ አዕረፈ እምአፈ ኵሉ ውሉደ ሰብእ እምዕለተ ድቀት <sup>12:26</sup>&nbsp;ወፈታሕኩ አፉሁ ወእዘኒሁ ወከናፍሪሁ ወአኀዝኩ እትናገር ምስሌሁ ዕብራይስጥ በልሳነ ፍጥረት። <sup>12:27</sup>&nbsp;ወነሥአ መጻሕፍተ አበዊሁ ወጽሑፋት እማንቱ ዕብራይስጥ ወደገሞን ወአኀዘ ይትመሀሮን እምአሜሃ ወአነ አየድዖ ኵሎ ዘይሰአኖ። ወተምህሮን ስድስተ ወርኀ ዝናም። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>12:22</sup>&nbsp;When he had finished speaking and praying, then the word of the Lord was sent to him through me: 'Now you, come from your land, your family, and your father's house to the land which I will show you. I will make you into a large and populous people. <sup>12:23</sup>&nbsp;I will bless you and magnify your reputation. You will become blessed in the earth. All the nations of the earth will be blessed in you. Those who bless you I will bless, while those who curse you I will curse. <sup>12:24</sup>&nbsp;I will become God for you, your son, your grandson, and all your descendants. Do not be afraid. From now until all the generations of the earth I am your God'. <sup>12:25</sup>&nbsp;Then the Lord God said to me: 'Open his mouth and his ears to hear and speak with his tongue in the revealed language'. For from the day of the collapse it had disappeared from the mouth(s) of all mankind. <sup>12:26</sup>&nbsp;I opened his mouth, ears, and lips and began to speak Hebrew with him — in the language of the creation. <sup>12:27</sup>&nbsp;He took his fathers' books (they were written in Hebrew) and copied them. From that time he began to study them, while I was telling him everything that he was unable (to understand). He studied them throughout the six rainy months.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>12:28</sup>&nbsp;በዓመት ሳብዕ ዘሱባዔ ሳድስ ወተናገረ ምስለ አቡሁ ወአይድዖ ከመ የሐውር ውእቱ እምካራን ለሐዊረ ምድረ ከናአን ይርአያ ወይግባእ ኀቤሁ <sup>12:29</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ ታራ አቡሁ ሖር በሰላም አምላከ ዓለም ያርትዕ ፍኖተከ ወእግዚአብሔር ምስሌከ ወይትማኅፀንከ እምኩሉ እኩይ። ወየሀብ ላዕሌከ ሣህለ ወምሕረተ ወሞገሰ በቅድመ እለ ይሬእዩከ ወኢይኰንንከ ኵሉ ውሉደ ሰብእ ለአእክዮ ዲቤከ ሖር በሰላም። <sup>12:30</sup>&nbsp;ወእመ ርኢከ ምድረ አዳም ለአዕይንቲከ ለኀዲር ውስቴታ ነዓ ወንሥአኒ ኀቤከ ወንሥኦ ለሎጥ ምስሌከ ወልደ አራን እኁከ ለከ ለወልድ እግዚአብሔር ምስሌከ <sup>12:31</sup>&nbsp;ወናኮርሃ እኅዋከ ኅድግ ኀቤየ እስከ ትገብእ በሰላም ወነሐውር ኵልነ ኅቡረ ምስሌከ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>12:28</sup>&nbsp;In the seventh year of the sixth week [1953], he spoke with his father and told him that he was leaving Haran to go to the land of Canaan to see it and return to him. <sup>12:29</sup>&nbsp;His father Terah said to him:
Go in peace.
May the eternal God make your way straight;
May the Lord be with you and protect you from every evil; 
May he grant you kindness, mercy, and grace before those who see you;
And may no person have power over you to harm you.
Go in peace.
<sup>12:30</sup>&nbsp;'If you see a land that, in your view, is a pleasant one in which to live, then come and take me to you. Take Lot, the son of your brother Haran, with you as your son. May the Lord be with you. <sup>12:31</sup>&nbsp;Leave your brother Nahor with me until you return in peace. Then all of us together will go with you'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>13:1</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረ አብራም እምካራን ወነሥአ ሶራይሃ ብእሲቶ። ወሎጥሃ ወልደ አራን እኁሁ ውስተ ምድረ ከናአን። ወመጽአ ውስተ አሱር ወአንሶሰወ እስከ ሰቂሞን ወኀደረ ኀበ ድርሰ ነዋኅ። <sup>13:2</sup>&nbsp;ወርእየ ወናሁ ምድር አዳም ጥቀ እምብዋአ ኤማት እስከ ኀበ ድርስ ነዋኅ። <sup>13:3</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ እግዚአብሔር ለከ ወለዘርእከ እሁብ ዛተ ምድረ <sup>13:4</sup>&nbsp;ወሐነጸ በህየ ምሥዋዐ ወአዕረገ ዲቤሁ ጽንሐሐ ለእግዚአብሔር ዘአስተርአዮ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>13:1</sup>&nbsp;Abram went from Haran and took his wife Sarai and Lot, the son of his brother Haran, to the land of Canaan. He came to Asur. He walked as far as Shechem and settled near a tall oak tree. <sup>13:2</sup>&nbsp;He saw that the land — from the entrance of Hamath to the tall oak — was very pleasant. <sup>13:3</sup>&nbsp;Then the Lord said to him: 'To you and your descendants I will give this land'. <sup>13:4</sup>&nbsp;He built an altar there and offered on it a sacrifice to the Lord who had appeared to him.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>13:5</sup>&nbsp;ወአንሥአ እምህየ ውስተ ደብረ ቤቴል ዘመንገለ ባሕር ወአጌ መንገለ ጽባሕ ወተከለ ደብተራሁ ህየ። <sup>13:6</sup>&nbsp;ወርእየ ወናሁ ምድር ጽፍሕት ወኄርት ጥቀ ወኵሉ ይሠርፅ ላዕሌሃ አውያን ወበለስ ወሮማን ዕፅ ባላን ወድርስ ወጤሬቤንቶስ ወዕፀወ ዘይት ወቄድሮስ ወቄጲሪሶስ ወሊባኖስ ወኵሉ ዕፀወ ገዳም ወማይ ዲበ አድባር። <sup>13:7</sup>&nbsp;ወባረኮ ለእግዚአብሔር ዘአውፅኦ እምነ ኡር ዘከለዳዊያን ወአምጽኦ ውስተዝ ደብር 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>13:5</sup>&nbsp;He departed from there toward the mountain of Bethel which is toward the sea, with Ai toward the east, and pitched his tent there. <sup>13:6</sup>&nbsp;He saw that the land was spacious and most excellent and (that) everything was growing on it: vines, fig trees, pomegranates, oak trees, holm oaks, terebinths, olive trees, cedars, cypresses, incense trees, and all (kinds of) wild trees; and (there was) water on the mountains. <sup>13:7</sup>&nbsp;Then he blessed the Lord who had led him from Ur of the Chaldeans and brought him to this mountain.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>13:8</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ በአሐዱ ዓመት በሱባዔ ሳብዕ በሠርቀ ወርኅ በዘ ቀዳሚ ሐነጸ ምሥዋዐ በዝ ደብር ወጸውዖ በስመ እግዚአብሔር አንተ አምላኪየ አምላከ ዘለዓለም። <sup>13:9</sup>&nbsp;ወአዕረገ ዲበ ምሥዋዕ ጽንሐሐ ለእግዚአብሔር ከመ የሀሉ ምስሌሁ ወኢይኅድጎ ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወቱ። <sup>13:10</sup>&nbsp;ወአንሥአ እምህየ ወሖረ መንገለ ደቡብ ወበጽሐ እስከ ኬብሮን ወኬብሮን አሜሃ ተሐንጸት ወነበረ ህየ ዓመተ ክልኤተ ወሖረ ውስተ ምድረ ደቡብ እስከ ቦአ ሎጥ። ወኮነ ዐባር ዲበ ምድር <sup>13:11</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረ አብራም ግብጽ በሣልስ ዓመት ዘሱባዔ ወኀደረ ውስተ ግብጽ ኀምስተ ዓመተ ዘእንበለ ትትሀየድ ብእሲቱ። እምኔሁ። <sup>13:12</sup>&nbsp;ወጠናይስ ዘግብጽ አሜሃ ተሐብጸት በሰብዓቱ ክረምት እምድኅረ ኬብሮን። <sup>13:13</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ አመ ሄዶ ፈርዖን ሶራይ ብእሲቶ ለአብራም ቀሠፈ እግዚአብሔር ፈርዖንሃ ወቤቶ በመቅሠፍት ዐቢይ በእንተ ሶራይ ብእሲቱ ለአብራም። <sup>13:14</sup>&nbsp;ወአብራም ክቡር በጥሪት ጥቀ በአባግዕ ወበአልህምት ወበአእዱግ ወበአፍራስ ወበአግማል ወበአግብርት ወበአእማት ወበብሩር ወበወርቅ ፈድፋደ። ወለሎጥኒ ወልደ እኁሁ በጥሪት። <sup>13:15</sup>&nbsp;ወአግብአ ፈርዖን ሶራይሃ ብእሲተ አብራም ወአፍለሶ እምድረ ግብጽ ወሖረ ውስተ መካን ኀበ ተከለ ደብተራሁ እንተ ቀዲሙ ውስተ መካነ ምሥዋዐ አጌ እምጽባሐ ቤቴል ወባሕር ወባሪኮ ለእግዚአብሔር አምላኩ ዘሜጦ በሰላም 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>13:8</sup>&nbsp;During the first year in the seventh week [1954] — on the first of the month in which he had initially built the altar on this mountain — he called on the name of the Lord: 'You, my God, are the eternal God'. <sup>13:9</sup>&nbsp;He offered to the Lord a sacrifice on the altar so that he would be with him and not abandon him throughout his entire lifetime. <sup>13:10</sup>&nbsp;He departed from there and went toward the south. When he reached Hebron (Hebron was built at that time), he stayed there for two years. Then he went to the southern territory as far as Boa Lot. There was a famine in the land. <sup>13:11</sup>&nbsp;So Abram went to Egypt in the third year of the week [1956]. He lived in Egypt for five years before his wife was taken from him by force. <sup>13:12</sup>&nbsp;Egyptian Tanais was built at that time — seven years after Hebron. <sup>13:13</sup>&nbsp;When the pharaoh took Abram's wife Sarai by force for himself, the Lord punished the pharaoh and his household very severely because of Abram's wife Sarai. <sup>13:14</sup>&nbsp;Now Abram had an extremely large amount of property: sheep, cattle, donkeys, horses, camels, male and female servants, silver, and very (much) gold. Lot — his brother's son — also had property. <sup>13:15</sup>&nbsp;The pharaoh returned Abram's wife Sarai and expelled him from the land of Egypt. He went to the place where he had first pitched his tent — at the location of the altar, with Ai on the east and Bethel on the west. He blessed the Lord his God who had brought him back safely.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>13:16</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ በዝ አርብዓ ወአሐዱ ኢዮቤልዎን በሣልስ ዓም ዘሱባዔ ቀዳሚ ገብአ ውስተ ዝመካን ወአዕረገ በዲቤሁ ጽንሐሐ ወጸውዐ በስመ እግዚአብሔር አምላክ ልዑል አምላኪየ ለዓለመ ዓለም። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>13:16</sup>&nbsp;During this forty-first jubilee, in the third year of the first week [1963], he returned to this place. He offered a sacrifice on it and called on the Lord's name: 'You, Lord, most high God, are my God forever and ever'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>13:17</sup>&nbsp;ወበራብዕ ዓመት ዘዝ ሱባዔ ተፈልጠ ሎጥ እምኔሁ ወኀደረ ሎጥ ውስተ ሰዶም ወሰብአ ሰዶም ኃጥኣን ጥቀ። <sup>13:18</sup>&nbsp;ወአከዮ በልቡ እስመ ተፈልጠ ወልደ እኁሁ እምኔሁ እስመ አልቦ ውሉደ <sup>13:19</sup>&nbsp;በውእቱ ዓመት አመ ተፄወወ ሎጥ። ወይቤሎ እግዚአብሔር ለአብራም እምድኅረ ተፈልጠ እምኔሁ ሎጥ በራብዕ ዓመት ዘዝ ሱባዔ። ወይቤሎ አንሥእ አዕይንቲከ እመካን ውእደ ሀለውከ ትነብር ህየ መንገለ ሰሜን ወሊባ ወባሕር ወጽባሕ <sup>13:20</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ኵላ ምድረ እንተ ትሬኢ ለከ ወለዘርእከ እመሁባ እስከ ለዓለም። ወእሬሲ ዘርእከ ከመ ኆፃ ባሕር እመ ይክል ሰብእ ኆልቆ ኆፃ ምድር ወዘርእከኒ ኢይትኆለቍ። <sup>13:21</sup>&nbsp;ተንሥእ ወአንሶሱ ውስተ ኑኃ ወርሕባ ወርኢ ኵሎ እስመ ለዘርእከ እሁባ። ወሖረ አብራም ኬብሮን ወኀደረ ህየ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>13:17</sup>&nbsp;In the fourth year of this week [1964] Lot separated from him. Lot settled in Sodom. Now the people of Sodom were very sinful. <sup>13:18</sup>&nbsp;He was brokenhearted that his brother's son had separated from him for he had no children. <sup>13:19</sup>&nbsp;In that year when Lot was taken captive, the Lord spoke to Abram — after Lot had separated from him, in the fourth year of this week — and said to him: 'Look up from the place where you have been living toward the north, the south, the west, and the east; <sup>13:20</sup>&nbsp;because all the land which you see I will give to you and your descendants forever. I will make your descendants like the sands of the sea. (Even) if a man can count the sands of the earth, your descendants will (still) not be counted. <sup>13:21</sup>&nbsp;Get up and walk through its length and its width. Look at everything because I will give it to your descendants'. Then Abram went to Hebron and lived there.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>13:22</sup>&nbsp;ወበዝ ዓመት መጽአ ከደለጎሞር ንጉሠ ኤላም አመርፋል ንጉሠ ሲናአር ወአሪአክ ንጉሠ ሴለሳር ወቴርጋል ንጉሠ አሕዛብ ወቀተልዎ ለንጉሠ ጎሞር ወጐየ ንጉሠ ሰዶም። ወብዙኃን ወድቁ በቍስል በስላ ሰዲማው በባሕረ ፄው <sup>13:23</sup>&nbsp;ወፄወዉ ሰዶምሃ ወአዳማሃ ወሴቦኤም ወፄወውዎ ለሎጥኒ ወልደ እኁሁ ለአብራም ሰኵሎ ጥሪቶ ወሖረ እስከ ዳን። <sup>13:24</sup>&nbsp;ወመጽአ ዘድኅነ ወነገሮ ለአብራም ከመ ተፄወወ ወልደ እኁሁ። <sup>13:25</sup>&nbsp;ወአስተረሰየ ልደ ቤቱ [ወሖረ አብራም ወቀተሎ ለከደለጎሞር ወየመይጠ ወዐሠረ ዐሥራተ እምኵሉ ወወሀቦ ለመልከ ጼዴቅ። ወዝንቱ ዐሥራት] ዲበ አብራም ወዲበ ዘርኡ ዓሥራተ ቀዳሚ ለእግዚአብሔር። ወእግዚአብሔር ሠርዖ ሥርዓተ ለዓለም ከመ የሀብዎ ለካህናት ለእለ ይትቀነዩ በቅድሜሁ ከመ የአኀዝዋ ለዓለም። <sup>13:26</sup>&nbsp;ወአልቦ ለዝ ሕግ ወሰነ መዋዕል እስመ ትውልድ ዘለዓለም ሠርዖ ከመ የሀቡ ዓሥራተ እምኵሉ ለእግዚአብሔር  እምዘርእ ወእምወይን ወእምቅብእ ወእምአልህምት ወእምአባግዕ <sup>13:27</sup>&nbsp;ወውእቱ ወሀበ ለካህናቲሁ ለበሊዕ ወለሰቲይ በፍሥሓ በቅድሜሁ።
