</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>13:22</sup>&nbsp;In this year Chedorlaomer, the king of Elam, Amraphel, the king of Shinar, Arioch, the king of Selasar, and Tergal, the king of the nations came and killed the king of Gomorrah, while the king of Sodom fled. Many people fell with wounds in the valley of Saddimaw, in the Salt Sea. <sup>13:23</sup>&nbsp;They took captive Sodom, Adamah, and Zeboim; they also took Lot, the son of Abram's brother, captive and all his possessions. He went as far as Dan. <sup>13:24</sup>&nbsp;One who had escaped came and told Abram that the son of his brother had been taken captive. <sup>13:25</sup>&nbsp;When he had armed his household servants, [Abram went and killed Chedorlaomer. Upon returning, he took a tithe of everything and gave it to Melchizedek. This tithe was] for Abram and his descendants the tithe of the firstfruits for the Lord. The Lord made it an eternal ordinance that they should give it to the priests who serve before him for them to possess it forever. <sup>13:26</sup>&nbsp;This law has no temporal limit because he has ordained it for the history of eternity to give a tenth of everything to the Lord — of seed, the vine, oil, cattle, and sheep. <sup>13:27</sup>&nbsp;He has given (it) to his priests to eat and drink joyfully before him.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>13:28</sup>&nbsp;ወበጽሐ ኀቤሁ ንጉሠ ሰዶም ወሰገደ ቅድሜሁ ወይቤ እግዚእነ አብራም ጸግወነ ነፍሰ እለ ባለሕከ ወምህርካሁሰ ይኩንከ። <sup>13:29</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ አብራም ሎቱ አነሥእ እደዊየ ኀበ አምላክ ልዑል እምፈትል እስከ ቶታነ አሣእን እመ እነሥእ እምኵሉ ዘዚአከ ከመ ኢትኩን በሃሌ አነ አብዐልክዎ ለአብራም። ዘእንበለ ዘበልዑ ዳእሙ ወራዙት ወመክፈልቶሙ ለዕደው እለ ሖሩ ምስሌየ አውናን ወኤስከል ወመምሪ እሙንቱ ይነሥኡ መክፈልቶሙ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>13:28</sup>&nbsp;When the king of Sodom came up to him, he knelt before him and said: 'Our lord Abram, kindly give us the people whom you rescued, but their booty is to be yours'. <sup>13:29</sup>&nbsp;Abram said to him: 'I lift my hands to the most high God (to show that) I will not take anything of yours — not a thread or sandal thongs, so that you may not say: «I have made Abram rich» — excepting only what the young men have eaten and the share of the men who went with me: Awnan, Eschol, and Mamre. These will take their share'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>14:1</sup>&nbsp;ወእምድኅረ ዝነገር በራብዕ ዓመት ዘዝ ሱባዔ በሠርቀ ሣልስ ወርኅ ኮነ ቃለ እግዚአብሔር ኀበ አብራም በሕልም እንዘ ይብል ኢትፍራህ አብራም አነ ውእቱ ቃውምከ ወዐስብከ ይፈደፍድ ጥቀ። <sup>14:2</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ እግዚኦ እግዚኦ ምንተ ትሁበኒ ወአንሰ አሐውር ዘእንበለ ውሉድ ወወልደ ማሴቅ አመትየ ውእቱ ደማስቆስ ኤሌኤዜር ውእቱ ይወርሰኒ ወሊተ ኢወሀብከኒ ዘርአ ሀበኒ ዘርአ። <sup>14:3</sup>&nbsp;2 ወይቤሎ ኢይወርሰከዝ ዘእንበለ ዘይወፅእ እምከርሥከ ውእቱ ይወርሰከ። <sup>14:4</sup>&nbsp;ወአውፅኦ አፍአ ወይቤሎ ነጽር ውስተ ሰማይ ወኆልቍ ከዋክብተ እመ ትክል ኆልቆቶሙ <sup>14:5</sup>&nbsp;ወነጸረ ሰማየ ወርእየ ከዋክብተ ወይቤሎ ከመዝ ይከውን ዘርእከ <sup>14:6</sup>&nbsp;ወአምኖ ለእግዚአብሔር ወተኆለቆ  ጽድቀ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>14:1</sup>&nbsp;After these things — in the fourth year of this week [1964], on the first of the third month — the word of the Lord came to Abram in a dream: 'Do not be afraid, Abram. I am your protector; your reward will be very large'. <sup>14:2</sup>&nbsp;He said: 'Lord, Lord, what are you going to give me when I go on being childless. The son of Maseq — the son of my maid servant — that is Damascene Eliezer — will be my heir. You have given me no descendants. Give me descendants'. <sup>14:3</sup>&nbsp;He said to him: 'This one will not be your heir but rather someone who will come out of your loins will be your heir'. <sup>14:4</sup>&nbsp;He brought him outside and said to him: 'Look at the sky and count the stars, if you can count them'. <sup>14:5</sup>&nbsp;When he had looked at the sky and seen the stars, he said to him: 'Your descendants will be like this'. <sup>14:6</sup>&nbsp;He believed the Lord, and it was credited to him as something righteous.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>14:7</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ አነ እግዚአብሔር ዘአውፃእኩከ እምነ ኡር ዘከለዳዊያን ከመ አሀብከ ምድረ ከነናዊያን ለእኂዝ ለዓለም ወለከዊነ ለከ አምላከ ወለዘርእከ እምድኅሬከ <sup>14:8</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ እግዚኦ እግዚኦ በምንት አአምር ከመ እወርስ። <sup>14:9</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ ንሣእ ሊተ ጠዕዋ ዘሠለስቱ ዓመት ወጠሌ ዘሠለስቱ ዓመት ወበግዐ ዘሠለስቱ ዓመት ወመንጤተ ወርግበ። <sup>14:10</sup>&nbsp;ወነሥአ ዘንተ ኵሎ በመንፈቀ ወርኅ ወውእቱ ይነብር ኀበ ድራይ ዘማምሪ እንተ ይእቲ ቅሩበ ኬብሮን <sup>14:11</sup>&nbsp;ወሐነጸ ምሥዋዐ ህየ ወዘብሐ ዘንተ ኵሎ ወከዐወ ደሞሙ ውስተ ምሥዋዕ ወነፈቆሙ እማእከል ወአንበሮሙ አንጸራቲሆሙ በበ ገጾሙ ወአዕዋፍሰ ኢነተፈ <sup>14:12</sup>&nbsp;ወይወርዱ አዕዋፍ ዲበ ስፍሕ ወይከልኦሙ አብራም ወኢየኀድግ አዕዋፍ ይልክፍዎን። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>14:7</sup>&nbsp;He said to him: 'I am the Lord who brought you from Ur of the Chaldeans to give you the land of the Canaanites to occupy forever and to become God for you and your descendants after you'. <sup>14:8</sup>&nbsp;He said: 'Lord, Lord, how will I know that I will inherit (it)'? <sup>14:9</sup>&nbsp;He said to him: 'Get for me a three-year-old calf, a three-year-old goat, a threeyear- old sheep, a turtledove, and a dove'. <sup>14:10</sup>&nbsp;He got all of these in the middle of the month. He was living at the oak of Mamre which is near Hebron. <sup>14:11</sup>&nbsp;He built an altar there and sacrificed all of these. He poured out their blood on the altar and divided them in the middle. He put them opposite one another, but the birds he did not divide. <sup>14:12</sup>&nbsp;Birds kept coming down on what was spread out, but Abram kept preventing them and not allowing the birds to touch them.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>14:13</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ ሶበ ዕርበተ ፀሐይ ድንጋፄ ወድቀ ላዕለ አብራም ወናሁ ግርማ ዐቢይ ጽልመት ወድቀ ላዕሌሁ ወተብህለ ለአብራም አእምሮ አእምር ከመ ፈላሴ ይከውን ዘርእከ ውስተ ምድረ ነኪር ወይቀንይዎሙ ወያሐምምዎሙ አርባዕተ ምእተ ዓመተ <sup>14:14</sup>&nbsp;ወለሕዝብኒ እለ ይትቀነዩ አነ እፈትሕ ሎሙ። ወእምድኅረዝ ይወፅኡ እምህየ ጥሪት ብዙኅ <sup>14:15</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተ ተሐውር ኀበ አበዊከ በሰላም ወትትቀበር በርስእ ሠናይ። <sup>14:16</sup>&nbsp;ወበትውልድ ራብዕ ይትመየጡ ዝየ እስመ ኢተፈጸመ ኃጢአቶሙ ለአሞሬዎን እስከ ይእዜ። <sup>14:17</sup>&nbsp;ወነቅህ እምንዋም ወተንሥአ ወፀሐይ ዐረበ ወነድ ኮነ ወናሁ እቶን ይጠይስ ወነበልባለ እሳት ኀለፈ ማእከለ ስፋሔ። <sup>14:18</sup>&nbsp;ወበይእቲ ዕለት ተካየደ ኪዳነ እግዚአብሔር ምስለ አብራም እንዘ ይብል ለዘርእከ እሁብ ዛተ ምድረ እምፈለገ ግብጽ እስከ ፈለገ ዐቢይ ፈለገ ኤውፍራጢስ ለቄኔውስ ወለቄኔዜውስ ወለቅድሞኔውስ ወለፌሬዜውስ ወለረፌእያን ወለፈከሬውስ ወለኤዌውስ። ወለአሞሬውስ። ወለከናኔውስ ወለጌርጌሴውስ ወለኢየቡሴው። <sup>14:19</sup>&nbsp;ወኀለፈ ወአዕረገ። አብራም ስፍሐተ ወአዕዋፈ ወመሥዋዕቶሙ ወሞጻሕቶሙ ወበልዖ እሳት። <sup>14:20</sup>&nbsp;ወበዛቲ ሌሊት ተካየድነ ኪዳነ ምስለ አብራም በከመ ኪዳን ዘተካየድነ በዛቲ ወርኅ ምስለ ኖኅ። ወአብራም ሐደሳ ለበዓል ወለሥርዓት ሎቱ እስከ ለዓለም 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>14:13</sup>&nbsp;At sunset, a terror fell on Abram; indeed a great, dark fear fell on him. It was said to Abram: 'Know for a fact that your descendants will be aliens in a foreign land. They will enslave them and oppress them for 400 years. <sup>14:14</sup>&nbsp;But I will judge the nation whom they serve. Afterwards, they will leave from there with many possessions. <sup>14:15</sup>&nbsp;But you will go peacefully to your fathers and be buried at a ripe old age. <sup>14:16</sup>&nbsp;In the fourth generation they will return to this place because until now the sins of the Amorites have not been completed'. <sup>14:17</sup>&nbsp;When he awakened and got up, the sun had set. There was a flame and an oven was smoking. Fiery flames passed between what was spread out. <sup>14:18</sup>&nbsp;On that day the Lord concluded a covenant with Abram with these words: 'To your descendants I will give this land from the river of Egypt as far as the great river, the Euphrates River: the Kenites, the Kenizzites, the Kadmonites, the Perizzites, the Rephaim, the Phakorites, the Hivites, the Amorites, the Canaanites, the Girgashites, and the Jebusites'. <sup>14:19</sup>&nbsp;It passed (along), and Abram offered what had been spread out, the birds, their (cereal) offering, and their libation. The fire devoured them. <sup>14:20</sup>&nbsp;During this night we concluded a covenant with Abram like the covenant which we concluded during this month with Noah. Abram renewed the festival and the ordinance for himself forever.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>14:21</sup>&nbsp;ወተፈሥሐ አብራም ወአይድዐ ዘንተ ኵሎ ለሰራይ ብእሲቱ። ወአምነ ከመ ይከውኖ ዘርእ ወይእቲሰ ኢትወልድ። <sup>14:22</sup>&nbsp;ወአምከረቶ ሰራይ ለአብራም ምታ ወትቤሎ ባእ ኀበ አጋር ልእክትየ ግብጻዊት እመቦ ከመ አሐንጽ ለከ እምኔሃ ዘርአ <sup>14:23</sup>&nbsp;ወስምዐ አብራም ቃለ ሰራይ ብእሲቱ ወይቤላ ግበሪ። ወነሥአት ሰራይ አጋርሃ ለአኪታ ግብጻዊት ወወሀበታ ለአብራም ለምታ ትኩኖ ብእሲተ። <sup>14:24</sup>&nbsp;ወቦአ ኀቤሃ ወፀንሰት ወወለደት ወልደ። ወጸውዐ ስሞ ይስማዔል በዓመት ኃምስ ዘዝ ሱባዔ ወውእቱ ዓመት ሰማንያ ወስድስቱ ዓም በሕይወተ አብራም።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>14:21</sup>&nbsp;Abram was very happy and told all these things to his wife Sarai. He believed that he would have descendants, but she continued not to have a child. <sup>14:22</sup>&nbsp;Sarai advised her husband Abram and said to him: 'Go in to my Egyptian slave-girl Hagar; perhaps I will build up descendants for you from her'. <sup>14:23</sup>&nbsp;Abram listened to his wife Sarai's suggestion and said to her: 'Do (as you suggest)'. So Sarai took her Egyptian slave-girl Hagar, and gave her to her husband Abram to be his wife. <sup>14:24</sup>&nbsp;He went in to her, she became pregnant, and gave birth to a son. He named him Ishmael in the fifth year of this week [1965]. That year was the eighty-sixth year in Abram's life.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>15:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበዓመት ኃምስ ዘሱባዔ ዘራብዑ ለኢዮቤልውን ዝንቱ በወርኅ ሣልስ በመንፈቀ ወርኅ ገብረ አብራም በዓለ ቀዳሜ ማእረረ ዘዘርአ ሥርናይ <sup>15:2</sup>&nbsp;ወአዕረገ መሥዋዕተ ሐዲስ ዲበ ምሥዋዕ ቀዳሜ እክል ለእግዚአብሔር። ላህመ ወበሐኰ ወበግዐ ዲበ ምሥዋዕ ጽንሓሐ ለእግዚአብሔር ወመሥዋዕቶሙ ወሞጻሕቶሙ አዕረገ ኵሎ ዲበ ምሥዋዕ ምስለ ስኂን። <sup>15:3</sup>&nbsp;ወአስተርአዮ እግዚአብሔር ወይቤሎ እግዚአብሔር ለአብራም አነ አምላከ ሰዳይ ወአሥምር በቅድሜየ ወኩን ፍጹመ <sup>15:4</sup>&nbsp;ወእሁብ ኪዳንየ ማእከሌየ ወማእከሌከ ወአልህቀከ ጥቀ <sup>15:5</sup>&nbsp;ወወድቀ አብራም በገጹ ወተናገሮ እግዚአብሔር ወይቤ <sup>15:6</sup>&nbsp;ናሁ ሥርዓትየ ምስሌከ ወእሬስየከ አበ ለብዙኃን አሕዛብ። <sup>15:7</sup>&nbsp;ወኢይጼዋዕ እንከ ስምከ አብራም ወይኩን ስምከ እምይእዜ ወእስከ ለዓለም አብርሃም እስመ አበ ብዙኃን አሕዛብ ሤምኩከ <sup>15:8</sup>&nbsp;ወአዐብየከ ጥቀ። ወእሁበከ ውስተ አሕዛብ ወነገሥት ይወፅኡ እምኔከ <sup>15:9</sup>&nbsp;ወእሁብ ኪዳንየ ማእከሌየ ወማእከሌከ ወማእከለ ዘርእከ እምድኅሬከ በትዝምዶሙ ወለሥርዓት ዘለዓለም ከመ እኩንከ አምላከ ወለዘርእከ እምድኅሬከ <sup>15:10</sup>&nbsp;[ወእሁብ ለከ ወለዘርእከ እምድኅሬከ] ምድረ ኀበ ፈለስከ ምድረ ከናአን ዘትኴንን ለዓለም ወእከውኖሙ አምላከ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>15:1</sup>&nbsp;During the fifth year of the fourth week of this jubilee [1986] — in the third month, in the middle of the month — Abram celebrated the festival of the firstfruits of the wheat harvest. <sup>15:2</sup>&nbsp;He offered as a new sacrifice on the altar the firstfruits of the food for the Lord — a bull, a ram, and a sheep; (he offered them) on the altar as a sacrifice to the Lord together with their (cereal) offerings and their libations. He offered everything on the altar with frankincense. <sup>15:3</sup>&nbsp;The Lord appeared to him, and the Lord said to Abram: 'I am the God of Shaddai. Please me and be perfect, <sup>15:4</sup>&nbsp;I will place my covenant between me and you. I will increase you greatly'. <sup>15:5</sup>&nbsp;Then Abram fell prostrate. The Lord spoke with him and said: <sup>15:6</sup>&nbsp;'My pact is now with you. I will make you the father of many nations. <sup>15:7</sup>&nbsp;You will no longer be called Abram; your name from now to eternity is to be Abraham because I have designated you the father of many nations. <sup>15:81</sup>&nbsp;will make you very great. I will make you into nations, and kings shall emerge from you. <sup>15:9</sup>&nbsp;I will place my covenant between me and you and your descendants after you throughout their generations and as an eternal pact so that I may be God to you and to your descendants after you. <sup>15:10</sup>&nbsp;[To you and your descendants after you I will give] the land where you have resided as an alien — the land of Canaan which you will rule forever. I will be their God'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>15:11</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ እግዚአብሔር ለአብርሃም ወአንተኒ ኪዳንየ ዕቀብ አንተ ወዘርእከ እምድኅሬከ ተከሰቡ ኵሎ ሮስክሙ ወተከሰቡ ቍልፈተክሙ ወይከውን ትእምርተ ሥርዓትየ ዘለዓለም ማእከሌየ ወማእከሌክሙ <sup>15:12</sup>&nbsp;ወለወልድ አመ ሳምንት ዕለት ትከስብዎ ኵሎ ሮሰ በትዝምድክሙ ወልደ ቤት። ወዘበወርቅ ተሣየጥክሙ እምኵሉ ውሉደ ነኪር ዘአጥረይክሙ ዘኢኮነ እምዘርእከ <sup>15:13</sup>&nbsp;ክስበተ ይትከሰብ ልደ ቤትከ ወዘበወርቅ ተሣየጥከ ይትከሰቡ። ወይከውን ኪዳንየ ውስተ ሥጋክሙ ለሥርዓት ዘለዓለም <sup>15:14</sup>&nbsp;ወዘኢኮነ ክሱበ ሮስ ዘኢተከስበ ሥጋ ቍልፈቱ በዕለተ ሳምንት ትሤሮ ይእቲ ነፍስ እምዘመዳ እስመ ኪዳንየ ነሠተ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>15:11</sup>&nbsp;Then the Lord said to Abraham: 'As for you, keep my covenant — you and your descendants after you. Circumcise all your males; circumcise your foreskins. It will be a sign of my eternal pact (which is) between me and you. <sup>15:12</sup>&nbsp;You will circumcise a child on the eighth day — every male in your families: the person (who has been born in your) house, the one whom you purchased with money from any foreigners — whom you have acquired who is not from your descendants. <sup>15:13</sup>&nbsp;The person who is born in your house must be circumcised; and those whom you purchased with money are to be circumcised. My covenant will be in your flesh as an eternal pact. <sup>15:14</sup>&nbsp;The male who has not been circumcised — the flesh of whose foreskin has not been circumcised on the eighth day — that person will be uprooted from his people because he has violated my covenant'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>15:15</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ እግዚአብሔር ለአብርሃም ሶራ ብእሲትከ ኢትጸዋዕ እንከ ስማ ሶራ እስመ ሳራ ስማ። <sup>15:16</sup>&nbsp;ወእባርካ ወእሁበከ እምኔሃ ወልደ ወእባርኮ ወይከውን ሕዝበ ወነገሥተ አሕዛብ እምኔሁ ይከውኑ። <sup>15:17</sup>&nbsp;ወወድቀ አብርሃም በገጹ ወተፈሥሐ ወይቤ በልቡ እመ ለዘ ምእትኑ ዓመቱ ይትወለድ ወልድ ወሳራሂ እንተ ተስዓ ዓመታ ትወልድ። <sup>15:18</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ አብርሃም ለእግዚአብሔር መፍትው ይሕየው ይስማዔል ቅድሜከ። <sup>15:19</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ እግዚአብሔር ኦሆ። ወሳራሂ ትወልድ ለከ ወልደ ወትጼውዕ ስሞ ይስሐቅ። ወአቀውም ኪዳንየ ምስሌሁ ኪዳነ ዘለዓለም ወለዘርኡ እምድኅሬሁ <sup>15:20</sup>&nbsp;ወበእንተ ይስማዔልሂ ሰማዕኩከ ወናሁ እባርኮ ወአልህቆ ወአበዝኆ ጥቀ። ወዓሠርተ ወክልኤተ መላእክተ ይወልድ ወእሰይሞ ውስተ ሕዝብ ዐቢይ። <sup>15:21</sup>&nbsp;ወኪዳንየ አቀውም ምስለ ይስሐቅ ዘትውልድ ለከ ሳራ በዝ መዋዕል በዓመት ካልእ። <sup>15:22</sup>&nbsp;ወፈጺሞ እንዘ ይትናገር ምስሌሁ ወዐርገ እግዚአብሔር እመልዕልተ አብርሃም። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>15:15</sup>&nbsp;The Lord said to Abraham: 'Your wife Sarai will no longer be called Sarai for her name will be Sarah. <sup>15:16</sup>&nbsp;I will bless her. I will give you a son from her and will bless him. He will become a nation, and kings of nations will come from him'. <sup>15:17</sup>&nbsp;Abraham fell prostrate and was very happy. He said to himself: 'Will a son be born to one who is 100 years of age? Will Sarah who is 90 years of age give birth (to a child)'? <sup>15:18</sup>&nbsp;(So) Abraham said to the Lord: 'I wish that Ishmael could live in your presence'. <sup>15:19</sup>&nbsp;The Lord said: 'Very well, but Sarah, too, will give birth to a son for you and you will name him Isaac. I will establish my covenant with him as an eternal covenant and for his descendants after him. <sup>15:20</sup>&nbsp;Regarding Ishmael I have listened to you. I will indeed bless him, increase him, and make him very numerous. He will father 12 princes, and I will make him into a large nation. <sup>15:21</sup>&nbsp;But my covenant I will estabhsh with Isaac to whom Sarah will give birth for you at this time next year'. <sup>15:22</sup>&nbsp;When he had finished speaking with him, the Lord went up from Abraham.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>15:23</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረ አብርሃም በከመ ይቤሎ እግዚአብሔር ወነሥአ ይስማዔልሃ ወልዶ ወኵሎ ልደ ቤቱ ወዘሂ በወርቅ ተሣየጠ ኵሎ ሮሰ ዘውስተ ቤቱ ወከሰበ ሥጋ ምክሳቦሙ። <sup>15:24</sup>&nbsp;ወበጊዜ ዛቲ ዕለት ተከስበ አብርሃም [ወልደ ቤቱ] ወሰብአ ቤቱ ወኵሎሙ እለ በወርቅ ተሣየጠ ወእምውሉደ ነኪራንኒ ተከስቡ ምስሌሁ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>15:23</sup>&nbsp;Abraham did as the Lord told him. He took his son Ishmael, everyone who was born in his house and who had been purchased with money — every male who was in his house — and circumcised the flesh of their foreskins. <sup>15:24</sup>&nbsp;On the same day Abraham was circumcised; [those who were born in his house], the men of his household, and all those who had been purchased with money (even from foreigners) were circumcised with him.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>15:25</sup>&nbsp;ወዝሕግ ለኵሉ ትውልድ ዘለዓለም ወአልቦ ክስበተ መዋዕል። ወአልቦ ተዐድዎ አሐተ ዕለተ እምሰማኒ መዋዕል እስመ ሥርዓት ዘለዓለም ውእቱ ሥሩዕ ወጽሑፍ ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ። <sup>15:26</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሉ ዘትውልደ ዘኢተከስበ ሥጋ ነፍስቱ እስከ ሰሙን ዕለት ኢኮነ እምውሉደ ሥርዓት ዘትካየደ እግዚአብሔር ለአብርሃም እስመ እምነ ውሉደ ሙስና። ወአልቦ እንከ ትእምርተ ላዕሌሁ ከመ ይኩን ለእግዚአብሔር እስመ ለአማስኖ ወለተሐጕሎ እምነ ምድር ወለተሠርዎ እምነ ምድር እስመ ኪዳኖ ለእግዚአብሔር አምላክነ ነሠተ <sup>15:27</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ኵሎሙ መላእክተ ገጽ። ወኵሎሙ መላእክተ ቅዳሴ ከመዝ ፍጥረቶሙ እምዕለተ ፍጥረቶሙ ወአንጸሮሙ ለመላእክተ ገጽ ወለመላእክተ ቅዳሴ ቀደሶ ለእስራኤል ከመ ይኩን ምስሌሁ ወምስለ መላእክቲሁ ቅዱሳን። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>15:25</sup>&nbsp;This law is (valid) for all history forever. There is no circumcising of days, nor omitting any day of the eight days because it is an eternal ordinance ordained and written on the heavenly tablets. <sup>15:26</sup>&nbsp;Anyone who is born, the flesh of whose private parts has not been circumcised by the eighth day does not belong to the people of the pact which the Lord made with Abraham but to the people (meant for) destruction. Moreover, there is no sign on him that he belongs to the Lord, but (he is meant) for destruction, for being destroyed from the earth, and for being uprooted from the earth because he has violated the covenant of the Lord our God. <sup>15:27</sup>&nbsp;For this is what the nature of all the angels of the presence and all the angels of hohness was like from the day of their creation. In front of the angels of the presence and the angels of holiness he sanctified Israel to be with him and his holy angels.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>15:28</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተኒ አዝዝ ለውሉደ እስራኤል ወይዕቀቡ ትእምርተዝ ኪዳን ለትውልዶሙ ለሥርዓት ዘለዓለም ወኢይሠረው እምነ ምድር <sup>15:29</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ትእዛዝ ተሠርዐ ለኪዳን ከመ ይዕቀብዎ ለዓለም። ዲበ ኵሎሙ ደቂቀ እስራኤል <sup>15:30</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ይስማዔልሃ ወውሉዶ ወአኃዊሁ ወዔሳውሃ ኢያቅረቦ ኀቤሁ እግዚአብሔር ወኢኀረየ ቦሙ እስመ እምውሉደ አብርሃም እሙንቱ እስመ አእመሮሙ ወእስራኤልሃ ኀረየ ይኩንዎ ሕዝበ <sup>15:31</sup>&nbsp;ወቀደሶ ወአስተጋብአ እምኵሉ ውሉደ ሰብእ። እስመ ብዙኅ አሕዛብ ወብዙኅ ሕዝብ ወኵሉ ሎቱ ወዲበ ኵሉ አስለጠ መናፍስተ ከመ ያስሕቶሙ እምድኅሬሁ <sup>15:32</sup>&nbsp;ወዲበ እስራኤልሰ ኢያስለጠ ወኢመነሂ መልአከ ወመንፈሰ። እስመ ውእቱ ባሕቲቱ መኰንኖሙ ወውእቱ የዐቅቦሙ ወይትኀሠሦሙ እምእደ መላእክቲሁ ወእምነ መናፍስቲሁ ወእምእደ ኵሉ ወኵሉ ትእዛዛቲሁ ከመ ይዕቀቦሙ ወይባርኮሙ ወይኩንዎ ሎቱ ወውእቱ ይኩኖሙ ሎሙ እምይእዜ ወእስከ ለዓለም። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>15:28</sup>&nbsp;Now you command the Israelites to keep the sign of this covenant throughout their history as an eternal ordinance so that they may not be uprooted from the earth <sup>15:29</sup>&nbsp;because the command has been ordained as a covenant so that they should keep it forever on all the Israehtes. <sup>15:30</sup>&nbsp;For the Lord did not draw near to himself either Ishmael, his sons, his brothers, or Esau. He did not choose them (simply) because they were among Abraham's children, for he knew them. But he chose Israel to be his people. <sup>15:31</sup>&nbsp;He sanctified them and gathered (them) from all mankind. For there are many nations and many peoples and all belong to him. He made spirits rule over all in order to lead them astray from following him. <sup>15:32</sup>&nbsp;But over Israel he made no angel or spirit rule because he alone is their ruler. He will guard them and require them for himself from his angels, his spirits, and everyone, and all his powers so that he may guard them and bless them and so that they may be his and he theirs from now and forever.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>15:33</sup>&nbsp;ወይእዜኒ አነ እዜንወከ ከመ በዛቲ ሥርዓት ይሔስዉ ውሉደ እስራኤል ወኢይከስቡ ውሉዶሙ በከመ ኵሉ ዝሕግ እስመ እምሥጋ ክስበቶሙ ይከውኑ መትርፋነ ውስተ ክስበተ ውሉዶሙ ወኵሎሙ ውሉደ ቤልአር የኀድጉ ውሉዶሙ ዘእንበለ ክስበት በከመ ተወልዱ። <sup>15:34</sup>&nbsp;ወትከውን መዓት ላዕለ ውሉደ እስራኤል ዐባይ እምኀበ እግዚአብሔር እስመ ኀደጉ ኪዳኖ ወእምቃሉ ተግኅሡ ወወሐኩ ወፀረፉ በከመ ኢገብሩ ሥርዓቶ ለዝ ትእምርተ። እስመ ገብሩ ነፍሳቲሆሙ ከመ አሕዛብ ለሰስሎ ወለተሠርዎ እምድር ወአልቦ እንከ ሎሙ ኅድገተ ወስርየተ ከመ ይስረይ ወይትኀደጉ እምኩሉ ኀጢአት ለስሕተተ ዛቲ ዘለዓለም።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>15:33</sup>&nbsp;I am now telling you that the Israelites will prove false to this ordinance. They will not circumcise their sons in accord with this entire law because they will leave some of the flesh of their circumcision when they circumcise their sons. All the people of Belial will leave their sons uncircumcised just as they were born. <sup>15:34</sup>&nbsp;Then there will be great anger from the Lord against the Israelites because they neglected his covenant, departed from his word, provoked, and blasphemed in that they did not perform the ordinance of this sign. For they have made themselves like the nations so as to be removed and uprooted from the earth. They will no longer have forgiveness or pardon so that they should be pardoned and forgiven for every sin, for (their) violation of this eternal (ordinance).
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>16:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበሠርቀ ወርኅ ራብዕ አስተርአይናሁ ለአብርሃም በኀበ ድርስ ዘማምሪም ወተናገርነ ምስሌሁ ወንሕነ አይዳዕናሁ ከመ ይትወሀቦ ወልድ እምሳራ ብእሲቱ። <sup>16:2</sup>&nbsp;ወሰሐቀት ሳራ እስመ ሰምዐት ከመ ተናገርነ ዘንተ ቃለ ምስለ አብርሃም። ወዘለፍናሃ ወፈርሀት ወሐሰወት ከመ ሰሐቀት በእንተ ቃል <sup>16:3</sup>&nbsp;ወነገርናሃ ስሞ ለወልዳ በከመ ሥሩዕ ወጽሑፍ ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ ይስሐቅ። <sup>16:4</sup>&nbsp;ወአመ ገባእነ ኀቤሃ በጊዜ ሰዓት ወይእቲኒ ፀንሰት ወልደ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>16:1</sup>&nbsp;On the first of the fourth month we appeared to Abraham at the oak of Mamre. We spoke with him and told him that a child would be given to him from his wife Sarah. <sup>16:2</sup>&nbsp;Sarah laughed when she heard that we had conveyed this message to Abraham, but when we chided her, she became frightened and denied that she had laughed about the message. <sup>16:3</sup>&nbsp;We told her the name of her son as it is ordained and written on the heavenly tablets — Isaac — <sup>16:4</sup>&nbsp;and (that) when we returned to her at a specific time she would have become pregnant with a son.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>16:5</sup>&nbsp;ወበዝ ወርኅ ገብረ እግዚአብሔር ኵነኔሆሙ ለሰዶም ወለገሞራ ወሶቦኤም ወለኵሉ አድያመ ዮርዳኖስ ወአውዓዮሙ በእሳት ወበተይ ወአጥፍኦሙ እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት። በከመ ናሁ አይዳዕኩከ ኵሎ ምግባሮሙ ከመ ፀዋጋን ወኃጥኣን ጥቀ ወይትራኰሱ ወይዜምዉ በሥጋሆሙ ወይገብሩ ርኵሰ በዲበ ምድር። <sup>16:6</sup>&nbsp;ወከማሁ ይገብር እግዚአብሔር ኵነኔ በመካናት በውእደ ይገብሩ በከመ ይኵሶሙ ለሰዶም ከመ ኵነኔሃ ለሰዶም። <sup>16:7</sup>&nbsp;ወለሎጥ ናድኅኖ እስመ ተዘከሮ እግዚአብሔር ለአብርሃም ወአውፅኦ እማእከለ ግፍታኤ። <sup>16:8</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረ ውእቱኒ ወአዋልዲሁኒ ኀጢአተ በዲበ ምድር ዘኢኮነ ዲበ ምድር እመዋዕለ አዳም እስከ አሜሁ እስመ ሰከበ ብእሲ ምስለ ወለቱ <sup>16:9</sup>&nbsp;ወናሁ ተአዘዘ ወተቈርፀ ላዕለ ኵሉ ዘርኡ ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ ከመ ያእትቶሙ ወከመ ይሠርዎሙ ወከመ ይግበር ኵነኔሆሙ በከመ ኵነኔ ሰዶም ወከመ ኢያትርፍ ሎቱ ኵሎ ዘርአ ውስተ ምድር ዘሰብእ በዕለተ ደይን። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>16:5</sup>&nbsp;During this month the Lord executed the judgment of Sodom and Gomorrah, Zeboim and all the environs of the Jordan. He burned them with fire and brimstone and annihilated them until the present in accord with what I have now told you (about) all their actions — that they were savage and very sinful, (that) they would defile themselves, commit sexual sins in their flesh, and do what was impure on the earth. <sup>16:6</sup>&nbsp;The Lord will execute judgment in the same way in the places where people commit the same sort of impure actions as Sodom — just like the judgment on Sodom. <sup>16:7</sup>&nbsp;But we went about rescuing Lot because the Lord remembered Abraham. So he brought him out from the overthrow (of Sodom). <sup>16:8</sup>&nbsp;He and his daughters committed a sin on the earth which had not occurred on the earth from the time of Adam until his time because the man lay with his daughter. <sup>16:9</sup>&nbsp;It has now been commanded and engraved on the heavenly tablets regarding all his descendants that he is to remove them, uproot them, execute judgment on them like the judgment of Sodom, and not to leave him any human descendants on the earth on the day of judgment.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>16:10</sup>&nbsp;ወአዝንቱ ወርኅ ግዕዘ አብርሃም እምነ ኬብሮን ወሖረ ወኀደረ ማእከለ ቃዴስ ወሱር ውስተ አድባረ ጌራሮን <sup>16:11</sup>&nbsp;ወበመንፈቀ ወርኅ ኃምስ ግዕዘ እምህየ ወኀደረ ኀበ ዐዘቅተ መሐላ። <sup>16:12</sup>&nbsp;ወበመንፈቀ ወርኅ ሳድስ ሐወጸ እግዚአብሔር ለሳራ ወገብረ ላቲ በከመ ይቤ <sup>16:13</sup>&nbsp;ወፀንሰት ወወለደት ወልደ በወርኅ ሣልስ ወበመንፈቀ ወርኅ በመዋዕል ዘይቤሎ እግዚአብሔር ለአብርሃም በበዓለ ቀዳሚ ማእረር ተወልደ ይስሐቅ <sup>16:14</sup>&nbsp;ወከሰቦ አብርሃም ወልደ መዋዕል ሰሙን ውእቱ ቀዳሚ ተከስበ በከመ ኪዳን እንተ ተሠርዐት ለዓለም። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>16:10</sup>&nbsp;During this month Abraham migrated from Hebron. He went and settled between Ḳadesh and Sur in the mountains of Gerar. <sup>16:11</sup>&nbsp;In the middle of the fifth month he migrated from there and settled at the well of the oath. <sup>16:12</sup>&nbsp;In the middle of the sixth month the Lord visited Sarah and did for her as he had said. <sup>16:13</sup>&nbsp;She became pregnant and gave birth to a son in the third month; in the middle of the month, on the day that the Lord had told Abraham — on the festival of the firstfruits of the harvest — Isaac was born. <sup>16:14</sup>&nbsp;Abraham circumcised him when he was eight days old. He was the first to be circumcised according to the covenant which was ordained forever.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>16:15</sup>&nbsp;ወበዓመት ሳድስ ዘሱባዔ ራብዕ መጻእነ ኀበ አብርሃም ኀበ ዐዘቅተ መሐላ ወአስተርአይናሁ በከመ ንቤላ ለሳራ ከመ ንግባእ ኀቤሃ ወይእቲሂ ፀንሰት ወልደ <sup>16:16</sup>&nbsp;ወተመየጥነ በወርኅ ሳብዕ ወረከብናሃ ለሳራ ፅንስተ ቅድሜነ ወባረክናሃ ወዜነውናሃ ኵሎ ዘተአዘዘ ሎቱ ከመ ኢይመውት ዓዲ እስከ ይወልድ ስድስተ ውሉደ ወይሬኢ ዘእንበለ ይሙት። ወበይስሐቅ ይጼዋዕ ሎቱ ስም ወዘርእ <sup>16:17</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሉ ዘርአ ውሉዱ አሕዛበ ይከውኑ ወምስለ አሕዛብ ይትኌለቁ። ወእምነ ውሉደ ይስሐቅሂ አሐዱ ይከውን ለዘርእ ቅዱስ ወውስተ አሕዛብኒ ኢይትኌለቍ። <sup>16:18</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ለመክፈልተ ልዑል ይከውን ወውስተ ዘይመልክ አምላክ ወረደ ኵሉ ዘርኡ ከመ ይኩን ለእግዚአብሔር ሕዝበ ትርሲት እምኵሉ ሕዝብ ወከመ ይኩን መንግሥተ ወክህነተ ወሕዝበ ቅዱሰ። <sup>16:19</sup>&nbsp;ወሖርነ ፍኖተነ ወዜነውናሃ ለሳራ ኵሎ ዘነገርናሁ ወተፈሥሑ ክልኤሆሙ ፍሥሐ ዐቢየ ጥቀ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>16:15</sup>&nbsp;In the sixth year of the fourth week [1987] we came to Abraham at the well of the oath. We appeared to him just as we had said to Sarah that we would return to her and she would have become pregnant with a son. <sup>16:16</sup>&nbsp;We returned during the seventh month, and in front of us we found Sarah pregnant. We blessed him and told him everything that had been commanded for him: that he would not yet die until he became the father of six sons and (that) he would see (them) before he died; but (that) through Isaac he would have a reputation and descendants. <sup>16:17</sup>&nbsp;All the descendants of his sons would become nations and be numbered with the nations. But one of Isaac's sons would become a holy progeny and would not be numbered among the nations, <sup>16:18</sup>&nbsp;for he would become the share of the Most High. All his descendants had fallen into that (share) which God owns so that they would become a people whom the Lord possesses out of all the nations; and that they would become a kingdom, a priesthood, and a holy people. <sup>16:19</sup>&nbsp;Then we went on our way and told Sarah all that we had reported to him. The two of them were extremely happy.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>16:20</sup>&nbsp;ወሐነጸ ህየ ምሥዋዐ ለእግዚአብሔር ዘባልሖ ወለዘያስተፈሥሖ በምድረ ፍልሰቱ። ወገብረ በዓለ ፍሥሓ በዝ ወርኅ ሰቡዐ መዋዕለ በቅሩበ ምሥዋዕ ዘሐነጸ ኀበ ዐዘቅተ መሐላ <sup>16:21</sup>&nbsp;ወሐነጸ ምጽላላተ ሎቱ ወለአግብርቲሁ በዛቲ በዓል ወውእቱ መቅድመ ገብረ በዓለ መጸላት በዲበ ምድር <sup>16:22</sup>&nbsp;ወበዝ ሰቡዕ መዋዕል ሀሎ ይቄርብ ኵሎ ዕለተ በበ ዕለት ውስተ ምሥዋዕ ጽንሐሐ ለእግዚአብሔር አልህምተ ክልኤተ ወአብሐኰ ክልኤተ አባግዐ ሰብዓተ መሐስአ ጠሊ አሐደ በእንተ ኃጢአት ከመ ያስተስሪ ቦቱ በእንቲአሁ ወበእንተ ዘርኡ <sup>16:23</sup>&nbsp;ወለመሥዋዕተ መድኃኒት አብሐኰ ሰብዓተ ወመሐስአ ሰብዓተ ወአባግዐ ሰብዓተ ወደቤላተ ሰብዓተ ወመሥዋዕቶሙሂ ወሞጻሕቶሙሂ ላዕለ ኵሉ ሥብሖሙ የዐጥን። በዲበ ምሥዋዕ ጽንሐሐ ኅሩየ ለመዓዛ ሠናይ። <sup>16:24</sup>&nbsp;ወበጽባሕ ወሰርክሂ የዐጥን አፈወ ስኂን ወቅንአተ ወማየ ልብን ወናርዶስ ወከርቤ ወሰንብልተ ወቍስጠ ሰብዓቲሆሙ ዘንተ ኵሎ ይቄርብ ወጉአ ዕሩየ ተዐርዮ ድሙረ ንጹሐ። <sup>16:25</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረ ዘንተ በዓለ ሰቡዐ መዋዕለ እንዘ ይትፌሠሕ በኵሉ ልቡ ወበኵሉ ነፍሱ ውእቱ ወኵሎሙ እለ ቤቱ ወአልቦ መነሂ ነኪረ ምስሌሁ ወኵሉ ዘኢኮነ ክሱበ። <sup>16:26</sup>&nbsp;ወባረኮ ለፈጣሪሁ ዘፈጠሮ በትዝምዱ እስመ ለሥምረቱ ፈጠሮ እስመ አእመረ ወጠየቀ ከመ እምኔሁ ይከውን ተክለ ጽድቅ ለትውልድ ዘለዓለም ወእምኔሁ ዘርእ ቅዱስ ከመ ይኩን ከማሁ ለዘ ገብረ ኵሎ። <sup>16:27</sup>&nbsp;ወባረከ ወተፈሥሐ ወጸውዐ ስማ ለዛቲ በዓል በዓለ እግዚአብሔር ፍሥሓ ስጥወተ ለአምላክ ልዑል። <sup>16:28</sup>&nbsp;ወባረክናሁ ለዓለም ወኵሎ ዘርአ ዘእምድኅሬሁ በኵሉ ትውልደ ምድር እስወ ገብረ ዘንተ በዓለ በጊዜሃ በከመ ስምዐ ጽላተ ሰማይ። <sup>16:29</sup>&nbsp;በእንተዝ ተሠርዐ ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ ላዕለ እስራኤል ከመ ይኩኑ ገባርያነ በዓለ መጸለት ሰቡዐ መዋዕለ በፍሥሓ በወርኅ ሳብዕ ዘይትወከፍ በቅድመ እግዚአብሔር ሕገ ዘለዓለም በትውልዶሙ በኵሉ ዓመት ወዓመታት። <sup>16:30</sup>&nbsp;ወአልቦ ለዝንቱ ወሰነ መዋዕል እስመ ለዓለም ውእቱ ሥሩዕ ላዕለ እስራኤል ከመ ይግበርዋ ወይንበሩ ወስተ ምጽላል ወከመ ያንብሩ አክሊላተ ዲበ ርእሶሙ ወከመ ይንሥኡ ዐጽቀ ቈጽል ወኲሐ እሙሐዝ። <sup>16:31</sup>&nbsp;ወነሥአ አብርሃም ልበ ፀበርት ወፍሬ ዕፅ ሠናይ ወበኵሉ ዕለት እምዕለት ሀሎ እንዘ የአውድ ምሥዋዐ በአዕፁቅ ስብዕ ለዕለት በጽባሕ ይጼብሕ ወይገኒ ለአምላኩ ኵሎ ዘበፍሥሓ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>16:20</sup>&nbsp;There he built an altar for the Lord who had recued him and who was making him so happy in the country where he resided as an alien. He celebrated a joyful festival in this month — for seven days — near the altar which he had built at the well of the oath. <sup>16:21</sup>&nbsp;He constructed tents for himself and his servants during this festival. He was the first to celebrate the festival of tabernacles on the earth. <sup>16:22</sup>&nbsp;During these seven days he was making — throughout all the days, each and every day — an offering to the Lord on the altar: two bulls, two rams, seven sheep, one goat for sins in order to atone 10 through it for himself and his descendants. <sup>16:23</sup>&nbsp;And as a peace offering: seven rams, seven kids, seven sheep, seven he-goats as well as their (cereal-)offerings and their libations over all their fat — (all of these) he would burn on the altar as a choice offering for a pleasing fragrance. <sup>16:24</sup>&nbsp;In the morning and evening he would burn fragrant substances: frankincense, galbanum, stacte, nard, myrrh, aromatic spices, and costum. All seven of these he would offer beaten, equally mixed, pure. <sup>16:25</sup>&nbsp;He celebrated this festival for seven days, being happy with his whole heart and all his being — he and all those who belonged to his household. There was no foreigner with him, nor anyone who was uncircumcised. <sup>16:26</sup>&nbsp;He blessed his creator who had created him in his generation because he had created him for his pleasure, for he knew and ascertained that from him there would come a righteous plant for the history of eternity and (that) from him there would be holy descendants so that they should be like the one who had made everything. <sup>16:27</sup>&nbsp;He gave a blessing and was very happy. He named this festival the festival of the Lord — a joy acceptable to the most high God. <sup>16:28</sup>&nbsp;We blessed him eternally and all the descendants who would follow him throughout all the history of the earth because he had celebrated this festival at its time in accord with the testimony of the heavenly tablets. <sup>16:29</sup>&nbsp;For this reason it has been ordained on the heavenly tablets regarding Israel that they should celebrate the festival of tabernacles joyfully for seven days during the seventh month which is acceptable in the Lord's presence — a law which is eternal throughout their history in each and every year. <sup>16:30</sup>&nbsp;This has no temporal limit because it is ordained forever regarding Israel that they should celebrate it, live in tents, place wreaths on their heads, and take leafy branches and willow branches from the stream. <sup>16:31</sup>&nbsp;So Abraham took palm branches and the fruit of good trees, and each and every day he would go around the altar with the branches — seven times per day. In the morning he would give praise and joyfully offer humble thanks to his God for everything.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>17:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበአሐዱ ዓመት ዘሱባዔ ኃምስ ኀደገ ጥበ ይስሐቅ በዝንቱ ኢዮቤልዉ ወገብረ አብርሃም ግዝአ ዐቢየ በወርኅ ሣልስ በዕለተ ኀድገ ጥበ ወልዱ ደስሐቅ። <sup>17:2</sup>&nbsp;ወይስማዔል ወልዳ ለአጋር ግብጻዊት በቅድመ ገጹ ለአብርሃም አቡሁ በመካኑ ወተፈሥሐ አብርሃም ወባረኮ ለእግዚአብሔር እስመ ርእየ ሎቱ ውሉዶ ወኢሞተ ዘእንበለ ውሉድ <sup>17:3</sup>&nbsp;ወተዘከረ ቃሎ ዘተናገሮ በዕለተ ተፈልጠ ሎጥ እምኔሁ። ወተፈሥሐ እስመ ወሀቦ እግዚአብሔር ዘርአ በዲበ ምድር ከመ ይረሳ ለምድር። ወባራኮ በኵሉ አፉሁ ለፈጣሬ ኵሉ። </span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>17:1</sup>&nbsp;In the first year of the fifth week [1989], in this jubilee, Isaac was weaned. Abraham gave a large banquet in the third month, on the day when his son Isaac was weaned. <sup>17:2</sup>&nbsp;Now Ishmael, the son of Hagar the Egyptian, was in his place in front of his father Abraham. Abraham was very happy and blessed the Lord because he saw his own sons and had not died childless. <sup>17:3</sup>&nbsp;He remembered the message which he had told him on the day when Lot had separated from him. He was very happy because the Lord had given him descendants on the earth to possess the land. With his full voice he blessed the creator of everything.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>17:4</sup>&nbsp;ወርእየቶ ለይስማዔል ሳራ እንዘ ይትዋነይ ወይዘፍን ወአብርሃምኒ እንዘ ይትፌሣሕ ፍሥሓ ዐቢየ ወቀንአት ለይስማዔል። ወትቤሎ ለአብርሃም ስድድ ዛተ ወለተ ወወልዳ እስመ ኢይወርስ ወልዳ ለዛ ወለት ምስለ ወልድየ ይስሐቅ። <sup>17:5</sup>&nbsp;ወማሕዝን ቃሉ በቅድመ አዕይንተ አብርሃም በእንተ አመቱ ወበእንተ ወልዱ ከመ ይስድዶሙ እምኀቤሁ። <sup>17:6</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ እግዚአብሔር ለአብርሃም ኢይኩን ሐዘን በቅድመ አዕይንቲከ በእንተ ሕፃን ወበእንተ ወለት ኵሎ ዘትቤለከ ሳራ ስማዕ ንባባ ወግበር እስመ በይስሐቅ ይጼዋዕ ለከ ስም ወዘርእ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>17:4</sup>&nbsp;When Sarah saw Ishmael playing and dancing and Abraham being extremely happy, she became jealous of Ishmael. She said to Abraham: 'Banish this girl and her son because this girl's son will not be an heir with my son Isaac'. <sup>17:5</sup>&nbsp;In Abraham's opinion the command regarding his servant girl and his son — that he should banish them from himself — was saddening, <sup>17:6</sup>&nbsp;but the Lord said to Abraham: 'It ought not to be a sad thing in your opinion regarding the child and the girl. Listen to everything that Sarah says to you and do (it) because through Isaac you will have a reputation and descendants.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>17:7</sup>&nbsp;ወበእንተ ወልዳስ ለዛ ወለት ውስተ ዐቢይ ሕዝብ እሬስዮ እስመ እምዘርእከ ውእቱ። <sup>17:8</sup>&nbsp;ወጌሠ አብርሃም በነግህ ወነሥአ ሐባውዘ ወዝቀ ማይ ወአስከማ ለአጋር ወለሕፃን ወፈነዋ <sup>17:9</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረት ወታንጌጊ በገዳመ ቤርሳቦ ወተፈጸመ ማይ እምዝቅ ወጸምአ ሕፃን ወስእነ ሐዊረ ወወድቀ። <sup>17:10</sup>&nbsp;ወነሥአቶ እሙ ወሐዊራ ገደፈቶ ታሕተ አሐቲ ኤልያስ ወሖረት ወነበረት አንጻሮ መጠነ አሐቲ ምንዳፍ እስመ ትቤ ኢይርአይ ሞቶ ለሕፃንየ ወነቢራ በከየት። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>17:7</sup>&nbsp;Now with regard to this girl's son — I will make him into a large nation because he is one of your descendants'. <sup>17:8</sup>&nbsp;So Abraham rose early in the morning, took food and a bottle of water, placed them on the shoulders of Hagar and the child, and sent her away. <sup>17:9</sup>&nbsp;She went and wandered about in the wilderness of Beersheba. When the water in the bottle was gone, the child grew thirsty. He was unable to go on and fell. <sup>17:10</sup>&nbsp;His mother took him and, going on, she threw him under an olive tree. Then she went and sat opposite him at a distance of a bowshot, for she said: 'May I not see the death of my child'. When she sat down she cried.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>17:11</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤላ መልአክ አምላክ አሐዱ እምቅዱሳን ምንተ ትበክዪ አንቲ አጋር ተንሢአኪ ንሥእዮ ለሕፃን ወአኀዝዮ በእዴኪ እስመ ሰምዐ እግዚአብሔር ቃለኪ ወርእዮ ለሕፃን። <sup>17:12</sup>&nbsp;ወከሠተት አዕይንቲሃ ወርእየት ዐዘቅተ ማይ ወሖረት ወመልአት ዝቃ ማየ ወአስተየት ሕፃና። ወተንሥአት ወሖረት መንገለ በድወ ፍራም። <sup>17:13</sup>&nbsp;ወልህቀ ሕፃን ወኮነ ነዳፌ ወሀሎ እግዚአብሔር ምስሌሁ ወነሥአት ሎሙ እሙ ብእሲተ እምአዋልደ ግብጽ <sup>17:14</sup>&nbsp;ወወለደት ሎቱ ወልደ ወጸውዐ ስሞ ናቤዎት እስመ ትቤ ቅሩብ እግዚአብሔር ሊተ ሶበ ጸዋዕክዎ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>17:11</sup>&nbsp;An angel of God — one of the holy ones — said to her: 'What are you crying about, Hagar? Get up, take the child, and hold him in your arms, because the Lord has heard you and has seen the child'. <sup>17:12</sup>&nbsp;She opened her eyes and saw a well of water. So she went, filled her bottle with water, and gave her child a drink. Then she set out and went toward the wilderness of Paran. <sup>17:13</sup>&nbsp;When the child grew up, he became an archer and the Lord was with him. His mother took a wife for him from the Egyptian girls. <sup>17:14</sup>&nbsp;She gave birth to a son for him, and he named him Nebaioth, for she said: 'The Lord was close to me when I called to him'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>17:15</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ በሱባዔ ሳብዕ በቀዳሚ ዓመት በወርኅ ቀዳሚ በዝ ኢዮቤልዉ አመ ዐሡሩ ወሰኑዩ ለዝ ወርኅ ኮነ ቃላት በሰማያት በእንተ አብርሃም። ከመ ውእቱ መሀይምን በኵሉ ዘይትናገሮ ወያፈቅሮ እግዚአብሔር። ወበኵሉ ምንዳቤ ኮነ ምእመነ። <sup>17:16</sup>&nbsp;ወመጽአ መኰንን መስቴማ ወይቤ ቅድሜሁ ለአምላክ ናሁ አብርሃም ያፈቅሮ ለይስሐቅ ወልዱ ወያስተአድሞ ኪያሁ እምኵሉ። በሎ ያዕርጎ ጽንሐሐ ዲበ ምሥዋዕ ወአንተ ትሬኢ ለእመ ይገብር ዘንተ ቃለ ወታአምር ለእመ ወሀይምን ውእቱ በኵሉ ዘታሜክሮ። <sup>17:17</sup>&nbsp;ወእግዚአብሔር ያአምር ከመ መሃይምን አብርሃም በኵሉ ምንዳቤ ዘይቤሎ እስመ አመክሮ በምድሩ ወበዐባር ወአመከሮ በብዕለ ነገሥት። ወአመከሮ ካዕበ በብእሲቱ እንዘ ትትሀየድ ወበክስበት ወአመክሮ በይስማዔል ወበአጋር አመቱ አመ ፈነዎሙ። <sup>17:18</sup>&nbsp;ወበኵሉ በዘአመከሮ ተረክበ ምእመነ ወኢተአንተለ ነፍሱ ወኢጐንደየ ገቢሮቶ እስመ ምእመን ወመፍቀሬ እግዚአብሔር።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>17:15</sup>&nbsp;During the seventh week, in the first year during the first month — on the twelfth of this month — in this jubilee [2003], there were voices in heaven regarding Abraham, that he was faithful in everything that he told him, (that) the Lord loved him, and (that) in every difficulty he was faithful. <sup>17:16</sup>&nbsp;Then Prince Mastema came and said before God: 'Abraham does indeed love his son Isaac and finds him more pleasing than anyone else. Tell him to offer him as a sacrifice on an altar. Then you will see whether he performs this order and will know whether he is faithful in everything through which you test him'. <sup>17:17</sup>&nbsp;Now the Lord was aware that Abraham was faithful in every difficulty which he had told him. For he had tested him through his land and the famine; he had tested him through the wealth of kings; he had tested him again through his wife when she was taken forcibly, and through circumcision; and he had tested him through Ishmael and his servant girl Hagar when he sent them away. <sup>17:18</sup>&nbsp;In everything through which he tested him he was found faithful. He himself did not grow impatient, nor was he slow to act; for he was faithful and one who loved the Lord.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>18:1</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ እግዚአብሔር አብርሃም አብርሃም ወይቤ ነየ አነ <sup>18:2</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ ንሥእ ወልደከ ፍቁረከ ዘታፈቅር ይስሐቅሃ ወሖር ውስተ ምደር ልዕልት ወአዕርጎ ውስተ አሐዱ እምአድባር ዘአነ አየድዐከ <sup>18:3</sup>&nbsp;ወአሌለየ በነገህ ወጸዐነ አድግቶ ወክልኤተ ደቆ ነሥአ ምስሌሁ ወይስሐቅሃ ወልዶ ወዕፀወ መሥዋዕት ሠፀረ ወሖረ ወስተ መካን በሠሉስ ዕለት። ወርእየ መካነ እምርሑቅ <sup>18:4</sup>&nbsp;ወበጽሐ እስከ ዐዘቅተ ማይ ወይቤ ለደቁ ንበሩ ዝየ ምስለ አድግት ወአነ ወሕፃን ነሐውር ወሰጊደነ ንገብእ ኀቤክሙ። <sup>18:5</sup>&nbsp;ወነሥአ ዕፀ መሥዋዕት ወአስከሞ ለይስሐቅ ወልዱ ወነሥአ በእዴሁ እሳተ ወመጥባሕተ። ወሖሩ ክልኤሆሙ ኅቡረ እስከ ውእቱ መካን። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>18:1</sup>&nbsp;The Lord said to him: 'Abraham, Abraham'! He replied: 'Yes'? <sup>18:2</sup>&nbsp;He said to him: 'Take your son, your dear one whom you love — Isaac — and go to a high land. Offer him on one of the mountains which I will show you'. <sup>18:3</sup>&nbsp;So he got up early in the morning, loaded his donkey, and took with him two servants as well as his son Isaac. He chopped the wood for the sacrifice and came to the place on the third day. He saw the place from a distance. <sup>18:4</sup>&nbsp;When he reached a well of water, he ordered his servants: 'Stay here with the donkey while I and the child go on. After we have worshiped, we will return to you'. <sup>18:5</sup>&nbsp;He took the wood for the sacrifice and placed it on his son Isaac's shoulders. He took fire and a knife in his hands. The two of them went together to that place.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>18:6</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ይስሐቅ ለአቡሁ አባ። ወይቤ ነየ አነ ወልድየ። ወይቤሎ ናሁ እሳት ወመጥባሕት ወዕፀው ወአይቴ በግዕ ዘለጽንሓሕ አባ። <sup>18:7</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ እግዚአብሔር ያሬኢ ሎቱ በግዐ ለጽንሓሕ ወልድየ። ወቀርበ ኀበ መካን ዘደብረ እግዚአብሔር <sup>18:8</sup>&nbsp;ወሐነጸ ምሥዋዐ ወአንበረ ዕፀወ ዲበ መሥዋዕት ወአሰረ ይስሐቅሃ ወልዶ ወአንበሮ ዲበ ዕፀው ዘመልዕልተ ምሥዋዕ ወሰፍሐ እዴሁ ይንሥእ መጥባሕተ ከመ ይዝብሖ ለይስሐቅ ወልዱ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>18:6</sup>&nbsp;Isaac said to his father: 'Father'. He replied: 'Yes, my son'? He said to him: 'Here are the fire, the knife, and the wood, but where is the sheep for the sacrifice, father'? <sup>18:7</sup>&nbsp;He said: 'The Lord will provide for himself a sheep for the sacrifice, my son'. When he neared the place of the mountain of the Lord, <sup>18:8</sup>&nbsp;he built an altar and placed the wood on the altar. Then he tied up his son Isaac, placed him on the wood which was on the altar, and reached out his hands to take the knife in order to sacrifice his son Isaac.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>18:9</sup>&nbsp;ወአነ ቆምኩ ቅድሜሁ ወቅድመ መኰንነ መስቴማ ወይቤ እግዚአብሔር በሎ ኢያውርድ እዴሁ ላዕለ ሕፃን ወኢይግበር ምንተኒ ላዕሌሁ እስመ አእመርኩ ከመ ፈራሄ እግዚአብሔር ውእቱ። <sup>18:10</sup>&nbsp;ጸዋዕክዎ እምሰማይ ወእቤሎ አብርሃም ወደንገፀ ወይቤ ነየ አነ። <sup>18:11</sup>&nbsp;ወእቤሎ ኢትፈኑ እዴከ ዲበ ሕፃን ወኢትግበረ ምንተኒ ዲቤሁ እስመ ይእዜ አእመርኩ ከመ ፈራሄ እግዚአብሔር አንተ ወኢመሐከ ወልደከ በኵረከ እምኔየ <sup>18:12</sup>&nbsp;ወተኀፍረ መኰንነ መስቴማ ወአንሥአ አብርሃም አዕይንቲሁ ወርእየ ወናሁ አሐዱ በሐኵ እኁዝ ወይመጽእ በአቅርንቲሁ ወሖረ አብርሃም ወነሥኦ ለበሐኵ ወአዕረጎ ለጽንሓሕ ህየንተ ወልዱ። <sup>18:13</sup>&nbsp;ወጸውዖ አብርሃም ለውእቱ መካን እግዚአብሔር ርእየ ከመ ይትበሀል እግዚአብሔር ርእየ ውእቱ ደብሩ ለጽዮን። <sup>18:14</sup>&nbsp;ወጸውዖ እግዚአብሔር ለአብርሃም በስሙ ዳግመ እምሰማይ በከመ አስተርአይነ ከመ ንትናገሮ በስመ እግዚአብሔር <sup>18:15</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ በርእስየ መሐልኩ ይቤ እግዚአብሔር እስመ ገበርከ ዘንተ ቃለ ወኢመሐከ ወልደከ በኵረከ እምኔየ ዘአፍቀርከ። እስመ ባርኮ እባርከከ ወአብዝኆ አበዝኅ ዘርአከ ከመ ከዋክብተ ሰማይ ወከመ ኆፃ ዘድንጋገ ባሕር። ወይወርሱ ዘርእከ አህጉረ ፀሮሙ <sup>18:16</sup>&nbsp;ወይትባረኩ በዘርእከ ኵሎሙ አሕዛበ ምድር ህየንተ ዘሰማዕከ ቃለ ዚአየ። ወአይዳዕኩ ለኵሉ ከመ ምእመን አንተ ሊተ በኵሉ ዘእቤለከ ሖር በሰላም። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>18:9</sup>&nbsp;Then I stood in front of him and in front of the prince of Mastema. The Lord said: 'Tell him not to let his hand go down on the child and not to do anything to him because I know that he is one who fears the Lord'. <sup>18:10</sup>&nbsp;So I called to him from heaven and said to him: 'Abraham, Abraham'! He was startled and said: 'Yes'? <sup>18:11</sup>&nbsp;I said to him: 'Do not lay your hands on the child and do not do anything to him because now I know that you are one who fears the Lord. You have not refused me your first-born son'. <sup>18:12</sup>&nbsp;The prince of Mastema was put to shame. Then Abraham looked up and saw a ram caught; it was coming with its horns. Abraham went and took the ram. He offered it as a sacrifice instead of his son. <sup>18:13</sup>&nbsp;Abraham named that place 'The Lord Saw' so that it is named 'The Lord Saw'. It is Mt. Zion. <sup>18:14</sup>&nbsp;The Lord again called to Abraham by his name from heaven, just as we had appeared in order to speak to him in the Lord's name. <sup>18:15</sup>&nbsp;He said: 'I have sworn by myself, says the Lord: because you have performed this command and have not refused me your first-born son whom you love, I will indeed bless you and will indeed multiply your descendants like the stars in the sky and like the sands on the seashore. Your descendants will possess the cities of their enemies. <sup>18:16</sup>&nbsp;All the nations of the earth will be blessed through your descendants because of the fact that you have obeyed my command. I have made known to everyone that you are faithful to me in everything that I have told you. Go in peace'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>18:17</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረ አብርሃም ኀበ ደቁ ወተንሥኡ ወሖሩ ቤርሳቤ ኅቡረ። ወኀደረ አብርሃም ኀበ ዐዘቅተ መሐላ። <sup>18:18</sup>&nbsp;ወይገብር ዛተ በዓለ በኵሉ ዓመታት ሰቡዐ ዕለተ በፍሥሓ ወሰመያ በዓለ እግዚአብሔር በከመ ሰቡዕ ዕለት እለ ሖረ ወተመይጠ በሰላም። <sup>18:19</sup>&nbsp;ወከመዝ ሥሩዕ ውእቱ ወጽሑፍ ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ በእንተ እስራኤል ወዲበ ዘርኡ ለገቢረ ዛቲ በዓል ሰቡዐ ዕለተ በፍሥሓ በዓል።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>18:17</sup>&nbsp;Then Abraham went to his servants. They set out and went together to Beersheba. Abraham lived at the well of the oath. <sup>18:18</sup>&nbsp;He used to celebrate this festival joyfully for seven days during all the years. He named it the festival of the Lord in accord with the seven days during which he went and returned safely. <sup>18:19</sup>&nbsp;This is the way it is ordained and written on the heavenly tablets regarding Israel and his descendants: (they are) to celebrate this festival for seven days with festal happiness. 
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>19:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበዓመት አሐዱ ዘሱባዔ ቀዳሚ በዘ አርብዓ ወክልኤቱ ኢዮቤልዉ ተመይጠ አብርሃም ወኀደረ አንጸረ ኬብሮን ዛቲ ይእቲ ቀሪያታርባቅ ክልኤ ሱባዔ ዓመት። <sup>19:2</sup>&nbsp;ወበዓመት ቀዳሚ ዘሱባዔ ሣልስ ዘዝ ኢዮቤልዉ ተፈጸመ መዋዕለ ሕይወተ ሳራ ወሞተት በኬብሮን። <sup>19:3</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረ አብርሃም ከመ ይብኪያ ወይቅብራ። ወናሜክሮ እመ ይትዔገሥ መንፈሱ ወኢይትአነተል በቃለ አፉሁ ወተረክበ በዝኒ ዕጉሠ ወኢተሀውከ። <sup>19:4</sup>&nbsp;እስመ በትዕግሥተ መንፈስ ተናገረ ምስለ ውሉደ ኬጥ ከመ የሀብዎ መካነ ከመ ይቅበር በድኖ ውስቴቱ። <sup>19:5</sup>&nbsp;ወእግዚአብሔር ወሀቦ ሞገሰ ሎቱ በቅድመ ኵሎሙ እለ ይሬእይዎ። ወአስተብቍዐ በየውሀት እምኀበ ውሉደ ኬጥ ወወሀብዎ ምድረ በዐት ዘካዕበት ዘአንጸረ መምብራም እንተ ይእቲ ኬብሮን በአርብዓ ብሩር <sup>19:6</sup>&nbsp;ወእሙንቱሂ ያስተበቍዕዎ እንዘ ይብሉ ነሀብከ በከ ወኢነሥአ እምእዴሆሙ በከ እስመ ወሀበ ሤጦ ለመካን ብሩረ ፍጹመ። ወሰገደ ሎሙ ካዕበ ወእምዝ ቀበረ በድኖ ውስተ በዐት ዘካዕበት። <sup>19:7</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ ኵሉ መዋዕለ ሕይወታ ለሳራ ምእት ወዕሥራ ወሰብዐቱ እሉ ዝክልኤ ኢዮቤልዉ ወአርባዕቱ ሱባዔ ወዓመት አሐዱ ዝንቱ መዋዕለ ዓመታተ ሕይወታ ለሳራ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>19:1</sup>&nbsp;During the first year of the first week in the forty-second jubilee [2010], Abraham returned and lived opposite Hebron — that is, Kiriath Arba — for two weeks of years. <sup>19:2</sup>&nbsp;In the first year of the third week of this jubilee [2024] the days of Sarah's life were completed and she died in Hebron. <sup>19:3</sup>&nbsp;When Abraham went to mourn for her and to bury her, we were testing whether he himself was patient and not annoyed in the words that he spoke. But in this respect, too, he was found to be patient and not disturbed, <sup>19:4</sup>&nbsp;because he spoke with the Hittites in a patient spirit so that they would give him a place in which to bury his dead. <sup>19:5</sup>&nbsp;The Lord gave him a favorable reception before all who would see him. He mildly pleaded with the Hittites, and they gave him the land of the double cave which was opposite Mamre — that is, Hebron — for a price of 400 silver pieces. <sup>19:6</sup>&nbsp;They pleaded with him: 'Allow us to give (it) to you for nothing'! Yet he did not take (it) from them for nothing but he gave as the price of the place the full amount of money. He bowed twice to them and afterwards buried his dead in the double cave. <sup>19:7</sup>&nbsp;All the time of Sarah's life was 127 — that is, two jubilees, four weeks, and one year. This was the time in years of Sarah's life.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>19:8</sup>&nbsp;ወዝመከራ ዓሥር በዘ ተመከረ ቦቱ አብርሃም ወተረክበ ምእመነ ዕጉሠ መንፈስ <sup>19:9</sup>&nbsp;ወኢይቤ ቃለ በእንተ ንባብ ዘምድር ዘይቤ እግዚአብሔር የሀባ ኪያሃ ሎቱ ወለዘርኡ እምድኅሬሁ። ወመካነ አስተብቍዐ በህየ ከመ ይቅበር በድኖ እስመ ተረክበ መሃይምነ ወተጽሕፈ ዐርከ እግዚአብሔር ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>19:8</sup>&nbsp;This was the tenth test by which Abraham was tried, and he was found to be faithful (and) patient in spirit. <sup>19:9</sup>&nbsp;He said nothing about the promise of the land which said that the Lord would give it to him and his descendants after him. He pleaded for a place there to bury his dead because he was found to be faithful and was recorded on the heavenly tablets as the friend of the Lord.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>19:10</sup>&nbsp;ወበዓመት ራብዕ ሎቱ ነሥአ ለይስሐቅ ወልዱ ብእሲተ ወስማ ርብቃ ወለተ ባቱኤል ወልደ ናኮር እኅወ አብርሃም እኅተ ላባ ወባቱኤል ወለዶሙ ለባቱኤላዊያን ወልደ ሜልከ ዘብእሲተ ናኮር እኅወ አብርሃም። <sup>19:11</sup>&nbsp;ወአብርሃም ነሥአ ሎቱ ሣልስተ ብእሲተ ወስማ ኬጡራ እምነ ውሉደ ልደ ቤቱ አመ ሞተት አጋር እምቅድመ ሳራ <sup>19:12</sup>&nbsp;ወወለደት ሎቱ ውሉደ ስድስተ ዘንበሪሃ ወያክስንሃ ወማዳይሃ ወማዳንሃ ወኢያዝቦቅሃ ወሴሂያሃ በክልኤ ሱባዔ ዓመት። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>19:10</sup>&nbsp;In its fourth year [2027] he took a wife for his son Isaac. Her name was Rebecca, the daughter of Bethuel (the son of Abraham's brother Nahor), the sister of Laban — Bethuel was their father — the daughter of Bethuel, the son of Milcah who was the wife of Abraham's brother Nahor. <sup>19:11</sup>&nbsp;Abraham married a third wife whose name was Keturah — one of the children of his household servants — when Hagar died prior to Sarah. <sup>19:12</sup>&nbsp;She gave birth to six sons for him — Zimran, Jokshan, Medai, Midian, Ishbak, and Shuah — during two weeks of years.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>19:13</sup>&nbsp;ወበሱባዔ ሳድስ በካልእ ዓመቱ ወለደት ርብቃ ለይስሐቅ ክልኤ ደቂቀ ያዕቆብሃ ወዔሳውሃ ወያዕቆብሰ ፍጹም ወራትዕ ወዔሳው ውእቱ ብእሲ ድሩክ ወሐቃላዊ ወጸጓር ወያዕቆብ የኀድር ውስተ ምጽላላት <sup>19:14</sup>&nbsp;ወልህቁ ወራዙት ወተምህረ ያዕቆብ መጽሐፈ ወዔሳውሰ ኢተምህረ እስመ ብእሲ ሐቃላዊ ውእቱ ወነዓዊ ወተምህረ ፀብአ ወኵሉ ግብሩ ድሩክ። <sup>19:15</sup>&nbsp;ወያፈቅር ያዕቆብሃ አብርሃም ወይስሐቅ ዔሳውሃ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>19:13</sup>&nbsp;In the sixth week, during its second year [2046], Rebecca gave birth to two sons for Isaac: Jacob and Esau. Jacob was perfect and upright, while Esau was a harsh, rustic, and hairy man. Jacob used to live in tents. <sup>19:14</sup>&nbsp;When the boys grew up, Jacob learned (the art of) writing, but Esau did not learn (it) because he was a rustic man and a hunter. He learned (the art of) warfare, and everything that he did was harsh. <sup>19:15</sup>&nbsp;Abraham loved Jacob but Isaac (loved) Esau.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>19:16</sup>&nbsp;ወርእየ አብርሃም ግብሮ ለዔሳው ወአእመረ ከመ በያዕቆብ ይጼዋዕ ሎቱ ስም ወዘርእ። ወጸውዓ ለርብቃ ወአዘዛ በእንተ ያዕቆብ እስመ ርእየ ከመ ይእቲኒ ታፈቅሮ ለያዕቆብ ፈድፋደ እምነ ዔሳው <sup>19:17</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤላ ወለትየ ዕቀቢ ወልድየ ያዕቆብሃ እስመ ውእቱ ይከውን ህየንቴየ ዲበ ምድር ወለበረከት በማእከለ ውሉደ ሰብእ ወለኵሉ ዘርአ ሴም ለትምክሕት <sup>19:18</sup>&nbsp;እስመ አአምር ከመ ኪያሁ የኀሪ እግዚአብሔር ሎቱ ለሕዝብ ቃውም እምኵሎሙ እለ ዲበ ገጸ ምድር። <sup>19:19</sup>&nbsp;ወናሁ ይስሐቅ ወልድየ ያፈቅሮ ለዔሳው እምነ ያዕቆብ ወአነ እሬእየኪ መፍቀሪተ ጽድቅ ያዕቆብሃ <sup>19:20</sup>&nbsp;ወስኪ ዓዲ አሠንዮ ላዕሌሁ ወይኩና አዕይንቲኪ ላዕሌሁ ለፍቁር። እስመ ውእቱ ይከውነነ ለበረከት ዲበ ምድር እምይእዜ ወእስከ ኵሉ ትውልደ ዓለም <sup>19:21</sup>&nbsp;ይጽንዓ እደዊኪ ወትትፈሣሕ ልብኪ በወልድኪ ያዕቆብ። እስመ ኪያሁ አፍቀርኩ ፈድፋደ እምኵሎሙ ውሉድየ እስመ ለዓለም ይትባረክ ወዘርኡ ይከውን ዘይመልእ ኵላ ምድረ <sup>19:22</sup>&nbsp;እመ ይክል ሰብእ ኆልቆ ኆፃ ምድር ከማሁ ይትኌለቁ ዘርኡሂ <sup>19:23</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሎን በረከት እለ ባረከኒ እግዚአብሔር ኪያየ ወዘርእየ ለያዕቆብ ወለዘርኡ ይኩን ኵሎ መዋዕለ <sup>19:24</sup>&nbsp;ወበዘርኡ ይትባረክ ስምየ ወስመ አበዊየ ሴም ወኖኅ ወሄኖክ ወመላልኤል ወሄኖስ ወሴት ወአዳም <sup>19:25</sup>&nbsp;ወእሙንቱ ይኩኑ ለሣርሮ ሰማይ ወለአጽንዖ ምድር ወለሐድሶ ኵሉ ብርሃናት ዘዲበ ምጽናዓት። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>19:16</sup>&nbsp;As Abraham observed Esau's behavior, he realized that through Jacob he would have a reputation and descendants. He summoned Rebecca and gave her orders about Jacob because he saw that she loved Jacob much more than Esau. <sup>19:17</sup>&nbsp;He said to her: 'My daughter, take care of my son Jacob because he will occupy my place on the earth and (will prove) a blessing among mankind and the glory of all the descendants of Shem. <sup>19:18</sup>&nbsp;For I know that the Lord will choose him as his own people (who will be) special from all who are on the surface of the earth. <sup>19:19</sup>&nbsp;My son Isaac now loves Esau more than Jacob, but I see that you rightly love Jacob. <sup>19:20</sup>&nbsp;Increase your favor to him still more; may your eyes look at him lovingly because he will prove to be a blessing for us on the earth from now and throughout all the history of the earth. <sup>19:21</sup>&nbsp;May your hands be strong and your mind be happy with your son Jacob because I love him much more than all my sons; for he will be blessed forever and his descendants will fill the entire earth. <sup>19:22</sup>&nbsp;If a man is able to count the sands on the earth, in the same way his descendants, too, will be counted. <sup>19:23</sup>&nbsp;May all the blessings with which the Lord blessed me and my descendants belong to Jacob and his descendants for all time. <sup>19:24</sup>&nbsp;Through his descendants may my name and the name of my ancestors Shem, Noah, Enoch, Malaleel, Enos, Seth, and Adam be blessed. <sup>19:25</sup>&nbsp;May they serve (the purpose of) laying heaven's foundations, making the earth firm, and renewing all the luminaries which are above the firmament'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>19:26</sup>&nbsp;ወጸውዖ ለያዕቆብ በቅድመ አዕይንቲሃ ለርብቃ እሙ ወሰዐሞ ወባረኮ ወይቤ <sup>19:27</sup>&nbsp;ወልድየ ያዕቆብ ፍቁር ዘአፍቀረት ነፍስየ ይባርከ አምላክ እመልዕልተ ምጽናዓት ወየሀብከ ኵሎን በረከታተ እለ ባረኮ ለአዳም ወሄኖክሃ ወኖኅሃ ወሴምሃ ወኵሎ ዘመጠነ ተናገረኒ። ወኵሎ ዘመጠነ ይቤ የሀበኒ ያጥግእ ላዕሌከ ወላዕለ ዘርእከ እስከ ለዓለም በከመ መዋዕለ ሰማይ ዲበ ምድር <sup>19:28</sup>&nbsp;ወኢይመብሉ ላዕሌከ ወላዕለ ዘርእከ መናፍስተ መስቴማ ከመ ያርኅቁከ እምድኅረ እግዚአብሔር ዘውእቱ አምላክከ እምይእዜ ወእስከ ለዓለም። <sup>19:29</sup>&nbsp;ወይኩንከ እግዚአብሔር አምላክ አበ ወአንተሂ ወልደ በኵረ ወለሕዝብ ኵሎ መዋዕለ። ሖር ወልድየ በሰላም። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>19:26</sup>&nbsp;Then he summoned Jacob into the presence of his mother Rebecca, kissed him, blessed him, and said: <sup>19:27</sup>&nbsp;'My dear son Jacob whom I myself love, may God bless you from above the firmament. May he give you all the blessings with which he blessed Adam, Enoch, Noah, and Shem. Everything that he said to me and everything that he promised to give me may he attach to you and your descendants until eternity — like the days of heaven above the earth. <sup>19:28</sup>&nbsp;May the spirits of Mastema not rule over you and your descendants to remove you from following the Lord who is your God from now and forever. <sup>19:29</sup>&nbsp;May the Lord God become your father and you his first-born son and people for all time. Go in peace, my son'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>19:30</sup>&nbsp;ወወፅኡ ክልኤሆሙ ኅቡረ እምኀበ አብርሃም <sup>19:31</sup>&nbsp;ወአፍቀረቶ ርብቃ ለያዕቆብ በኵሉ ልባ ወበኵሉ መንፈሳ ብዙኀ ፈድፋደ እምነ ዔሳው ወይስሐቅ ያፈቅሮ ለዔሳው ፈድፋደ እምያዕቆብ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>19:30</sup>&nbsp;The two of them departed together from Abraham. <sup>19:31</sup>&nbsp;Rebecca loved Jacob with her entire heart and her entire being very much more than Esau; but Isaac loved Esau much more than Jacob.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>20:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበአርብዓ ወክልኤቱ ኢዮቤልዉ በዓመት ቀዳሚ ዘሱባዔ ሳብዕ ጸውዐ አብርሃም ይስማዔልሃ ወዐሠርተ ወክልኤተ ደቂቆ ወይስሐቅሃ ወክልኤሆሙ ደቂቆ ወስድስተ ደቂቀ ኬጡራ ወውሉዶሙ <sup>20:2</sup>&nbsp;ወአዘዞሙ ከመ ይዕቀቡ ፍኖተ እግዚአብሔር ከመ ይግበሩ ጽድቀ ወያፍቅር አሐዱ አሐዱ ቢጾ ወከመ ይኩኑ ከማሁ በውስተ ኵሉ ፀብእ ከመ ይሖሩ ዲበ አሐዱ ላዕሌሆሙ ወለገቢረ ፍትሕ ወጽድቅ በዲበ ምድር <sup>20:3</sup>&nbsp;ከመ ይክስቡ ውሉዶሙ በኪዳን እንተ ተካየደ ምስሌሆሙ ወከመ ኢይትዐደዉ የማነ ወፀጋመ እምኵሎን ፍናዌ ዘአዘዘነ እግዚአብሔር ወከመ ንትዐቀብ እምኵሉ ዝሙት ወርኵስ ወከመ ንኅድግ እማእከሌነ ኵሎ ርኵሰ ወዝሙተ። <sup>20:4</sup>&nbsp;ወእመ ዘመወት ለክሙ ኵላ ብእሲት ወእመኒ ወለት አውዕይዋ በእሳት ወኢይዘምዋ ድኅረ አዕይንቲሆን ወልቦንሂ ከመ ይንሥኡ ሎሙ ብእሲተ እምነ አዋልደ ከናአን እስመ ይሤሮ ዘርአ ከናአን እምድር። <sup>20:5</sup>&nbsp;ወነገሮሙ ኵነኔሆሙ ለረዐይት ወኵነኔ ሰዶም ከመ ተኰነኑ በእንተ እከዮሙ በእንተ ዝሙት ወርኵስ ወሙስና በበይናቲሆሙ በዝሙት ሞቱ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>20:1</sup>&nbsp;During the forty-second jubilee, in the first year of the seventh week [2052], Abraham summoned Ishmael and his twelve children, Isaac and his two children, and the six children of Keturah and their sons. <sup>20:2</sup>&nbsp;He ordered them to keep the way of the Lord so that they would do what is right and that they should love one another; that they should be like this in every war so that they could go against each one (who was) against them; and do what is just and right on the earth; <sup>20:3</sup>&nbsp;that they should circumcise their sons in the covenant which he had made with them; that they should not deviate to the right or left from all the ways which the Lord commanded us; that we should keep ourselves from all sexual impurity and uncleanness; and that we should dismiss all uncleanness and sexual impurity from among us. <sup>20:4</sup>&nbsp;If any woman or girl among you commits a sexual offence, burn her in fire; they are not to commit sexual offences (by) following their eyes and their hearts so that they take wives for themselves from the Canaanite women, because the descendants of Canaan will be uprooted from the earth. <sup>20:5</sup>&nbsp;He told them about the punishment of the giants and the punishment of Sodom — how they were condemned because of their wickedness; because of the sexual impurity, uncleanness, and corruption among themselves they died in (their) sexual impurity.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>20:6</sup>&nbsp;ወአንትሙኒ ተዐቀቡ እምኵሉ ዝሙት ወርኵስ ወእምኵሉ ግማኔ ኀጢአት ከመ ኢተሀቡ ስመነ ለመርገም ወኵሎ ሕይወተክሙ ለትምክሕት ወኵሎ ውሉደክሙ ለሙስና በሰይፍ ወትከውኑ ርጉማነ ከመ ሰዶም ወኵሉ ተረፍክሙ ከመ ውሉደ ገሞራ። <sup>20:7</sup>&nbsp;አነ አሰምዕ ለክሙ ውሉድየ አፍቅርዎ ለአምላከ ሰማይ ወተፀመዱ ኵሎ ትእዛዞ ወኢትሖሩ ድኅረ ጣዖቶሙ ወድኅረ ርኵሶሙ። <sup>20:8</sup>&nbsp;ወአማልክተ ስብኮ ኢትግበሩ ለክሙ ወግልፈዋተ እስመ ከንቱ ውእቱ። ወኢምንተኒ መንፈስ አልቦሙ እስመ ግብረ እደው እሙንቱ ወኵሎሙ እለ ይትዌከሉ ቦሙ ወኢበምንትኒ ኵሎሙ ተወከሉ ኢታምልክዎሙ ወኢትስግዱ ሎሙ <sup>20:9</sup>&nbsp;አላ አምልኩ አምላከ ልዑለ ወስግዱ ሎቱ ወትረ ወተሰፈዉ ገጸ ዚአሁ በኵሉ ጊዜ ወግብሩ ጽድቀ ወርትዐ በቅድሜሁ ከመ ይፍተው ላዕሌክሙ ወየሀብክሙ ምሕረቶ ወያውርድ ለክሙ ዝናመ ነግህ ወሰርክ። ወይባርክ ኵሎ ተግባረክሙ ኵሎ ዘተገበርክሙ በዲበ ምድር ወይባርክ እክለከ ወማየከ ወይባርክ ዘርአ ከርሥከ ወዘርአ ምድርከ ወመራዕየ አልህምቲከ። ወመራዕየ አባግዒከ <sup>20:10</sup>&nbsp;ወትከውን ለበረከት በዲበ ምድር ወይፈትዉክሙ ኵሎሙ አሕዛበ ምድር። ወይባርኩ ውሉድክሙ በስምየ ከመ ይኩኑ ቡሩካነ በከመ አነ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>20:6</sup>&nbsp;'Now you keep yourselves from all sexual impurity and uncleanness and from all the contamination of sin so that you do not make our name into a curse, your entire lives into a (reason for) hissing and all your children into something that is destroyed by the sword. Then you will be accursed like Sodom, and all who remain of you like the people of Gomorrah. <sup>20:7</sup>&nbsp;I testify to you my sons: love the God of heaven and hold fast to all his commandments. Do not follow their idols and their uncleanness. <sup>20:8</sup>&nbsp;Do not make for yourselves gods that are molten images or statues because they are something empty and have no spirit in them. For they are made by hands, and all who trust in them all trust in nothing at all. Do not worship them or bow to them. <sup>20:9</sup>&nbsp;Rather, worship the most high God and bow to him continually. Look expectantly for his presence at all times, and do what is right and just before him so that he may be delighted with you, give you his favor, and make the rain to fall for you morning and evening; bless everything that you do — all that you have done on the earth; bless your food and water; and bless the products of your loins, the products of your land, the herds of your cattle, and the flocks of your sheep. <sup>20:10</sup>&nbsp;You will become a blessing on the earth, and all the nations of the earth will be delighted with you. They will bless your sons in my name so that they may be blessed as I am'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>20:11</sup>&nbsp;ወወሀቦ ለይስማዔል ወለውሉዱ ወለውሉደ ኬጡራ ሀብተ ወፈነዎሙ እምይስሐቅ ወልዱ ወኵሎ ወሀቦ ለይስሐቅ ወልዱ <sup>20:12</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረ ይስማዔል ወውሉዱ ወውሉደ ኬጡራ ወውሉዶሙ ኅቡረ ወኀደሩ እምፋርሞን እስከ ምብዋአ ባቢሎን ውስተ ኵሉ ምድር እንተ ገጸ ጽባሕ አንጻረ ገዳም። <sup>20:13</sup>&nbsp;ወተደመሩ እሉ ምስለ እሉ ወተጸውዐ ስሞሙ ዐረብ ወእስማዔላዊያን።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>20:11</sup>&nbsp;When he had given gifts to Ishmael, his sons, and Keturah's sons and sent them away from his son Isaac, he gave everything to his son Isaac. <sup>20:12</sup>&nbsp;Ishmael, his sons, Keturah's sons, and their sons went together and settled from Paran as far as the entrance of Babylon — in all the land toward the east opposite the desert, <sup>20:13</sup>&nbsp;They mixed with one another and were called Arabs and Ishmaelites.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>21:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበሳድስ ዓመት ዘሳብዕ ሱባዔ ዘዝንቱ ኢዮቤልዉ ጸውዐ አብርሃም ይስሐቅሃ ወልዶ ወአዘዞ እንዘ ይብል አነ ረሳእኩ ወኢያአምር ዕለተ ሞትየ እስመ ጸገብኩ መዋዕልየ። <sup>21:2</sup>&nbsp;ወናሁ አነ ወልደ ምእት ወሰብዓ ወኀምስቱ ዓመት ወበኵሉ መዋዕለ ሕይወትየ ሀሎኩ እንዘ እዜከሮ ለእግዚአብሔር ወእንዘ አኀሥሥ በኵሉ ልብየ ከመ እግበር ፈቃዳቲሁ ወከመ አርትዕ ሐዊረ በኵሉ ፍናዊሁ <sup>21:3</sup>&nbsp;ጣዖተ ጸልአት ነፍስየ ከመ እትዓቀብ ለገቢረ ፈቃዱ ለዘ ፈጠረኒ <sup>21:4</sup>&nbsp;እስመ አምላክ ሕያው ውእቱ ወቅዱስ ውእቱ ወምእመን ወጻድቅ ውእቱ እምኵሉ ወአልቦ በኀቤሁ ነሢአ ገጽ ወነሢአ ሕልያን እስመ አምላክ ጻድቅ ውስቱ ወገባሬ ኵነኔ ውእቱ እምኵሎሙ እለ ይትዐደዉ ትእዛዞ ወለእለ ይሜንኑ ኪዳኖ። <sup>21:5</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተኒ ወልድየ ዕቀብ ትእዛዞ ወሥርዓቶ ወኵነኔሁ ወኢትሖር ድኅሬሆሙ ለርኩሳን ወድኅሬሆሙ ለግልፎ ወድኅሬሆሙ ለስብኮ <sup>21:6</sup>&nbsp;ወኢትብላዕ ምንተኒ ደመ ዘአርዌ ወእንስሳ ወዘኵሉ ዖፍ ዘይሰርር ውስተ ሰማይ <sup>21:7</sup>&nbsp;ወለእመ ኀረድከ ኅርድ ለጽንሐሐ ሰላም ዘይሰጠው ኅርድዎ ወደሞሙ ትክዕዉ ውስተ ምሥዋዕ ወኵሎ ስብሐ ጽንሐሕ ታዐርግ ውስተ ምሥዋዕ ምስለ ስንዳሌ ወመሥዋዕተ ልዉስ በቅብእ ምስለ ሞጻሕቱ ታዐርጎ ኵሎ ኅቡረ ዲበ ምሥዋዕ ጽንሐሐ መዓዛ ሠናይ ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር <sup>21:8</sup>&nbsp;በከመ ስብሐ መሥዋዕተ መድኃኒት ታነብር ዲበ እሳት ዘዲበ መሥዋዕት በከመ ስብሕ ዘዲበ ከርሥ ወኵሎ ስብሐ ዘዲበ ንዋየ ውስጥ ወክልኤ ኵልያተ ወኵሎ ስብሐ ዘዲቤሆሙ ወዘዲበ መናቅዕ ወከብድ ምስለ ኵልያት ጥብሉለ <sup>21:9</sup>&nbsp;ወታዐርግ ዘንተ ኵሎ ለመዓዛ ሠናይ ዘይሰጠው ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር ምስለ መሥዋዕቱ ወምስለ ሞጻሕቱ ከመዓዛ ሠናይ ኅብስተ ጽንሐሕ ለእግዚአብሔር። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>21:1</sup>&nbsp;In the sixth year of the seventh week of this jubilee [2057] Abraham summoned his son Isaac and gave him orders as follows: 'I have grown old but do not know when I will die because I have reached the full number of my days. <sup>21:2</sup>&nbsp;Now I am 175 years of age. Throughout my entire lifetime I have continually remembered the Lord and tried to do his will wholeheartedly and to walk a straight course in all his ways. <sup>21:3</sup>&nbsp;I have personally hated idols in order to keep myself for doing the will of the one who created me. <sup>21:4</sup>&nbsp;For he is the living God. He is more holy, faithful, and just than anyone. With him there is no favoritism nor does he accept bribes because he is a just God and one who exercises judgment against all who transgress his commands and despise his covenant. <sup>21:5</sup>&nbsp;Now you, my son, keep his commands, ordinances, and verdicts. Do not pursue unclean things, statues, or molten images. <sup>21:6</sup>&nbsp;Do not eat any blood of an animal, cattle, or of any bird that flies in the sky. <sup>21:7</sup>&nbsp;If you slaughter a victim for a peace offering that is acceptable, slaughter it and pour their blood onto the altar. All the fat of the sacrifice you will offer on the altar with the finest flour; and the offering kneaded with oil, with its libation — you will offer it all together on the altar as a sacrifice. (It is) an aroma that is pleasing before the Lord. <sup>21:8</sup>&nbsp;As you place the fat of the peace offering on the fire which is on the altar, so also remove the fat which is on the stomach and all the fat which is on the internal organs and the two kidneys and all the fat which is on them and which is on the upper thighs and liver with the kidneys. <sup>21:9</sup>&nbsp;All of this you will offer as a pleasant fragrance which is acceptable before the Lord, with its sacrifice and its libation as a pleasant fragrance — the food of the offering to the Lord.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>21:10</sup>&nbsp;ወሥጋሁ ብላዕ በይእቲ ዕለት ወበሳኒታ ወኢይዕረብ ላዕሌሁ ፀሐይ ዘአመ ሳኒታ እስከ ሶበ ይትበላዕ ወኢይትርፍ ለዕለት ሣልስት እስመ ኢይሠጠዎ እስመ ኢኮነ ኅሩየ ወኢይትበሀል እንከ። ወኵሎሙ እለ ይበልዕዎ ኀጢአተ ሎሙ ይነሥኡ እስመ ከመዝ ረከብኩ ጽሑፈ ውስተ መጽሐፈ አበዊየ ቀደምት ውስተ ነገረ ኤኖክ ወውስተ ነገረ ኖኅ። <sup>21:11</sup>&nbsp;ውስተ ኵሉ ምሥዋዓቲከ ትደይ ፄወ ወኢይጸራዕ ኪዳነ ፄው ውስተ ኵሉ ምስዋዓቲከ ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>21:10</sup>&nbsp;Eat its meat during that day and on the next day; but the sun is not to set on it on the next day until it is eaten. It is not to be left over for the third day because it is not acceptable to him. For it was not pleasing and is not therefore commanded. All who eat it will bring guilt on themselves because this is the way I found (it) written in the book of my ancestors, in the words of Enoch and the words of Noah. <sup>21:11</sup>&nbsp;On all your offerings you are to place salt; let the covenant of salt not come to an end on any of your sacrifices before the Lord.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>21:12</sup>&nbsp;ወተዐቀብ በዕፀወ መሥዋዕት ከመ ኢታብእ ዕፀወ ዲበ ምሥዋዕ ዘንተ ክመ ቄጳርሶን ወዴፍራን ወሶጋድ ወሰጠሮቢሎን ወጲጢን ወቄድሮን ወቡራቲ ወታናክ ወዕፀ ዘይት ምርስኔ ወድፍን ወቄዳር ዘስሙ አርባት ወቤስም <sup>21:13</sup>&nbsp;ወእምእሉ ዕፀው አንብር መትሕተ ጽንሐሕ ዲበ ምሥዋዕ ምኩረ ርእዮሙ ወኢታንብር ኵሎ ዕፀ ንቁዐ ወሬዋ ዕፀወ ጽኑዓነ ወጽኑዐ ዘአልቦ ምንተኒ ነውረ ፍጹመ ወሐደስተ ተክለ ወኢታንብር ዕፀ ብሉየ እስመ ወፅአ መዓዛሁ እስመ እንከ አልቦ መዓዛ ላዕሌሁ ከመ ቀዳማዊ <sup>21:14</sup>&nbsp;ዘእንበለ እሉ ዕፀው አልቦ ዘታነብር ባዕደ። እስመ መዓዛሁ ፍሎጥ ወየዐርግ ጼና መዓዛሁ ወስተ ሰማይ። <sup>21:15</sup>&nbsp;ዑቅ ዛትእዛዘ ወግበራ ወልድየ ከመ ታርትዕ በኵሉ ግብርከ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>21:12</sup>&nbsp;Be careful about the (kinds of) woods (that are used for) sacrifice so that you bring no (kinds of) woods onto the altar except these only: cypress, silver-fir, almond, fir, pine, cedar, juniper, date, olive wood, myrtle, laurel wood, the cedar whose name is the juniper bush, and balsam. <sup>21:13</sup>&nbsp;Of these (kinds of) woods place beneath the sacrifice on the altar ones that have been tested for their appearance. Do not place (beneath it) any split or dark wood; (place there) strong (kinds of) woods and firm ones without any defect — a perfect and new growth. Do not place (there) old wood, for its aroma has left — because there is no longer an aroma upon it as at first. <sup>21:14</sup>&nbsp;Apart from these (kinds of) woods there is no other which you are to place (beneath the sacrifice) because their aroma is distinctive and the smell of their aroma goes up to heaven. <sup>21:15</sup>&nbsp;Pay attention to this commandment and do it, my son, so that you may behave properly in all your actions.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>21:16</sup>&nbsp;ወበኵሉ ጊዜ ኩን ንጹሐ በሥጋከ ወኅዕብ በማይ ዘእንበለ ትሖር ለአዕርጎ ውስተ ምሥዋዕ ወኅፅብ እዴከ ወእግረከ ዘእንበለ ትቅረብ ውስተ መሥዋዕት ሶበ ፈጸምከ አዕርጎ ግባእ ወተኀፀብ እደዊከ ወእገሪከ <sup>21:17</sup>&nbsp;ወኢያስተርኢ በዲቤክሙ ኵሉ ደም ወውስተ አልባሲክሙ ተዐቀብ ወልድየ በደም ተዐቀብ ጥቀ ድፍኖ ምድረ <sup>21:18</sup>&nbsp;ወኢትብልዑ እንከ ደመ እስመ ደም ነፍስ ይእቲ ወኢትብላዕ ምንተኒ ደመ። <sup>21:19</sup>&nbsp;ወኢትንሣእ ሕልያነ ዲበ ኵሉ ደመ ሰብእ ከመ ኢይትከዐው በከ ዘእንበለ ኵነኔ እስመ ደም ውእቱ ዘይትከዐው ያኀጥኣ ለምድር ወደም ኢትክል ነጺሐ እምደመ ሰብእ ዘእንበለ በደመ ዘከዐዎ። <sup>21:20</sup>&nbsp;ወኢትንሣእ ሕልያነ ወአምኃ በደመ ሰብእ ደመ በደም ወይሠጠው ቅድመ አምላክ ልዑል። ወይከውን ዑቃቤሁ ለሠናይ ወከመ ትትዐቀብ እምኵሉ እኩይ ወከመ ያድኅንከ እምኵሉ ሞት። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>21:16</sup>&nbsp;At all times be clean with respect to your body. Wash with water before you go to make an offering on the altar. Wash your hands and feet before you approach the altar [or: sacrifice]. When you have finished making an offering, wash your hands and feet again. <sup>21:17</sup>&nbsp;No blood is to be visible on you or on your clothing. My son, be careful with blood; be very careful to cover it with dirt. <sup>21:18</sup>&nbsp;You are not, therefore, to consume any blood because the blood is the vital force. Do not consume any blood. <sup>21:19</sup>&nbsp;Do not take a bribe for any human blood so that it may not be shed casually — without punishment — because it is the blood that is shed which makes the earth sin. The earth will not be able to become pure from human blood except through the blood of the one who shed it. <sup>21:20</sup>&nbsp;Do not take a bribe or gift for human blood; blood for blood — then it will be acceptable before the most high God. He will be the protection of the good; and (he will be this) so that you may be kept from every evil one and that he may save you from every (kind of) death. 
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>21:21</sup>&nbsp;እሬኢ አነ ወልድየ ኵሎ ግብረ እጓለ እመሕያው ከመ ኃጢአት ወእከይ ወኵሉ ግብሮሙ ርኵስ ወምናኔ ወግማኔ። ወአልቦ ጽድቀ ምስሌሆሙ <sup>21:22</sup>&nbsp;ተዐቀብ ኢትሖር ውስተ ፍኖቶሙ ወለከይደ አሰሮሙ ወኢትስሐት ስሕተተ ለሞት ቅድመ አምላክ ልዑል። ወየኀብእ ገጾ እምኔከ ወያገብአከ ውስተ እደ አበሳከ ወይሤርወከ እምነ ምድር ወዘርአከኒ እምታሕተ ሰማይ ወይትሐጐል ስምከ ወዘርእከ እምኵሉ ምድር። <sup>21:23</sup>&nbsp;ረገሐሥ እምኵሉ ምግባሪሆሙ ወእምኵሉ ርኵሶሙ ወተዐቀብ ዑቃቤ ዘአምላክ ልዑል ወግበር ፈቃዳቲሁ ወታረትዕ በኵሉ። <sup>21:24</sup>&nbsp;ወይባርከከ በኵሉ ምግባሪከ ወያነሥእ እምኔከ ተክለ ጽድቅ በኵሉ ምድር በኵሉ ትውልደ ምድር ወኢይትረመም ስምየ ወስምከ በመትሕተ ሰማይ በኵሉ መዋዕል 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>21:21</sup>&nbsp;I see, my son, that all the actions of mankind (consist of) sin and wickedness and all their deeds of impurity, worthlessness, and contamination. With them there is nothing that is right. <sup>21:22</sup>&nbsp;Be careful not to walk in their ways or to tread in their paths so that you may not commit a mortal sin before the most high God. Then he will hide his face from you and will hand you over to the power of your offenses. He will uproot you from the earth and your descendants from beneath heaven. Your name and descendants will be destroyed from the entire earth. <sup>21:23</sup>&nbsp;Depart from all their actions and from all their impurity. Keep the obligations of the most high God and do his will. Then you will act properly in every regard. <sup>21:24</sup>&nbsp;He will bless you in all your actions. He will raise from you a righteous plant in all the earth throughout all the history of the earth. Then my name and your name will not be passed over in silence beneath heaven throughout all time.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>21:25</sup>&nbsp;ሖር ወልድየ በሰላም ያጽንዕከ አምላክ ልዑል አምላኪየ ወአምላክከ ለገቢረ ፈቃዳቲሁ ወይባርክ ኵሎ ዘርእከ ተርፈ ዘርእከ ለትውልድ ዘለዓለም በኵሉ በረከተ ጽድቅ ከመ ትኩን በረከተ በኵሉ ምድር። <sup>21:26</sup>&nbsp;ወወፅአ እምኀቤሁ እንዘ ይትፌሣሕ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>21:25</sup>&nbsp;Go in peace, my son. May the most high God — my God and your God — strengthen you to do his will. May he bless all your descendants — the remnant of your descendants — throughout the history of eternity with every proper blessing so that you may become a blessing throughout the entire earth'. <sup>21:26</sup>&nbsp;Then he left him feeling happy.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>22:1</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ በሱባዔ ቀዳሚ በዘ አርብዓ ወአርባዕ ኢዮቤልዉ በካልእ ዓመት በዘ ሞተ አብርሃም መጽኡ ይስሐቅ ወይስማዔል እምዐዘቅተ መሐላ ከመ ይግበሩ በዓለ ሱባዔያት ዛቲ በዓል ዘቀዳሚ ማእረር ኀበ አብርሃም አቡሆሙ ወተፈሥሐ አብርሃም እስመ ክልኤሆሙ ደቂቁ መጽኡ <sup>22:2</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ብዙኅ ጥሪቱ ለይስሐቅ በቤርሳቤ ወየሐውር ይስሐቅ ወይዋሒ ጥሪቶ ወይገብእ ኀበ አቡሁ <sup>22:3</sup>&nbsp;ወበዝ መዋዕል መጽአ ይስማዔል ይርአይ አባሁ ወመጽኡ ኵሎሙ ኅቡረ ወጠብሐ ይስሐቅ መሥዋዕተ ለጽንሐሕ ወአዕረገ ዲበ ምሥዋዐ አቡሁ ዘገብረ በኬብሮን። <sup>22:4</sup>&nbsp;ወሦዐ መድኃኒተ ወገብረ ግዝአ ግሥሓ በቅድመ ይስማዔል እኁሁ። ወገብረት ርብቃ ዳፍንተ ሐዳሰ እምስርናይ ሐዲስ ወወሀበቶ ለያዕቆብ ወልዳ ከመ ያብእ ለአብርሃም አቡሁ እምቀዳሚ ፍሬ ምድር ከመ ይብላዕ ወይባርክ ፈጣሬ ኵሉ እንበለ ይሙት። <sup>22:5</sup>&nbsp;ወይስሐቅኒ ውእቱ ፈነወ በእደ ያዕቆብ ዘይሤኒ መሥዋዕተ ዘመድኃኒት አብርሃም ይብላዕ ወይስተይ። <sup>22:6</sup>&nbsp;ወበልዐ ወሰትየ ወባረኮ ለአምላክ ልዑል ዘፈጠረ ሰማየ ወምድረ ዘገብረ ኵሎ ስብሐ ምድር ወወሀቦሙ ለውሉደ ሰብእ ይብልዑ ወይስተዩ ወይባርኩ ፈጣሪሆሙ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>22:1</sup>&nbsp;In the first week in the forty-fourth jubilee, during the second year [2109] — it is the year in which Abraham died — Isaac and Ishmael came from the well of the oath to their father Abraham to celebrate the festival of weeks (this is the festival of the firstfruits of the harvest). Abraham was happy that his two sons had come. <sup>22:2</sup>&nbsp;For Isaac's possessions in Beersheba were numerous. Isaac used to go and inspect his possessions and then return to his father. <sup>22:3</sup>&nbsp;At that time Ishmael came to see his father, and all of them came together. Isaac slaughtered a sacrifice for the off'ering; he offered (it) on his father's altar which he had made in Hebron. <sup>22:4</sup>&nbsp;He sacrificed a peace offering and prepared a joyful feast in front of his brother Ishmael. Rebecca made fresh bread out of new wheat. She gave it to her son Jacob to bring to his father Abraham some of the firstfruits of the land so that he would eat (it) and bless the Creator of everything before he died. <sup>22:5</sup>&nbsp;Isaac, too, sent through Jacob [his] excellent peace offering [and wine to his father] Abraham for him to eat and drinic. <sup>22:6</sup>&nbsp;He ate and drank. Then he blessed the most high God who created the heavens and the earth, who made all the fat things of the earth, and gave them to mankind to eat, drink, and bless their Creator.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>22:7</sup>&nbsp;ወይእዜኒ እትጋነይ ለከ አምላኪየ እስመ አርአይከኒ ዛተ ዕለተ ናሁ አነ ወልደ ምእት ወሰብዓ ወኃምስ ክረምት ልሂቅ ወፍጹመ መዋዕል ወኵሎን መዋዕልየ ኮናኒ ሰላመ <sup>22:8</sup>&nbsp;ሰይፈ ጸላኢ ኢሞአኒ። ወበኵሉ ዘወሀብከኒ ወለውሉድየ ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወትየ እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት <sup>22:9</sup>&nbsp;ትኩን ሣልስከ ወሰላምከ ላዕለ ገብርከ ወላዕለ ዘርአ ውሉዱ ከመ ይኩንከ ሕዝበ ኅሩየ ወርስተ እምኵሉ አሕዛበ ምድር እምይእዜ ወእስከ ኵሉ መዋዕል ዘትውልደ ምድር ለኵሉ ዓለማት። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>22:7</sup>&nbsp;'Now I offer humble thanks to you, my God, because you have shown me this day. I am now 175 years of age, old and with (my) time completed. All of my days have proved to be peace for me. <sup>22:8</sup>&nbsp;The enemy's sword has not subdued me in anything at all which you have given me and my sons during all my lifetime until today. <sup>22:9</sup>&nbsp;May your kindness and peace rest on your servant and on the descendants of his sons so that they, of all the nations of the earth, may become your chosen people and heritage from now until all the time of the earth's history throughout all ages'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>22:10</sup>&nbsp;ወጸውዖ ለያዕቆብ ወይቤሎ ወልድየ ያዕቆብ ይባርክ አምላከ ኵሉ ወያኀይልከ ለገቢረ ጽድቅ ወፈቃዱ በቅድመ ዚአሁ ወይኅረይ ብከ ወበዘርእከ ከመ ትኩንዎ ሕዝበ ለርስቱ በከመ ፈቃዱ በኵሉ መዋዕል። ወአንተኒ ወልድየ ያዕቆብ ቅረብ ወሰዐመኒ <sup>22:11</sup>&nbsp;ወቀርበ ወሰዐሞ። ወይቤ ቡሩክ ወልድየ ያዕቆብ ወኵሎሙ ውሉዱ ለእግዚአብሔር ልዑል ለኵሉ ዓለማት። የሀብከ እግዚአብሔር ዘርአ ጽድቅ ወእምውሉድከ ይቀድስ በማእከለ ኵላ ምድር ይትቀነዩ ለከ አሕዛብ ወይስግዱ በቅድመ ዘርእከ ኵሎሙ አሕዛብ። <sup>22:12</sup>&nbsp;ኩን ኀያለ በቅድመ ሰብእ ወእንዘ ትሜብል ውስተ ኵሉ ዘርአ ሴት አሜሃ ይጸድቃ ፍናዊከ ወፍናወ ውሉድከ ለከዊነ ሕዝብ ቅዱስ <sup>22:13</sup>&nbsp;የሀብከ አምላክ ልዑል ኵሎን በረከታተ እለ ባረከኒ ወእለ ባረኮ ለኖኅ ወአዳምሃ ያዕርፍ ዲበ ድማኀ ቅዳሴ ዘርእከ ለኵሉ ትውልደ ትውልድ ወእስከ ለዓለም። <sup>22:14</sup>&nbsp;ወያንጽሕከ እምኵሉ ርስሐተ ርኵስ ከመ ታስተስሪ እምኵሉ አበሳ ዘበ ኢያእምሮ ጌጋይከ። ወያኀይልከ ወይባርከ ወትረስ ኵላ ምድረ <sup>22:15</sup>&nbsp;ወየሐድስ ኪዳኖ መስሌከ ከመ ትኩኖ ሕዝበ ለርስቱ በኵሉ ዓለማት። ወውእቱ ይኩንከ ለከ ወለዘርእከ አምላከ ዘበህልው ወዘበጽድቅ በኵሉ መዋዕለ ምድር 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>22:10</sup>&nbsp;He summoned Jacob and said to him: 'My son Jacob, may the God of all bless and strengthen you to do before him what is right and what he wants. May he choose you and your descendants to be his people for his heritage in accord with his will throughout all time. Now you, my son Jacob, come close and kiss me'. <sup>22:11</sup>&nbsp;So he came close and kissed him. Then he said: 'May my son Jacob and all his sons be blessed to the most high Lord throughout all ages. May the Lord give you righteous descendants, and may he sanctify some of your sons within the entire earth. May the nations serve you, and may all the nations bow before your descendants. <sup>22:12</sup>&nbsp;Be strong before people and continue to exercise power among all of Seth's descendants. Then your ways and the ways of your sons will be proper so that they may be a holy people. <sup>22:13</sup>&nbsp;May the most high God give you all the blessings with which he blessed me and with which he blessed Noah and Adam. May they come to rest on the sacred head of your descendants throughout each and every generation and forever. <sup>22:14</sup>&nbsp;May he purify you from all filthy pollution so that you may be pardoned for all the guilt of your sins of ignorance. May he strengthen and bless you; may you possess the entire earth. <sup>22:15</sup>&nbsp;May he renew his covenant with you so that you may be for him the people of his heritage throughout all ages. May he truly and rightly be God for you and your descendants throughout all the time of the earth.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>22:16</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተኒ ወልድየ ያዕቆብ ተዘከር ቃልየ ወዕቀብ ትእዛዛተ አብርሃም አቡከ። ተፈለጥ እምአሕዛብ ወኢትብላዕ ምስሌሆሙ ወኢትግበር በከመ ምግባሪሆሙ ወኢትኩኖሙ ቢጸ እስመ ግብሮሙ ርኵስ ወኵሉ ፍናዊሆሙ ግሙን ወምናኔ ወሰቆራር። <sup>22:17</sup>&nbsp;መሥዋዕቶሙ ለአብድንት ይዘብሑ ወለአጋንንት ይሰግዱ። ወበውስተ መቃብራት ይበልዑ ወኵሉ ግብሮሙ ከንቱ ወበክ <sup>22:18</sup>&nbsp;ወአልቦሙ ልበ ለኀልዮ ወኢኮነ አዕይንቲሆሙ ዘይሬኢ። ምንተ ግብሮሙ ወእፎ እሙንቱ ይስሕቱ እንዘ ይብሉ ለዕፅ አንተ አምላኪየ ወለእብን አንተ እግዚእየ ወአንተ መባልሕየ ወኢሀሎ ልብ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>22:16</sup>&nbsp;Now you, my son Jacob, remember what I say and keep the commandments of your father Abraham.
Separate from the nations,
and do not eat with them.
Do not act as they do,
and do not become their companion,
for their actions are something that is impure,
and all their ways are defiled and something abominable and detestable.
<sup>22:17</sup>&nbsp;They offer their sacrifices to the dead,
and they worship demons.
They eat in tombs,
and everything they do is empty and worthless.
<sup>22:18</sup>&nbsp;They have no mind to think,
and their eyes do not see what they do
and how they err in saying to (a piece of) wood:
«You are my god»;
or to a stone:
«You are my Lord;
you are my deliverer». 
(They have) no mind.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="ethiopic" lang="gez">
<sup>22:19</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተኒ ወልድየ ያዕቆብ አምላክ ልዑል ይርዳእከ ወአምላከ ሰማይ ይባርከ ወያግኅሥከ እምነ ርኵሶሙ ወእምኵሉ ስሕተቶሙ <sup>22:20</sup>&nbsp;ተዐቀብ ወልድየ ያዕቆብ ከመ ኢትንሣእ ብእሲተ እምነ ኵሉ ዘርአ አዋልደ ከናአን። እስመ ኵሉ ዘርኡ ለሥራዌ እምድር <sup>22:21</sup>&nbsp;እስመ በአበሳ ካም ስሕተ ከናአን ወኵሉ ዘርኡ ይደምሰስ እምድር ወኵሉ ተርፉ ወዘይድኅን አልቦ እምኔሁ አመ ዕለተ ደይን <sup>22:22</sup>&nbsp;ወለኵሎሙ እለ ያመልኩ ጣዖተ ወለጽሉኣን አልቦሙ ምንተኒ ተስፋ በምድረ ሕያዋን እስመ ውስተ ሲኦል ይወርዱ ወውስተ መካነ ደይን የሐውሩ። ወአልቦሙ ምንተኒ ዝክረ በዲበ ምድር። ከመ ተንሥኡ ውሉደ ሰዶም እምድር ከማሁ ይትንሥኡ ኵሎሙ እለ ያመልኩ ጣዖተ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="english" lang="en">
<sup>22:19</sup>&nbsp;As for you, my son Jacob, may the most high God help you and the God of heaven bless you.
